Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words 2  
Compiled by the Committee on Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words  

Foreword                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon Jo  

Table of Contents  
Foreword …………………………………………………… 3  
1) Jesus' View on Life for Restoration  
Matthew 6:16-34  
<Prayer> Father! We thank You for protecting us over the past year. Now, as we celebrate the first Sunday of the new year, we come before You with joyful hearts to worship. We reflect on our past shortcomings and, from this moment on, we wish to become sanctified bodies and minds as You desire, humbly worshiping You. Loving Father, please accept us. If there are any thoughts or claims in our hearts that are unworthy before You, please remove them. If our bodies have been defiled by evil, please burn it away with the fire of the Holy Spirit, forgive us with the grace of compassion, and sanctify us to become sons and daughters who can receive the joy of Your love. Father, we earnestly hope and wish that from this day forth, the gift of holiness may connect us and allow the power to subdue evil Satans to manifest through us. May our hearts and bodies move to inspire all creation in heaven and earth, and guide us to bring joy to our Father in heaven. We sincerely hope and wish that our gathering may be the true gathering that You desire. Now, we dedicate all our sincerity to reveal the love hidden within You. It has come time to manifest the view of life for restoration through Jesus, and it has come time to reveal Your providence of 6,000 years. Father! Please allow Your sons and daughters gathered here to stand in a sanctified position, receive Your sanctified power, and become children who can feel the heart of Moses, who parted the Red Sea with the staff You gave him. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Father, in this year, please bestow Your blessings upon the thirty million people of this nation, and may Your glory and love rest upon the many denominations gathering for this nation. Please reveal Your promised will to Your hidden sons and daughters so that soon the Korean Peninsula may become a mountain of victory. Thus, may this sleeping nation return the glory of joy to You and be guided to resonate the will of restoration upon this earth. We earnestly hope and wish for this. Please allow us to possess the sincere hearts of the hidden saints, move the many denominations to awaken the thirty million people, and mobilize this nation to awaken the 2.4 billion humanity so that we may quickly realize the original garden. Loving Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Father, at this time, please sanctify our bodies and minds with the new promise and new law established today, and grant us the grace of Your joy. Please allow the promise and response to be established here, and from this time forth, may Your protective hand be with us so that we may be offered as a victorious sacrifice before You. Please allow us to be sons and daughters of loyalty who can dedicate our bodies, minds, and everything for the purpose that pleases You, Father. We earnestly hope and wish for this. On this day, there are groups scattered in the regions holding onto Your words and taking on lonely altars, so please sanctify them from Satan, and establish Your tangible power before the forces of darkness so that they may become proud children who manifest the glorious dignity of You, our beloved Father. We earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Also, in every gathering place, please allow Your sons and daughters to receive the power of Your authority and protect them from Satan's invasion. Father! At this time, may the Triune God operate and allow the resurrection of joy and glory to manifest, and from the beginning to the end, may Your Holy Spirit fill our bodies and hearts. We earnestly ask this, and we pray all these words in Your name. Amen.  
<Words> I would like to speak to you for a moment on the topic of "Jesus' View on Life for Restoration."  
The fallen humanity has not yet found the eternal value of life that the world, the earth, and heaven can testify to. Therefore, fallen humanity has the mission of restoration to find the value of individual life, to find the value of life on a global scale through individuals, and to find the eternal value of life that transcends the world.  
Then, where will the purpose of God’s providence, which has been established until today, conclude? It will not conclude in your individual selves or in the world. We must find the value of life that can make heaven and earth one, where God can be joyful, and at the same time, the world can be joyful, and the individual can be joyful. Only then will the providence of salvation in heaven come to an end, the global morality centered on Satan will end, and the individual moral concepts will also come to an end. You must understand that fallen humanity has the responsibility to pioneer this path of life.  
You may easily see yourselves as individual beings, but you must recognize that the entire ideal of creation is contained within you. Therefore, you must first manifest the value of life on a global scale.  
Only after that will your individual value of life be established. You all know that living to find such value of life is precisely what faith is about. Therefore, you must analyze yourselves and possess eternal life instead of the life that your nature demands, and unify all historical ideals into one to complete the global life. You must also establish a foundation of life that can relate eternal life or global life to your individual life. Otherwise, your current life cannot become eternal life through global life.  
The human ancestors Adam and Eve lost this universal life due to their fall, and God has worked hard for 6,000 years to restore it. This historical effort of God is called the providential history of restoration.  
To establish this universal value of life, God sent one person who could represent the entire value of life after going through 4,000 years of effort; that person was Jesus Christ. Jesus Christ, as one body, represented the eternal and infinite global life and the eternal individual life. Because Jesus came with this historical background, He had to manifest eternal hope based on reality and testify to the value of life that could eternally exist on heaven and earth.  
Then, what standard did Jesus Christ, who came with this mission, live by? Jesus did not live for His individual life but for the life of the world, and furthermore, He fought every day for eternal life. This was the standard of Jesus' life.  
In other words, the vision that Jesus had and the feelings He experienced, and the life He lived were not only for Himself. They were personal, yet they represented the world, and at the same time, they represented God. Furthermore, the gospel that Jesus preached was not only for Himself but was a message for the world and, beyond that, an eternal message of life representing God.  
Those Christians who do not realize this cannot understand the true content of the gospel of Jesus Christ and cannot fulfill the purpose for which Jesus Christ came. You must understand this.  
The Standard of Love Established by Jesus  
Then, what did Jesus put forth to realize this universal value of life? Jesus put forth love. In other words, to complete the universal value of life on heaven and earth, He preached a new gospel, the center of which was love.  
The most important thing for an individual to connect their life to eternal value is, as Jesus said, the love that can sacrifice one's life for others. In reality, Jesus established the standard of life value not for Himself but by loving others more than Himself.  
Thus, Jesus, who represented the value of the entire universal life, taught that to save oneself, one must possess the love that can sacrifice one's life for others. You must clearly understand that Jesus Christ is the one who stepped forward with love for others, for the world, and even for God and the countless saints in the spirit world.  
Jesus did not live with an individualistic concept to find the value of His individual life or with individual love. Even when Jesus loved a friend, He did not love merely within that friendship. Behind it, He had the concept of loving on behalf of the world and loving on behalf of God.  
Thus, Jesus' love was not a one-to-one relationship. Even if Jesus loved an individual, it contained God's love, universal love, and personal love. You must become those who experience this. Only then can you correctly understand the value of Jesus' life.  
So, to what extent did Jesus set the standard for His life? He set the standard of existing for the world. Even when Jesus sacrificed Himself to love a friend, He held the concept of loving for the world behind it.  
The reason Jesus could establish the standard of love for global salvation on the cross was that He had the heart of sacrifice and love that could die for individuals while also dying for the whole. You must understand that Jesus Christ was the protagonist of love, life, and character.  
Not only that, but Jesus also prayed to heaven, saying, “My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as You will.” (Matthew 26:39) Because Jesus wanted to live only according to the will of the Father beyond the peak of death, He could introduce God's love to humanity. We must understand that there is amazing love contained in the journey of Jesus.  
And what did Jesus Christ, who came with the mission to restore universal life, put forth to find the value of life? It was also love. And that love was not for individual humans but was for the world, for God, and even for the spirits in the eternal world.  
Now, as we who must bear the life of total restoration, we must not approach everything with just the feelings we experience at that moment in our daily lives. We must face everything with the determination and resolution to represent the character of Jesus Christ, who stood for the universal whole.  
Only by going through such daily lives can we complete the global life and establish a relationship with eternal life. In other words, if the value of your daily life only pertains to yourself, it cannot establish a relationship with eternity. That is why you must live a life that relates to the eternal love of God. Only then will the eternal God be with you.  
And you must realize that because Jesus Christ lived every day in relationship with God throughout His life, although He died, the will of God that He sought to fulfill through Jesus continues to unfold.  
The Center of the Life of True Saints  
So, what must we do today to establish this relationship? In believing in Jesus and moving forward, the concept that must be established at our center is that, like Jesus, we were born not only for individuals but also for the world and for heaven.  
You must clearly understand that only by living a life of love and service for others can you establish an eternal relationship with God. If we have a heart of gratitude for Jesus today, we must not consider that gratitude as merely our own. We must establish that gratitude as a gratitude for all humanity.  
If there is such a person, they will bear a global mission and, furthermore, will be able to take responsibility for God's overall mission. If we live with this center of life, we will not be discouraged. No matter what difficulties arise or what hardships we encounter, we will be able to overcome them sufficiently.  
That is why, in the scripture we just read, Jesus said, “Do not worry about anything.” In other words, do not worry about what to eat, what to wear...
14 Jesus said not to worry about the life of His return. This statement does not mean to deny the whole, but rather to become a person who worries about solving global problems before resolving personal issues in order to find and establish the value of the whole that represents God's will. Furthermore, for those who live with such determination, personal suffering is not a problem. So how should we, who must fulfill God's will, live? Our daily lives should not be solely about solving our own internal and external problems. We must take responsibility to go beyond our own issues and connect with the overall problems to realize eternal values. Only then can you fulfill the meaning of the heavenly gospel. Additionally, when you embark on the path of evangelism with such a sense of mission, God will be with you. If you live with a heart of love and care for others, there will surely be a work of love's recreation taking place. You must clearly understand this. Until now, we have lived our faith too self-centeredly. We have worked and loved for ourselves. From now on, you must not do this. Even when you ask for love from heaven, you must demand love for all humanity, and you must also seek love that can care for the countless spirits in the spiritual world. The history that has come down to find eternal life for humanity is the providential path, and the history of humanity that remains to find global life is the historical path, while the path of daily life is for finding life for one day. When viewed in terms of human values, seeking global life is humanity, while seeking personal life is the concept of morality. You must understand that all issues from the world to the individual are interconnected within yourself. Furthermore, to possess the value of life that the Father can guarantee eternally, you must learn the life perspective of Jesus Christ centered on love. So what was the life perspective of Jesus Christ? His life perspective was to govern daily life with a heart of care centered on love and the cosmic owner's heart. This was the central content of the life perspective that Jesus Christ established to restore cosmic life. Therefore, even when you encounter trivial problems in your daily life, you must approach them with the mindset that you are responsible for the overall movement of life’s restoration entrusted to you by God. You must also feel that Jesus Christ stepped forward as a practitioner of love for restoration. We, who must inherit Jesus' mission and fulfill His will, must live for others. Only then can you connect with the overall life and achieve the value of life that the eternal God can testify to. Jesus came with the mission to restore cosmic life, so He went through personal service, personal sacrifice, and personal suffering. And in taking on this responsibility, He did not just seek to be responsible for His time but lived with the determination to take responsibility for the life of all humanity until the overall mission of restoration is complete. In other words, Jesus has been carrying the mission of restoring cosmic life even to this day, 2000 years later. However, since Jesus could not complete that mission by Himself, He sent the Holy Spirit to work and mobilized countless spirits in the spiritual world to complete that mission. You must understand that Jesus Christ came to restore the value of cosmic life, but because He could not complete that work, the mission to fulfill it still remains. That is why Jesus is still laboring on this earth to carry out that mission. However, this responsibility cannot be completed by Jesus alone. So through whom should that mission be completed? God wants to complete that mission through you. In other words, because Jesus could not fulfill the mission of restoring cosmic life, we must take responsibility for that mission.
16 You must fulfill the life perspective of Jesus for restoration. And if you feel the responsibility to conclude that mission in your lifetime, you must have a firm determination to achieve that mission throughout your life. Now, you must experience that Jesus Christ is working in the providential historical process to establish the value of cosmic life in your daily life. Otherwise, you must understand that the will of Christ, who has labored as the messenger of the restoration of cosmic life until now, will not be fulfilled through you. Now, you must first know how to establish yourself as a condition of oath before heaven. Jesus also established a condition of oath just once for the world, for heaven and earth, or for the people, and that was the cross. Through this cross, Jesus transcended the standard that countless prophets and sages had worked hard for with their lives. Therefore, you must have a clear idea that in order to realize the value of cosmic life, you will become a sacrificial offering of oath before heaven, the world, or individuals at some point in the future. Wherever you go, whatever situation you find yourself in, you must always strive to stand as a condition of oath in the environment you are in at that time. This is what faith life is. Now, you have the mission to establish the value of cosmic life before the Father, so you must live in a way that connects your life with Jesus' life as a condition of oath. You must also have the determination to establish yourself as a global condition. Furthermore, you must have the determination to become a sacrificial offering of oath on behalf of the countless prophets who have worked hard until now and on behalf of Jesus Christ. In this way, as each of you creates such conditions of oath, you can move from one to two, four, and eventually to the world. You must understand that when such an environment is created, the global suffering to find the value of life will come to an end. In other words, if the foundation that can end the global suffering to find life is not formed within each of you and does not expand to the church, society, nation, and world, then God's providential will to establish Jesus Christ and restore cosmic life will not be concluded. You must clearly realize this. However, when you think about yourselves who have come this far regarding this providential will, or when you think about today's Christians, you will find that there has not been a standard established that represents the value of cosmic life, connecting individuals and families to society, nations, and the world. The whole, that is, all of humanity, must enter into that realm, but it has not been able to do so. If such a standard is not established on this earth, the mission of restoring cosmic life through Jesus Christ will not be concluded. The purpose of life that the saints of the last days must have is to recognize that while the true individual, Jesus Christ, has been established, it has not yet expanded to families, society, nations, and the world. The sorrow of Jesus Christ has remained as cosmic sorrow, and it has also remained as God's sorrow, as the sorrow of the universe. Thus, until now, humanity has been longing for the day when such sorrow will be resolved and eternal victory in heaven will be achieved. You must have the determination to testify to the value of the entire providence of heaven and earth through your own life and to express the love of the whole of heaven and earth. However, the value of life you desire and the value of cosmic life that God desires to fulfill the entire providence are different. Therefore, you must cultivate the mindset that you can live a global and cosmic life even in your personal life while going through the path of life that is based on the heavenly principles of hope. If such a mindset is cultivated, even if you cannot fully practice that will, you can continue to relate to the whole on the inner side. That is why Jesus said, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." What does this mean? Jesus, who came as the embodiment of cosmic love and truth, said this because the values given by God to each individual must be completed and become their foundation for the kingdom of heaven to be realized. When individuals belonging to the kingdom of heaven gather and unite to initiate a global movement of life, and when they can connect with the countless spirits in the spiritual world, only then will the purpose of Jesus Christ, who came to restore cosmic life on this earth, be concluded through such people. When the people of that time faced Jesus, who came with the mission of restoring cosmic life, from a position that could not even dare to think of such a mission, Jesus rebuked them, saying they should not hope for eating, drinking, and clothing more than the kingdom of God and righteousness, nor should they take those as standards of life. If there is someone who lives in a mindset of being able to live on behalf of God, on behalf of Jesus Christ, and to fight on behalf of the world, that person is not alone. For that person, God will be with them to the end of the world, Jesus will be with them, and the Holy Spirit will be with them. However, because the people of that time did not know this relationship and lived with a mindset that only served themselves, Jesus rebuked them. So what is the purpose of your belief in Jesus in the last days? It is not to receive any external blessings from the world. It is not for personal comfort or to live well as an individual. Our well-being is for Jesus and God. However, when this purpose changes, it may seem that everything is going well, but as time goes on, rather than achieving it, things become blocked. On the other hand, if humans live for Jesus, for God, and for the world, Jesus has said that God will take responsibility for everything. However, for you, who have the responsibility to fulfill God's will, the question is how much you can sacrifice for God's will. If you sacrifice for the individual, you will become a personal protagonist; if you sacrifice for the world, you will become a global protagonist; and if you sacrifice for heaven and earth and establish a victorious standard of life, you will become the protagonist who can govern heaven and earth. Therefore, Jesus has been working behind the scenes until now, so that people can resemble His character and establish values of life. The effort you make to find your own individual life and to initiate this movement of restoration is incredibly important from the historical perspective of humanity, from the current global perspective, and from the eternal hopeful perspective of the future. At the same time, your responsibility is immeasurably great. The standard of all your daily lives must be to restore the overall life on behalf of Christ, and you must be those who take on the responsibility to practice the value of life that God seeks, centered on the love that Jesus Christ established. Only when you become such people will God's will to restore cosmic life be completed through you. The place where such people gather is heaven, and the more such individuals there are, the more God will be with them and the more He will rejoice. <Prayer> We feel in our hearts the labor of the Father who has established the laws of the heavenly principles to connect the life of restoration cosmically. Father! Please guide us to realize that You have labored for 6,000 years to establish the value of global life. We have come to understand that it is a heavenly law that religion that does not relate to Christ from the individual to the whole cannot be intervened by God, so now allow us to live the life that Jesus Christ desires, and let us know the value of Jesus Christ's love, dear Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. We have come to know that we must also have the determination that Jesus Christ had regarding life, so please be with us to overcome and win against Satan's attacks in the battlefield where we can find the value of our individual lives. We understand that there are accusations from Satan as we take on the path of restoring the values of life left by Jesus Christ, so please guide us not to become those who are accused by Satan in the path that extends from our individual lives to the life of the world and the universe. Allow us to boldly block Satan's accusations in our daily lives and to have the determination to block them historically, so that we can fulfill that life and responsibility, dear Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Now, in order to achieve a global life that possesses the value of eternal life, we must resemble the perfect character of Jesus, who governed all things on earth, so dear Father of love, please guide us to resemble that character of Christ. Also, we are in a position where we must walk the path of battle practically, regardless of who it is, so Father, in our social lives and in the personal aspects we present before You, or in the love we must give to humanity, please lead us not to be accused by Satan. May we be able to realize the love of Christ, who earnestly hoped for the fulfillment of the eternal love of the Father. May we possess the values of life established by Christ and may You govern us so that we can realize those values on this earth, dear Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Only when we take on the responsibility for this can we connect from the individual to the world and to heaven and earth, so please allow us to feel this at this time. Lead us to become sons and daughters who can fight by overcoming all external conditions and taking on the overall standard of life and the values of life as our conditions of oath. We earnestly ask and wish that You govern everything according to Your will and take care of these matters, praying in the name of the Lord. Amen. *  
2) Jesus, looking back as He walks the final path.
Luke 22:54-62

<Prayer> Father, the sons and daughters who have been fighting centered on Your will for a week, who have been struggling not to be deceived by Satan's cunning schemes, are now bowing down before You. Please personally manifest Yourself and govern each of their bodies and minds. Is there anyone here who harbors deep-seated resentment in their heart? Is there anyone who bears the traces of Satan in their body? My loving Father, show them the work of recreation, extend Your hand of compassion, and let them become those who can worship You with hearts and bodies that are not lacking before Your desired will. At this time, we earnestly hope and wish that You will grant us Your grace and sanctify us. Beloved Father! We bow our heads before Your will, which seeks to announce the cosmic providence by calling us, who are insignificant. At this time, please command our hearts, stir our bodies, and lead us to run towards the garden of good will, towards the will of goodness, and towards the garden of victory that You desire. Also, please raise us up so that we can strive towards Your will, and grant us the conscious strength and determination to step forward. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. We are still those who have elements of sin that are unworthy before You. 

February 10, 1957, Sunday, Headquarters Church.

As Jesus walks the final path and looks back, O Father! With the majestic power of Your work, please remove the elements of our sins, and with Your mighty hand, touch us and awaken our hearts of repentance, we earnestly hope for this, Father. This day is a holy day, a day promised for blessings, so please bless the countless altars gathered for the nation and lead us to raise the torch of victory. Bless the countless sons and daughters who are worshiping at this time to receive Your glory and comfort, and grant us the work of the Holy Spirit, we earnestly hope and wish for this, beloved Father. Father, we have gathered to confess everything before You, so please guide us to analyze whether we are worthy before You once again. If there are still any shortcomings that are unworthy before You, please allow us to repent of everything and confess everything so that we can receive Your counsel and advice. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. At this time when the path of battle still remains, please allow us to become heavenly soldiers who can unite our hearts and rush towards the garden of life. We know that lonely sons and daughters are building altars of labor to testify to the words of the Gospel in various regions. Wherever they gather, may You personally work and testify that they are victorious sons and daughters, and lead them to build altars of victory where You can personally operate and work. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. 

Please allow the sons and daughters present here not to have any notions or claims centered on themselves. With a childlike heart, allow them to lay down everything and, by the words given, to repent of their shortcomings before You and become sons and daughters who can be held by Your hand of recreation at this time. We have entrusted everything before You, so please do not allow this time to be one where Satan intrudes, and raise us up through the work of sanctification so that You can personally govern, and let this time be one where only Your glory is revealed. We earnestly hope and wish for this, and we pray all these words in Your name. Amen.

<Word> Today, I will speak for a moment on the title "Jesus Looking Back as He Walks the Final Path." 

The coming of Jesus and the disbelief of the Jewish people caused Adam and Eve to lose the eternal ideal garden that God had permitted due to their fall. In other words, Adam and Eve lost the garden of goodness where they could share life with God. As a result, they left the embrace of God and began a sorrowful life where they had to long for God. Thus, humanity, having left the loving embrace of God, has walked a history of suffering for 6,000 years, looking back at God with sorrowful hearts. Just as our ancestors walked the path of life looking towards heaven, all of humanity today is also going through a life journey looking towards heaven in hopes of restoring their original position. And Jesus, who came to save humanity, was also looking for people on earth who could look towards heaven. He sent Jesus Christ as a condition of heavenly love so that people of the world could turn back and hold onto Jesus Christ through the new Gospel. However, at that time, not only humans but also countless people until now have not been able to properly welcome such protagonists who could lead them to look towards heaven and achieve the purpose of life. Therefore, all of you today are inevitably faced with a destiny that requires you to look towards heaven. However, since humanity cannot turn towards heaven by their own strength, God sent Jesus Christ to enable those who could not return to find their way back. If humanity had looked in the direction He was looking and walked as He walked, they would have been able to fulfill their desire to return to God's embrace. This is the central purpose for which God sent Jesus Christ, and you must understand this clearly.

As Jesus walked the final path, not only the Jews but also the entire humanity of Israel should have held onto Jesus and completed the purpose of life by looking towards heaven to return to God's embrace. However, due to disbelief, Jesus and humanity became divided. Therefore, you must remember that Jesus stopped His steps and was in a position to look back towards the earth. However, among humanity, there have been no saints who have turned towards heaven and devoted their hearts and strength to heaven throughout the long history of 6,000 years. Furthermore, there has not been a single person who has offered their life, love, and actions to stop Jesus Christ, who is walking the path of suffering on behalf of humanity. This is the deep resentment of God. Humanity, who should have broken away from the world and moved towards heaven, became fixated on the earth, and due to their disbelief in Jesus, God's providence over the earth for 4,000 years was frustrated. God sent Jesus Christ to fulfill the desires of the people on earth, but because they could not look towards Jesus, God had to again take a position to look back at the earth after a long history of 2,000 years. Jesus and the Holy Spirit also had to take a position to look back at the earth. 

So what was the desire that Jesus had for over 30 years? His desire was simply to serve others. Even though He bore the sorrow and grief felt by Adam and Eve when they were cast out of the Garden of Eden, He did not express it and lived solely for the sake of others. If the people of that time had recognized Jesus as the protagonist who could restore all their wishes and turned towards Him, He would not have gone to the cross. As the ignorant people betrayed Him, Jesus was forced to stop His steps, which were meant to lead humanity towards God. 

You must remember that Jesus, who could not complete the mission entrusted to Him from heaven, had to stand again looking towards heaven and walk the path back to God's embrace as the representative of humanity. Therefore, if humanity had devoted their hearts and sincerity to God and Jesus, and had walked in the direction Jesus was walking, Jesus could have treated humanity as God treats humanity, and furthermore, they could have established an altar of joy on this earth to welcome a glorious day. However, because the people of that time did not follow the steps towards heaven, Jesus became divided from humanity. 

Since God bears the responsibility of the creative principle, He sought to establish a victorious day where humanity could turn back towards God through Jesus. However, Jesus, who came to the earth, was rejected by the Israelite people and was led to the cross, which means that the providential purpose for which God sent Jesus was frustrated. 

The Heart of Jesus Looking Back at Peter 

When Jesus was walking the lonely path of the cross, who did He look back at? He looked back at Peter, the representative of His beloved twelve apostles. This was because He was worried that Peter's heart, which should have followed Him first, might change. Thus, even though His heart was filled with anguish over God's will, Jesus looked back at Peter with love. You must become those who can feel that gaze of Jesus today. However, Peter denied knowing Jesus three times. As a result, he stood in a position completely separated from heaven's will and became disconnected from Jesus. 

Even though Jesus knew this, He was looking for even one person among humanity who could protect His steps towards death, who could sympathize with Him in heart and body. This is why He looked back at His beloved disciple Peter. You must understand that the desire to find a true person was embedded in that gaze towards Peter. For Jesus, who was responsible for the overall providence of God, there could be no sadder scene than this. This is because there was no one who could understand His painful heart as He sought even one person to inherit His mission of walking the path of Golgotha, the path of death. Therefore, Jesus was filled with indescribable sorrow. Only God understood Jesus' painful heart and was concerned for His sorrowful situation. 

When Jesus reflected on the laborious path He had walked for over 30 years on behalf of heaven's sorrow, He felt a desire to rebuke humanity and curse the earth. Yet, He suppressed that feeling and looked at Peter, who was following Him. If you cannot feel Jesus' inner feelings today, you must understand that you cannot stand before all humanity with the mission of God's will centered on Jesus. 

What must have been Peter's heart as he looked at Jesus, who was finishing His life in lonely suffering? He must have been in a position of deep sorrow, unable to forget the bond of love he had with Jesus in the past, groaning in loneliness. He must have felt great pain seeing Jesus, who was insulted and blamed, being dragged away despite being innocent. However, because Peter did not realize that Jesus was the Messiah who came with the representative mission to turn all humanity back, he could not step forward on behalf of the disciples and remained in a position of self-interest. 

When the servant girls questioned Peter whether he was one of Christ's followers, he denied it three times. You must clearly understand that Peter's individual stance represented all humanity on earth. 

When we reflect again on the positions of Jesus and Peter, we see that Jesus looking back at Peter, who denied Him three times, was not just a matter between them but was indicative of the entire historical process. In the journey of all humanity towards heaven, there will inevitably be three accusations from Satan against those who step forward as true Christians representing Christ's will. This can be seen as symbolizing the positions of Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent throughout the 6,000 years of history. This is also manifested in the form of global World Wars I, II, and III at the end of days. Such events appear not only throughout the historical process but also in your individual faith journeys today. 

The Awareness of Peter 

So what will happen to you just before you meet the Lord today? Just as Peter had a moment of betrayal when he said, "I do not know Him," there may also come a time for us today as we face the end. We have a historical, providential, and faith-based destiny that requires us to rise above the position of external Peter and follow the victorious Jesus. We must understand what position we should take and what responsibilities we must fulfill as we cross the peak of this destiny. 

Furthermore, just as Jesus walked the path of Golgotha before His resurrection on the cross, all Christians in the end times must walk the final path of Golgotha to participate in the glory of resurrection with the Lord at the time of the Second Advent. You must remember that such a time will surely come. 

So what position should we take in our faith life today? Just as Peter could not openly say, "I know Him," when his beloved teacher was being led away by the Roman soldiers without any sin, there was a moment when he felt sorrow inside but could not express it outwardly.
28   As Jesus looked back while walking the final path, there may be times today when we, due to some worldly condition, find ourselves in a position where we have to say we do not ‘know’ Jesus. At that time, we must be able to say we ‘know’ Him. We must also be vigilant in our faith life, reflecting on ourselves in such situations. Jesus, who walked the path of Golgotha on earth, has continued to walk the global Golgotha path in the spirit world until today. In this way, with beloved saints behind Him in both the physical and spiritual realms, Jesus, who personally walked the path of the cross and suffering, will engage in a major confrontation with Satan in the future. When the time of such a confrontation appears on earth, what position should we take? We must not stand in the same position as Peter, who denied knowing Jesus. We must stand in Jesus' position, confessing all our circumstances, all our sins, and all our shortcomings, reflecting on ourselves, and becoming victorious sons and daughters who can uphold the path of labor that Jesus walked. If we cannot stand in that position, we will not be able to partake in the glorious position of welcoming the Lord upon His return. Although Peter denied knowing his Master three times while in a difficult position, Jesus truly turned His body and looked at Peter. Thus, forgetting His own difficulties, sorrows, and circumstances, when Peter saw Jesus looking back at him, a great transformation occurred in Peter's heart. Even though Peter had denied Jesus three times, when he saw that Jesus, forgetting His own sorrow, was genuinely concerned for him and worried about his path, Peter's emotions erupted. Moreover, feeling the old bond of sharing joys and sorrows with the Lord, Peter momentarily realized his true identity. As Jesus Christ, determined to fulfill the will of Heaven, walked the path of death toward Heaven without being overwhelmed by human sorrow, striving to pave the way for human salvation while also caring for even the inadequate Peter, Peter felt a sense of inadequacy in his heart. In other words, reflecting on the position of Jesus representing God and comparing it to his own position, Peter felt the vast difference between his faith in Jesus and Jesus' faith in God. He realized that although he claimed to believe in Jesus, he did not believe with the same heavenly-centered faith as the Lord, but rather with a self-centered faith. At that moment, he was so shocked by the gaze of Jesus looking at him that he did not know where to put himself. In other words, he lamented over his self of disbelief.

29   The value of Peter's repentance and new resolution. At the moment Peter looked at Jesus, who was unwaveringly pushing forward with a cosmic mission to fulfill the eternal and unchanging purpose of Heaven, his heart was transformed, and he felt a strong impulse to live for the Lord for the rest of his life. When he became aware of his self of disbelief, Peter increasingly felt the inadequacy of himself by comparing the relationship between himself and Jesus or their respective life journeys. As he observed Jesus, who did not seek his own happiness but offered everything as a sacrifice before Heaven for the sake of all people on earth, and who, while being led to the cross, did not complain, the three disciples realized how self-centered their own lives had been. Thus, before the selfless Jesus Christ, the disciples reflected on themselves and vowed to carry out the will that Jesus always desired on this earth. Then, what did Peter feel next? He felt his own disbelief while simultaneously sensing the disbelief around him. Seeing the wicked people around him rejoicing as they bound and whipped the sinless Jesus Christ, whom anyone would declare innocent, Peter was able to penetrate the sorrowful and lonely heart of Jesus through the gaze of Jesus, who was being persecuted. In such an unjust position, witnessing Jesus maintaining the heavenly path, Peter felt the insincerity of the surrounding environment. There, as Jesus walked the final path and looked back, Peter resolved to fight against the insincere forces around him until the Lord returned to eliminate the wicked. The good and unchanging appearance of Jesus heading toward Heaven and the insincerity of the surrounding environment were worlds apart. Thus, through the momentary gaze of Jesus Christ looking back, Peter was able to settle his foolish life and resolved to purify the surrounding environment and establish a standard of goodness.

30   Through the death of Jesus Christ, who returned without a word for Heaven, for the earth, for all humanity, and for the purpose, Peter naturally came to respect the Lord and wept bitterly in repentance before that death. This realization made Peter feel that there was an apostle who recognized him in the moment when Jesus Christ looked back for the last time, and it was a moment when the severed connection between Heaven and humanity was restored. Peter alone, representing Heaven and earth, all humanity, and countless apostles, shed tears of repentance over his inadequacies before Jesus, who died for the will of God. In this way, only Peter wept and lamented as he witnessed the suffering of the Lord before His crucifixion. Because of such events, a standard was established through which Jesus could work centered on the apostles, creating a new basis for humans to connect with Jesus. Just as Christians have clung to the will of God and awaited the time of resurrection and return since the crucifixion of Jesus, you too must go through such a position. And you must restore the position of Peter. If this is the final fate left in your faith journey, you must seriously reflect on the relationship between yourself and Jesus, and you should be able to emulate Jesus' resolve and bow down in repentance before His posture. The question is how much we have lived with concern for the Lord, just as He has cared for us in our faith life thus far. While one may claim to have lived a life concerned for Jesus, how can that compare to the life of Jesus, who looked at Peter while traversing the path of death? Now, according to the principle of restoration, just as Jesus looked back at the crowd while walking the path of death, we too must become those who can look back at Jesus Christ while on the path of death. In that position, while standing in the place of Jesus, we must also look back to honor Him and share in His suffering and concerns. The question is whether you have had such a moment. If you have not had such a moment, when the end comes, you will not be able to hold the resurrected Lord and say, ‘My Lord’ and ‘My Bride’ as Mary Magdalene did when she held the resurrected Jesus Christ. Jesus looked back at Peter on the cross, and while Peter and the three disciples were found, there are no saints who have directly held onto Jesus and gone to Heaven.

31   The responsibility of saints to look back at Jesus. Now, as you stand at the end, to become true saints who can dwell with Jesus and allow Him to operate, you must be able to genuinely care for Jesus and fight against Satan just as Jesus looked back at Peter while walking the path of death. If you cannot do this, you must understand that you cannot hold the glorious Lord and worship God. Although we are living a life of faith, we have not lived a life of concern for Jesus through our daily lives. Therefore, even though Jesus has come to us hundreds and thousands of times, He must have turned away with sorrowful eyes because of our unbelieving lives, merely looking at us. There have been many times when Jesus came to us and looked at us with sorrowful eyes, but we did not understand His circumstances and heart, and we have lived a comfortable life of faith, only seeking our own will. 

32   As Peter compared his life with the life of Jesus in the gaze of Jesus, he reproached his own disbelief and felt that he had lived too self-centeredly. Likewise, you should compare your own life with the 30 years of Jesus' life and the historical life of Jesus, who has worked for God for the past 2,000 years. You cannot help but feel that you have lived centered on yourself, just as Peter did. If you do not escape from this mark of disbelief, you must understand that you will have no way to meet the returning Jesus. So, to what position must you go? You must be able to perceive the heart of Jesus in the gaze He continuously gives you, and you must be able to go beyond the hill of the cross to the place of resurrection grace, not just to the summit of Golgotha before the suffering of the cross. To do this, like Peter, you must repent of having a faith concept centered on yourself. Just as Jesus did not live centered on Himself but lived centered on God's will, you must not have the idea that you believe to gain salvation or for your own well-being; you must live for God's will. Peter, who came out with the faith concept for his own well-being, denied Jesus three times without realizing it. Today, if you have a self-centered faith concept, you must be mindful that at any time, at any moment, and in any period, you may unknowingly reject Heaven. In other words, you must live a faith life that believes in Jesus, not a faith life that believes in yourself; a faith life that seeks Jesus, not a faith life that seeks yourself; a faith life that serves Jesus, not a faith life that serves yourself. When Peter lived a faith life seeking himself, he faced unspeakable suffering that blocked him and ultimately severed his relationship with Jesus. You must avoid such a position. You must change from a faith life centered on yourself to a faith life that serves Jesus and God. Furthermore, just as Peter restored the environment of disbelief to an environment of faith and mourned over his disbelief, you must also go out with an unutterable sense of indignation and animosity upon seeing the disbelief that God does not desire. Thus, you must walk the path of goodness that God desires. And goodness must not be centered on yourself but must be centered on God, and that goodness must relate to you. Only when you find this goodness can you, like Peter, mourn for the environment where God's will is not fulfilled and feel sorrow for humanity and Heaven.

33   Now, today you have the responsibility to build the final victory before the Father, before Jesus, or before the Holy Spirit. You must be those who can follow Jesus along the path of Golgotha without betraying Him. And you should not be those who worry about yourselves but rather forget your own pain and follow Jesus, being able to say, ‘Teacher!’ In other words, you should not be those who receive the gaze of Jesus' concern but rather enter into Jesus' position and become those who can comfort Him with a heart of concern. Who has done this? Only Jesus has continued to labor for humanity, hoping for the day when this will be accomplished. Now, you must not become the object of Jesus' concern in your life, nor should you become those who rebel against the will of Jesus, who has placed all hope in you, and against God's providence. Just as Peter lamented over his disbelief after denying Jesus, you must lament your disbelief and be ready to step forward, prepared to die, through the heart of Jesus, who has taken on the painful circumstances of representing God's will. Thus, you must set out with the determination that you will walk the path that Jesus walked, and only by crossing Golgotha can you welcome the resurrected Jesus as your Bride and give joy and glory to Heaven.

34   The prayer of Jesus looking back while walking the final path. The mission to traverse the sorrowful path of Golgotha with a cosmic heart, blocking the historical course of humanity and building the foundation of heavenly victory remains for the 2.4 billion people of humanity today. O loving Father, may we be granted the understanding that Your concern in sending Jesus and worrying for Him was not only fulfilled on the ancient Golgotha but is also deeply felt in our presence today. While we should certainly be able to weep over our current inadequacies, we earnestly hope and wish to be sons and daughters who can weep over the fruits that Jesus desires. We must become those who weep over our own imperfections while also being able to shed tears and repent upon seeing the disbelief that God does not desire, as the wicked world shouts against Jesus and mocks Him. Just as Jesus devoted Himself as a sacrificial offering until the moment He returned, feeling the gaze of God upon Him to complete the path of restoration, may we also not forget the gaze and footsteps of Jesus when He comes to find us one day. Furthermore, let us realize how many times we have rejected that gaze and those footsteps of Jesus. Father! Even if we betray You not once but twice or three times, may we repent of how much we have comforted the heart of Jesus, who has come to find us without change, and how many tears we have shed before Heaven. O Father, Your lonely sons and daughters, the time of global judgment is not far off, and the cosmic Golgotha garden is approaching before us. Therefore, guide us not to walk a faith journey centered on ourselves. Our lives are not ours, nor is the life we live ours, nor are the hopes we desire ours. Please guide us not to live for ourselves, and allow us not to possess our abilities, our needs, and our desires for ourselves.
35 Dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. Even if we go out on the path of the cross instead of Jesus, may we finally come to know Jesus's unwavering faith, and like Peter who sighed in his heart and shed tears upon seeing Jesus carrying the cross as a fellow believer in God, may we be able to shed tears of repentance before Jesus before the judgment day of Golgotha. May we be led to be sons and daughters who can take on the cosmic repentance and cry out before You, expressing our own wrongdoings, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. Father! As we walk in place of Jesus's footsteps, please entrust us with the mission to save the poor people of this land, and allow us to walk the remaining path of Golgotha. Thus, may we break down the Satan throughout the world and establish the foundation of victory's glory, so that we may be able to welcome the resurrected Jesus in our lifetime. Dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. Please allow us to surely fulfill Your will at the end of days. May we be led to escape the self of disbelief and leave the world of disbelief as eternal believers, and may we be sons and daughters who can rest eternally with You, stand on the side of heaven, and command billions of Satans with Your love, I earnestly hope and wish, and I pray in Your name. Amen. *

3) Let us become the people Jesus desires
John 11:1-20 <Prayer> Father who has lost the garden of love and the garden of goodness! As we have gone through a long history, please allow the sons and daughters gathered here today to feel Your situation of not being able to find that one will You have established, and the true human beings You desire. Please work at this time so that we can stand as beings who are not lacking in being embraced in the bosom of Your love, in place of Your eternal providence. We are in a position where we cannot help but ask You for everything from one, so Father, please lead us with a hand of compassion. Also, the power and nature of sin inherited from our ancestors are closing the doors of our hearts, so please manifest the gifts of power and open the doors of our dark hearts, and lead us to run towards goodness. Dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. There are various difficulties blocking the sons and daughters who wish to move towards Your heavenly will, so Father, please grant us strength, hold us with Your powerful hand, and allow us to win by entrusting us with the entire battle You fought. Thus, may we be sons and daughters who can highly praise Your will before billions of Satans, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. At this time, may we who have come before Your knees reflect on what we have to offer before You. If there is no offering that You can joyfully receive, please allow this hour to be one where we can repent and receive Your grace of compassion, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. We have come to know that the mission entrusted to us by heaven is not just for our individual selves, but a mission that must resolve the grievances of nations and humanity and tens of millions of saints. We must fulfill such a heavenly purpose, so please accept the bodies and hearts of Your sons and daughters who are prostrated here as offerings, and accomplish that one cosmic will You desire, and establish us as beings who are not lacking at all in fulfilling that will, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. If there are children who still possess elements that cannot be accepted before Your will, Your grace, and Your loving bosom, please, with the workings of power and the words of re-creation, lead them to shed tears of repentance for not understanding Your heart, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. We thank You for entrusting us with the heavenly mission to fight on behalf of thirty million nations. The sons and daughters gathered here, looking towards Your will, have a cosmic responsibility to raise the banner of battle and go towards heaven, so Father, please grant them Your power. May they be led to run towards the eternal and unchanging path through the workings of Your inspiration and Your direct movement in their lives, so that they can testify that they are the sons and daughters who are with You before all multitudes after winning against billions of Satans, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. This day is a holy day, a day promised and established to bless us, so may the sons and daughters gathered here today be embraced in the deep and high love of the Father and be granted the grace to live a heavenly life, I earnestly hope and wish. 

38 Let us become the people Jesus desires
In every place where lonely family members are working hard to convey the words allowed, Father, please manifest the promised will. Thus, may it be evidenced that we are the living sons and daughters of the Father, and allow a direct work to awaken and raise the multitudes in the realm of darkness, dear loving Father, I earnestly hope and wish. Now, we who are prostrated before You, if there have been any claims or actions that are not worthy before You, please allow us to lay them all down and have hearts that can humbly worship to be cleared by Your dignified grace. At this time, may Satan not find a gap, Father, please oversee us, and lead us to be able to offer thanks and worship before Your grace that has led us to overcome suffering and achieve victory, dear Father, I earnestly hope and wish. I earnestly ask that only Your will and love be with us during this hour, and I pray all these words in Your name. Amen. <Word> Today, I would like to think together with you for a short time on the title "Let us become the people Jesus desires." 

The purpose of Jesus's coming
You all know well that Jesus Christ, who appeared on this earth carrying the heavenly will hidden in the heart of God, came to find the true sons and daughters who would stand on the mountain of victory, having trampled over the sinful history committed by our ancestors. So, when Jesus appeared before the humans on this earth, what kind of heart did He have? He appeared with the heart that humanity had towards God before the fall. Everything Jesus saw, heard, felt, and thought was not a feeling that Satan could enjoy within the realm of fallenness, but rather represented the heavenly nature, and He established the standard of life while proclaiming the new gospel, embodying the entire will that God required of humanity. 

39 You must understand that the eyes Jesus looked through, the ears He listened with, the mouth He spoke with, the nose that smelled, and all the limbs that felt were fundamentally different from those of humans on earth who feel for their own desires. They were established solely as a condition of victory that transcended the world of sin, aligned with God's heart, suitable before God's will, and could be practiced as words that God could enjoy, allowing all people to follow His example. So what kind of person does Jesus desire? In other words, what kind of person is Jesus looking for? If there is no one who understands the criteria of the person Jesus desires and restores that standard, not only will the will Jesus desires not be fulfilled on this earth, but God's will will also not be fulfilled. You must be clear about this. The will that God demands through Jesus Christ is for all people to become one with Jesus as a condition of global victory, based on Jesus Himself as the model. In other words, God desired that all people would follow Jesus and become people who could enjoy being with Him, and Jesus desired this as well. Thus, Jesus appeared on this earth with the mission to restore all humanity, and the words He spoke or the emotions and sensations He felt in His body were fundamentally different from the words we use today or the emotions and sensations we feel. 

So what should we, who have Jesus as our Lord today, do? First, we must understand the heart of responsibility that Jesus had to fulfill the heavenly will and complete the work of salvation for the universe. We must advance to the standard of feeling, experiencing, and thinking that Jesus had, so that we can stand in a relative position to directly face Jesus. If you cannot become such people, Jesus will become a pitiful figure. God created Adam and Eve with all His might, intending to feel joy through them, but because they fell, God's heart was filled with sorrow. Who came to resolve this sorrow? It was Jesus. However, when Jesus came to this earth, 

40 what was He trying to do? He sought to establish a true person who could appear before God as one who does not bear the fallen nature and does not receive accusations from the enemy Satan. The Jewish religion, which had been prepared for 4,000 years, should have presented a true love that could please Jesus, but it failed to do so. In this position, Jesus felt indescribable sorrow when the Jewish religion, which was prepared for God's will, became disbelieving and led Him to the cross, just as God felt sorrow when Adam and Eve fell. Therefore, you must become saints who can resolve the grievances of Jesus, who came to resolve the sorrow caused by our ancestors, but because of the disbelief of the Jewish religion, He found Himself again in a position of sorrow. If you cannot become such people, you cannot be the people Jesus desires, nor can you be the people God desires. You must keep this in mind. 

Today, we have gathered to become the people Jesus desires and the people God desires, but there are many conditions around us that prevent us from becoming such people. This is because Satan always blocks our path. Satan is always trying to find conditions for accusations in our lives. In the past, Adam and Eve fell because they could not discern what words were being spoken to them. When Eve heard the words of the archangel, she could not discern whether those words were true or false, and that is where the fall began. So, what should we, who are to restore this today, do? We must have the ability to discern whether the words we hear are good or evil. If you cannot discern what the words you hear mean, you must understand that you will be led into Satan's temptation and commit acts that ruin the heavenly lineage without even realizing it. 

Today, there are many words ringing in your ears on this earth. Among them, there may be words of heaven that represent God, words centered on human pleasures, and words centered on Satan. However, if you cannot discern which realm these words are coming from, you may find yourself hearing Satan's words at any time and in any place, and through that, Satan may take away your life. Therefore, you must always be alert and be able to properly distinguish between good and evil. Jesus, who preached the word to save all people, cried out to the Jewish people at that time, "Let those who have ears hear." Jesus said this because He was confident that those with true ears would hear His words as words of life. However, there was not a single person among the humans on earth who believed His cries as words from heaven. Therefore, Jesus's heart was indescribably sorrowful and painful. 

Thus, we who have gathered to resolve Jesus's sorrow must recognize the words He preached as words that represent our lives and words that represent heaven, and we must listen attentively. We must also reflect on whether we are such beings. You must understand that only by becoming those who listen to the words of heaven can you stand properly before Jesus's will. Furthermore, you must recognize that the words you hear through your ears carry historical and cosmic responsibilities. Next, you must become people who can see correctly. The people of that time could never have imagined that the Messiah sent from heaven to represent 4,000 years of history would appear in such a humble form. That is why they could not see Him as the Messiah. Who knew that Jesus, born as the son of Joseph and working as a carpenter for over 30 years, was the protagonist that God wanted to show to all people? No one knew. No one knew. 

But today, you must be able to see that Jesus is bearing the cross of historical labor. In other words, you must recognize that His very being appeared as a sacrificial offering that could compensate for the entire path of labor God had endured for 4,000 years. If the people of that time had understood that God sent numerous prophets during the 4,000-year historical process to find one Jesus, 


43 If you had known that He had come out, would you have recognized Jesus? Why did Jesus have to bear the cross? It was because the eyes of the Jewish people, who should have been able to see Him clearly, were darkened, and thus Jesus was left alone at the summit of Golgotha. However, Jesus sought to find someone who could understand the circumstances that prevented Him from being in a position of joy, knowing that He alone understood God's will and that He was called to reveal Himself to all people or to show God's internal nature to all. Yet, He could not find that one person and ultimately had to die on the cross. Therefore, you, who are walking the path of purpose today to conclude 6,000 years of history, must find and establish someone who can walk this path with you. If you fail to find and establish such a person, you will not be able to atone for the mistakes of our ancestors who did not recognize Jesus when He appeared. You must keep this in mind. For this reason, today you must place your hearts before the Father and understand how the deceased Jesus is addressing and calling us. In other words, after Jesus cried out alone and died, He sent the Holy Spirit, who is now reaching out to us with deep emotion and expressing His sorrow through actions for us. Thus, you must become people who can atone for the position of the Jews who could not recognize Jesus 2,000 years ago and say, "Indeed, You are the victorious being who has come as the representative of God's will after 4,000 years," and worship Him. Furthermore, you must realize that for 2,000 years since Jesus' departure, Jesus and the Holy Spirit have been working in the spiritual world to find and establish you. If you cannot become such people, you will not be able to resolve the 4,000 years of resentment that was bound at the time of Jesus, nor will you be able to alleviate God's sorrow that has been bound throughout the 2,000 years of history after Jesus. Therefore, you, who are burdened with this historical debt, must not carelessly criticize the words or actions of the past prophets.

44 Thus, today, as Jesus gestures and speaks to us, we must humbly worship before the image of Jesus, who is burning with historical mission, and a being who can become a friend of Jesus must appear. Only when such a being appears on this earth can you follow that person and advance to the position of a bride who can comfort the heart that has labored for 2,000 years through the path of over 30 years of life. 

Should we follow Jesus? Do you know how many times Jesus came to find you when you were caught in sin and groaning in the darkness of death? You may not know. Because this is a land where the destiny of restoration must be fulfilled, Jesus comes to you to ensure that you go through the same path He took to the cross. In other words, because there was a history of God's providence for 4,000 years, sending prophets and saints so that Jesus could establish the purpose of salvation on the cross, God desires to restore this through you. In other words, although we are individuals, we are meant to embody historical value and possess a heart that can completely unite with Jesus. Because you must break free from the bloodline of sin in 6,000 years of history, Jesus is seeking you to resolve the resentment of many prophets and saints who could not fulfill their purpose on earth. That is, Jesus treats you with the same heart with which He addressed Adam, who had not fallen, regardless of when or where you are. God sought to fulfill His purpose through many prophets such as Noah, Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, Moses, and the four great prophets, but they could not fully accomplish God's will. Jesus came to fulfill the purpose of this entire historical providence, but He also could not complete it due to the disbelief of the Jewish people and died on the cross. Now, you must fulfill the historical responsibility that you are to inherit.

45 To do so, you must resemble Jesus, the central being of the universe. In other words, as the central being of the universe, you must atone for all of this and practice the lifestyle that Jesus showed. Only such people can receive testimony from Jesus at the end. Until now, Christians have focused solely on the Lord who died on the cross in their faith. However, this should not be the case. You must understand that Jesus is the one who atoned for 4,000 years of historical processes throughout His life, and you must have faith while looking at Jesus' entire life. Today, there are people who carry out the missions of Abraham, Moses, or John the Baptist, who came and went in the past, but they do not only fulfill personal missions; they are also responsible for the missions of many people who appeared in the historical process. You yourselves bear such missions and responsibilities, and to fulfill them, you must follow the entirety of Jesus' life. If you truly become such people, you will be able to become new beings. 

How many Christians today truly listen to the words of Jesus? Jesus came to find humanity with a heart full of sorrow after walking the path of labor for 6,000 years, without a single moment of comfort. However, there were few who welcomed Jesus with such a heart, comforted His heart, and stood before His dignified image as He desired. If you, who have embarked on the path to become true saints today, have not yet reached such a standard, you must reflect on yourselves. Moreover, you must go a step further and offer yourselves as living sacrifices before Heaven. Today, humanity has become blind to the sorrowful gestures of Jesus reaching out to them. Therefore, now you must have ears that can hear and eyes that can see. You must be able to hear the words of truth and see them as well. Following that, you must have a mouth that can speak the truth on behalf of Jesus. In other words, you must be able to correctly introduce the 6,000 years of history and the life and circumstances of Jesus to the poor humans living on this earth who are in need of the inner heart that Jesus wanted to convey.

46 Such people are being sought by both Jesus and God. Today, you must speak words that resonate with the heart of Jesus. Although you are of the bloodline of the serpent with two tongues, you must not speak with two voices. You must listen to God's words and see God's image and be able to present that fact to all people without deceit, as a person with one tongue, not two. God is seeking a righteous person who can represent His tongue, a person who can represent Jesus' tongue. 

The true saint who must convey the words should be one who possesses a nature centered on God. The heart of a human, created by God, always desires to resemble the heart of Heaven and hopes to make it the standard of their own truth. Humans always wish to be beings of true character. We must restore this original intention and establish the heart and body of Jesus as the center of our own heart and body. Furthermore, through this, we must become the representatives of Jesus and convey the words that Jesus delivered in this world of death. Heaven is seeking those who possess the mouth and tongue to convey Jesus' words in this way. 

Today, humanity has become people who speak with two tongues. Because the heart is one but the speech is two, providential history aims to restore humanity to a state where they speak with one voice. If you speak on behalf of God's words and represent the heart and life of Jesus with confidence, and if you live each day without changing throughout your life, there will be no accusations from Satan against you. You will also be able to overcome the trials of Satan.

47 Therefore, today, you must become true saints who can testify to the true words. In other words, you must convey the words that can unite with God, which have been taught through many prophets and saints, and you must be able to testify to the words that Jesus and the Holy Spirit have conveyed over 2,000 years, and you must be able to initiate the history of recreation. If such people exist, God and Jesus will be with them, countless saints will welcome those words, and those who admire Heaven will naturally follow those words with the help of the spiritual world. Furthermore, if there are those who establish those words as eternal words, the highest words of their lives, with an unchanging heart and dedicate their lives to conveying them, as long as God does not disappear, and as long as Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and countless saints do not disappear, they will surely accomplish the history of recreation on this earth under their protection. 

Therefore, we must understand that the words spoken by Jesus are not limited to 2,000 years ago. So what is the sorrow of Jesus? The closer we get to the end, the more Jesus longs for humanity to follow His heart, which came to seek the world and humanity, and hopes to be embraced by God after going through the path of sacrifice. However, many are unaware of this heart and are led into darkness and brought before the judgment seat by living their own selfish lives. Looking at such a situation, Jesus feels an indescribable sorrow. 

Therefore, you must grasp the heart of Jesus, who looks at you with a heart more sorrowful than when He came to conclude the providence of salvation 2,000 years ago, and you must become a true person who conveys the historical providence that could not be spoken and the words of Jesus regarding the entire universe to all humanity. You must understand that Jesus is earnestly hoping for the appearance of such a true person who can convey His words on His behalf. 

And although Jesus is the one who represents the words of Heaven, He felt the sorrow of not being able to convey all of them and is seeking true Christians who can convey the words on His behalf to those who do not know the fear of judgment. 

48 You must become the people Jesus desires. You must not neglect yourselves. Although you may think of yourselves as insignificant, God has been laboring for 6,000 years to find you. Jesus has labored for 2,000 years, and countless prophets and saints have also worked through the long course of history. Therefore, you must value yourselves and become offerings to establish a condition of victory for God in the final battle against Satan. You must become victors who can say, "I have lived responsibly on behalf of the universe and God." You must be able to accept any words or commands gladly. You must reflect on whether you are truly such beings. 

In ordinary social life, externally, the chosen children of God and those under Satan's authority may appear similar. However, God is seeking true sons and daughters who have the conviction to fully realize the inner and outer character of Jesus Christ, who came to fulfill the purpose of saving humanity with a heart full of sorrow. If you truly possess such a heart, you will feel that you cannot rejoice freely when something joyful happens or be happy carelessly when something pleasant occurs. This is because God's sorrowful heart is connected to the grievances of the world, society, and the countless saints in Heaven. 

Therefore, you must not stop God's sorrowful heart at your individual level, nor should you live limited to your personal or family circumstances. You must possess a standard of character that can resonate with all beings in the universe across time and space, and you must become a value that represents overall completion. If such a person exists on this earth, Heaven will not be disheartened. Furthermore, such a person cannot go to hell. 

You must fight against the evils of your environment in your daily life, bearing this responsibility. You will find that while your heart accepts God's will, your body resists it. Humanity is thus unable to unify heart and body and cannot complete itself as the sons and daughters of God. 

So what is the standard of completion that God desires? It is for humans to accept God's words with their hearts and for their bodies to also accept those words and become one. After that, those words must be conveyed to the surrounding environment. If God's will is realized centered on you, then your heart can move toward eternity through the center of the heart that God permits. Until you complete this standard on earth, you cannot become the true sons and daughters of God. 

How can you know the evidence of being a son or daughter of God? It cannot be known solely through your actions. Actions can be performed by anyone, so one cannot judge based solely on them. The person acting must have the internal value that allows them to say, "I am a son or daughter of God, and a friend of Jesus," and that must be connected to reality for them to be called the sons and daughters of God. 

You must establish a relationship where you can freely exchange commands from God with your body, meaning that your body moves as your heart desires, and your heart moves along with your body. Only then can you be called the sons and daughters of God and initiate the history of recreation on this earth. 

So what should you think about before you pray to God saying, "Father!" today? You must delve into the core of your heart and see if that core can represent the image of Jesus Christ.
50   Let us become the people that Jesus desires. It is a self-questioning and answering process. Because Satan has taken away life from the fallen human ancestors, you do not possess a character that can replace the image of Jesus Christ. Therefore, countless humans have struggled to establish the principles of heaven by transcending the eternal and unchanging heart, the core valley of human conscience, until today. Thus, if you have restored that heart through faith in Jesus, it should not be a problem for you to subjugate your body through the commands of that heart. Those who are to inherit God's will are struggling here today. What resonates in the heart stimulates the body, but the body does not comply. This is due to a lack of power to stimulate the body. Therefore, today you must cultivate the power of the heart that can strongly stimulate the body, and to do that, you must become one who rightly inherits the heart and will of Jesus. For this reason, today Christian believers are praying to Jesus. They long only for the glorious Jesus, not for the suffering Jesus, but that should not be the case. You must understand that Jesus went through an unknown path of suffering before the resurrection and glory. Therefore, you must also overcome the unknown path of suffering to advance to the place of glory, so that you can escape the historical shackles of sin and become a being that possesses the value to relate to the heart of the resurrected Jesus. You can also become a protagonist who can bring about the overall resurrection history on this earth. Now, when you pray before the Father, you must not pray foolishly. You must become a person who can pray through your heart. When the words or actions you express through your body are connected to the center of your heart, those words or actions will not be ashamed before God, Satan, or anyone else. God is seeking such beings. Therefore, if you have the power of nature that can eternally exist in your heart, you must form a true character. No matter what you face or where you are, if you accept such eternal and unchanging core truths and speak from that center, those words will bring about the history of recreation in place of God. 

51   So, where is the enemy you must fight? When you believe in the words Jesus has conveyed and walk the path He has shown, what can stand in your way? It is the Satan that comes through the world, the arrows of Satan that invade through the flesh.
