Just as the archangel who was closest to the Garden of Eden caused the fall of Eve, today Satan appears to you in the closest form to tempt you. It will appear in beautiful forms and with things that sound good. The words that are expressed will seem plausible. Therefore, you must have your own hearing, vision, and an unchanging standard of heart to protect your heart. If you do not have such standards, you cannot prevent the invasion of Satan that comes unexpectedly. On the other hand, if you have such an unchanging core and your body can move according to the desires of your heart, you will live in a way that always pleases God, and you will not need to pray for God to forgive your sins. Because you are a fallen human, you need a prayer of atonement to escape the fate of restoration. Therefore, today, if you have the most important core of the heart that can be compared to the radiant power of the sun, you must possess cosmic knowledge and intellectual standards that can discern all things with your heart and body. Thus, you must become those who can inherit the words that Jesus Christ represented the heavenly nature and the overall will. If you cannot become such beings, God cannot trust and believe in you. Because God only interacts with those who manifest good actions and reveals Himself only through true words. He is not a being that appears in false forms, but is the one true God who possesses one will and one character, and cannot relate to humans who harbor two hearts. You must clearly understand this.

52   You must also realize that the most fearful thing is not Satan, but humans. God manifests His position through good, and Satan through evil, but humans embody both actions. When you step out believing in God, you manifest good, and when centered on Satan, you manifest evil. Therefore, how should you position yourself today? You must not take the position of Satan in your real life. You must not live in a way that can fall under the conditions of Satan's accusations, whether in three-dimensional or two-dimensional aspects. You must possess something that can discern good and evil correctly with sharp wisdom through constant prayer and sincere living. However, you must not pursue wisdom alone. If you only seek wisdom, you can easily become cunning like Satan and make mistakes. So how has Christianity, which said to just believe, become so divided? To what extent should you believe? What is the content of the words you have believed while looking at Jesus with hope? What is the standard of truth established in place of God's will? The words up to today are not enough. You must embody the personality of God, which is the core of truth, and become an unchanging being that achieves oneness with God. Thus, even if the times change and the environment changes, you must become a living being that does not change. If you achieve oneness with God, and if God is an unchanging being, you will also become an unchanging being; if God is the only existence, you will also become the only existence; and if God never leaves His ideal garden, you will not leave that ideal garden either. However, currently, you are not in such a position.

53   You will feel that your current self is more cunning than Satan, whether you wake up in the morning, sleep at night, or act during the day. Therefore, you must regard yourself as more fearful than both God and Satan. The one who has ruined the universe is not Satan, but humans. The one who can revive the universe is also humans. You must remember that it is you who can ruin and revive the universe. And you are at a crossroads where you can become a sign of heaven or a sign of Satan. What must you do to belong to the side of heaven at this crossroads? First, you must be able to hear the words of heaven. Furthermore, you must be able to see the forms of heaven and speak the words of heaven. You must become such a person who can discern good and evil. To do this, you must first fight to find your own individuality. At the same time, you must fight to restore the environment and to restore the world and the universe. Only after going through this process can Jesus come to you. So, in what form will Jesus come? He will come as the ideal standard of resurrection. Thus, He will come to this earth and proclaim the greatest gospel. He will also reveal all glory. When the Lord of universal resurrection comes, you must be someone who follows the Lord without change, even if you are abandoned or killed. Otherwise, you will only see the appearance of Jesus and hear His words. You cannot become a bride who can eternally give and receive love on behalf of heaven in a relationship of bride and groom. When Mary Magdalene went to find Jesus right after the resurrection, Jesus said, “Do not touch me, for I have not yet ascended to my Father” (John 20:17). However, Jesus appeared to Mary Magdalene because she had a heart that could comfort Him. 

54   In this way, you must feel the ideals and will of heaven beyond yourself, and it is in that feeling that the Lord will appear. If you can hear God's words and convey God's words instead, the Lord will come without you needing to call Him. Rather, you must understand that the Lord is beckoning you and opening His arms towards you. God is the same. God desires to see true sons and daughters appear. Today, if we cannot bear this cosmic responsibility, we cannot awaken the sleeping nations and the world. Now is the time to enter a four-dimensional world that transcends time and space. At such a time, if you become a heavenly person with a three-dimensional character, or a cosmic person, and live while understanding the inner heart of heaven, being able to hear, see, and speak, even if you say, “God, do not come. Jesus, do not come,” God and Jesus cannot help but follow you. Even if such a person is sent to hell, he will turn hell into heaven. Only when many such people appear will peace come to this earth. Today, you must not pray to go up, but you must learn to pray to let God come down to you. If a true Christian who can be a person that can be the bride of Jesus appears on this earth, God Himself will come and find him. In other words, if true sons and daughters of peace and true sons and daughters of love, whom God has awaited for 6,000 years, appear on this earth, not only will God be pleased, but all creation will rejoice with them, and you must be sure of this. 

55   Today, Christianity carries the weight of this cosmic mission on its shoulders, yet it does not deeply realize this and merely calls out “God the Father.” This should not be the case. After walking the path of the cross and overcoming adversity, you must call out, “Father!” Such a person will be sought by heaven. Moreover, if you establish the standard of such a heart in your daily life, what you wish to see will be shown to you, and your words will come forth naturally before you even speak. You must advance to this level. However, there are enemies that block you here. Just as the Israelite people blocked Jesus with their conventional conditions during His 30 years of life, similar events appear to you today. Therefore, you must not become like the Israelite people who appeared in the historical process today. You must boldly break through the past customs that have been handed down historically. You, who are seeking a new ideal garden toward the fruits of resurrection! You must connect the historical phenomena to your body and mind, penetrate the heavenly will, and become those who can host Christ and represent the character of Christ. Only such beings can receive and bear what God wants to say, show, and convey in the new ideal garden. You must follow the path that Jesus walked, breaking through the conventional conditions that appeared in the historical process, and love God. Even when difficult environments confront you on the path of heavenly will, you must not complain, and even when faced with the trials of Satan that evoke fear and terror, you must become those who can overcome and host the Lord. You must host the Lord in the highest freedom among freedoms, the highest glory among glories, and the highest joy among joys. Thus, you must be able to call upon the Father, free from all the conditions of accusation that Satan historically presented. When you become such beings, heaven will come to you before you speak. Therefore, you must establish such standards in your life process. God will first seek a person who possesses the value of a compassionate personality centered on His cosmic love, a person who represents Jesus and history. Jesus desires that such people gather to find the nation, the world, and the heavenly earth. You must also understand that this is God's will.

56   Let us become the people that Jesus desires. Even if you find yourselves caught in the conditions of Satan's accusations, or if countless waves of adversity try to subdue you, you must become a practitioner who inherits the entire secret within God and Jesus as an unchanging being, who not only escapes the conditions of Satan's accusations but also becomes the victorious protagonist who can fight and subdue Satan, comforting God and Jesus. When Jesus was nearing the day of His crucifixion, He gathered His beloved disciples and said, “I still have many things to say to you, but you cannot bear them now” (John 16:12). This shows that the apostles did not understand Jesus' will. Therefore, you must become a bride who understands Jesus' will, not an apostle who does not understand it, and establish the standard of personality that can advance to the position of a wife, taking responsibility for the will left by Jesus and being able to comfort Him. You must be able to subdue Satan and come before God, saying, “Please receive the eternal glory of victory alone.” Only then will God's resentment, which has been accumulated over 6,000 years of restoration providence, be resolved, and you will be able to find the true bride that Jesus has been seeking. Furthermore, you will be able to find the true wife that Jesus Christ desires and build the garden of peace on this earth. Now, you who have stepped out according to the will must remember that you are a being more fearful than Satan, and regardless of the process or difficulties you face, no matter how harsh the circumstances, you must hold onto the will you have set in your heart and fight unchangingly until the day you receive the recognition of heaven, humbly bowing before Jesus. Only by becoming such a person can you truly become the person Jesus desires, and all humanity will set you in the place of glory before the Father as a standard of love. You must keep this in mind.

<Word> The title of the message I would like to think about with you at this time is ‘Jesus Who Seeks to Establish the Love of Heaven.’ I will speak briefly under this title. 

The Love of God That Needs to Be Found Again Because an eternal center could not be established on this fallen earth, the love that God wishes to seek has also not been established, as you all know well. The purpose of God’s creation was to create a world of love where created beings and God could eternally give and receive the utmost love. However, because humanity fell without knowing God’s such intention, that world has not been realized. Therefore, God’s love remains as a standard of hope before the entire universe and humanity, which you must understand. For this reason, today, we humans have a providential responsibility to seek and establish this love of God as an eternal ideal for all creation. Although countless people have lived on this earth until now, the standard that can fulfill this inner love of God and realize the overall ideals of humanity has not yet been completely established. Thus, God has been working hard to establish that standard until now, and you must understand that He must continue to work until the day comes when the heavenly love that remains as hope for humanity is connected and all created beings can sing that love as eternal love.

The history of God’s labor has passed 6,000 years, and if an individual has received the grace to feel God’s love, that grace is not just for that individual. It is a grace that must be established as a love that can bring joy to all people and to the countless saints in heaven, the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit. Only then can I rejoice, and all people can rejoice and resonate together, and the countless saints in the heavenly world can resonate together. When God’s grace manifests as a love that brings joy to heaven and earth, in other words, only after that love, which must be sought, is found, can God finally forget all grievances and sorrows and rejoice. You must deeply realize this. Therefore, fallen humanity must meet a central being, which is the condition of victorious destiny and the unchanging reality of love, whether they live or die as long as life remains. Only by meeting such a central being can a day and time come when God can enjoy. If humanity cannot accomplish this, their sorrows will not end. As long as human sorrow continues, sorrow in heaven will also continue, and as long as sorrow remains in heaven, God’s sorrow will also continue. 

Thus, the one center that is established as the eternal and unchanging reality of love, representing heaven and earth, is the root of hope that all humanity and all creation must meet, and the one who was sent as that root of hope, as the central being to establish the standard of eternal and unchanging love, is Jesus Christ. However, until Jesus came to this earth, there were many prophets who worked hard to introduce the love of heaven through the 4,000 years of history, and there were countless saints who, through uncountable hardships and trials, worked hard to connect the standard of love that God sought. Their labor was all in hope of the one Jesus, who is the center of all created beings that wish to live within God’s will. Therefore, God chose and established nations and peoples centered around such people, allowing them to prepare to welcome Jesus. 

On the other hand, with the coming of Jesus, who represents the nation of Israel, the joy of heaven reached the earth, and the hope of the earth reached heaven, allowing heaven and earth to finally resolve the grievances of 4,000 years and rejoice together. 

The Mission and Hope Centered on Love Jesus had to first experience God’s love in His life and then appear before all people as the embodiment of God’s love. Therefore, after 4,000 years, He finally revealed the eternal love of God to all humanity, and to resolve the grievances of 4,000 years, the heart of Jesus, who was sent as the embodiment of love, always wanted to meet someone who could connect God’s love to humanity. Thus, Jesus sought such a gathering and nation. However, because the Jewish people did not believe in Jesus, the love of God that He sought to reveal through His life and the will of God that He worked for over 4,000 years could not be fulfilled, and Jesus had to walk the path of the cross of grievance. You must realize this. If the Jewish people had recognized Jesus as the Messiah who stood in place of God, as the embodiment of God’s love, as the reality of hope that their ancestors fought for with blood for 4,000 years, they would have held onto Jesus and said, “You are our hope, the embodiment of eternal love of God, the one who will resolve the grievances of heaven and connect that joy to us, the ancestor who will connect God’s love to us.” However, there was not a single person like that at the time. Everything Jesus saw, heard, and thought was aimed at establishing a victorious standard of love that could forever tear down the barriers between humanity and God. However, there was not a single person who could be a counterpart to His mission. 

Therefore, Jesus said, “No one knows the Son except the Father who sent me.” This statement carries the sorrow and anguish of Jesus. The Jesus who came to resolve the grievances of heaven, the Jesus who came to testify of God’s love, and the Jesus who came to connect God’s love from the world of creation to heaven did not know the hearts of the people at that time, nor did they understand His will. Therefore, now you must become believers who understand the sorrow of not only Jesus but also God, who was saddened because the Jewish people did not recognize and believe in Jesus, who was sent from God. If you do not, you must understand that you will become people who have no connection to the heavenly love of God. Now you must clearly understand what the Lord will desire when He returns at the end. The returning Lord will take responsibility for the disbelief of the Jewish people who did not believe in Jesus, who came 2,000 years ago, and will seek true people who can realize His will by understanding that He is the center of God’s love, the embodiment of love that must be revealed, and what Jesus desired. 

Because the Jewish people did not believe, Jesus, who brought the love of God, found Himself in a sorrowful situation where He could not fulfill His responsibilities. This sorrow of Jesus was not only His own sorrow but also the sorrow of countless prophets throughout history who came with the determination to believe in God, and moreover, it was the sorrow of God the Father, who is working to realize the purpose of creation. The Jesus who came to bring joy to the spirits of the heavenly world and the ancestors had to die on the cross due to human disbelief, and as a result, He caused God to bear even more sorrow. This was the mistake committed by the Jewish people, and you must understand that this grievance still remains on this earth. 

We must not forget that when Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, “My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as You will.” (Matthew 26:39), His lonely situation was not only His own, and you must also understand that the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who went to the cross with the burdens of thirty years, was not only His own. His situation is our situation and the situation that humanity must face today. Furthermore, the reason Jesus prayed and grieved was not because He was going to perish and die, nor was it because He had to overcome a sorrowful fate. He was worried about the responsibility He had to reach the destination of history while carrying the heart of heavenly, sorrowful love, and He was concerned about how He, who was sent to replace God’s love, could make humanity the embodiment of God’s love. He was also worried about the fact that all humanity must overcome the peak of sorrow. You must understand that Jesus was not one who had sorrow only for Himself or anguish only for Himself.

Responsibilities of the Saints at the End So, what kind of people should we become? Just as Jesus fulfilled the victorious mission of establishing the love of heaven alone before Judaism, which has borne the providential history of 4,000 years, today you must stand before Christianity, which bears the providential history of 6,000 years, and testify to God’s love. Furthermore, you must become true co-workers of Christ, who is coming to build a world where all can eternally rejoice and resonate. If you do not fulfill such a mission, the Lord will not be able to come to this earth. You must also understand that God cannot send a Messiah centered on God’s love to this earth. If we, who have inherited the blood of our ancestors who betrayed the will of heaven over 6,000 years, repeat the sinful path of our ancestors, how can the Lord come to such a place again? 

We must remember that the first coming of Jesus was as the center of cosmic love, as the Lord of the universe, who could breathe the love of heaven on behalf of heaven and earth.
64   We must understand that Jesus had to go to the cross because the people of His time did not become His co-workers in establishing the love of heaven. However, even if hope and faith disappear on the path toward the ideal of life, the path toward the love that can endure forever is a historical path of destiny that one cannot avoid. Therefore, although Jesus went to the cross to lead humanity along this path, the Holy Spirit has taken over that mission and has been working on earth. Under the guidance of the Holy Spirit, how far have we come? We have reached a position similar to that of Mary, who was able to have hope by meeting the resurrected Jesus after going through the moment just before His resurrection. So, if we now seek the love of God that can embrace the universe, what should we do? We must become the substantial brides of love that fulfill the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, the substantial brides of love that Jesus sought during His time. That is why today we are wandering in search of the name of the bride. If there had been true saints 2,000 years ago, Jesus could have stood as a being of hope on this earth. However, among our ancestors who have come through history until today, there has been no one who has fulfilled this hope of Jesus. The entire purpose that God has been guiding for the past 2,000 years since Jesus came and went is to find and establish true people who can comfort God's sorrowful heart, true people who can comfort Jesus, who felt sorrow on Mount Calvary, true people who can comfort the Holy Spirit, and true people who can comfort heaven and earth. A person who knows this will be able to approach God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit and say, "Is this not what You are seeking?" and should be able to urge to fulfill that task. Until such true saints appear, the sorrow and resentment that dwell within God and the grievances of Jesus and the Holy Spirit will not be resolved. If three people had held onto Jesus’ command to love me more than anyone else, representing God, who had worked hard for 4,000 years to establish Jesus, and had been willing to die for God's will while believing in and following Jesus and the Holy Spirit, Satan would have naturally surrendered. However, the ignorant disciples did not realize that there was a purpose to establish such a heavenly religion that represented the work of the Trinity in the human world. Therefore, you must possess wisdom. You must be equipped with wisdom and knowledge regarding God's providence, and you must be those who clearly understand the heavenly content. You should not stand in the position of the apostles, who followed Jesus yet did not understand His deep intentions. You must become people who can dedicate your lives to the church and purpose that called and chose you, establishing the heavenly countenance. Only then can the kingdom that Jesus hoped for finally appear on earth, and we can naturally overcome the enemy, Satan.

73 Therefore, a person must appear on this earth who can mobilize the countless saints and angels in heaven and the saints on earth, centered on the heavenly character, to naturally overcome Satan and sing the glory of heaven, and who can gather all of them for the restoration providence. Only then can we realize the hope and love of Jesus, who dedicated His heart, will, character, and strength, and live within the eternal realm of God's love, where we cannot help but rejoice. <Prayer> Please allow us to realize at this moment that we are pitiful beings who live in a biased manner, thinking that we are not. Father! Have we ever offered our hearts, wills, and strength to You? If there has never been a time when we represented humanity, nations, and the world, please allow us to repent of this and become sons and daughters who deeply feel our own shortcomings before You. Now we understand that we must offer our entire lives to You, and we must dedicate all our strength to You, and we must offer our bodies and hearts to You, and we must dedicate our characters to You. Knowing the circumstances of the Father, who cannot accept anything less than the best, we have offered what is left over before heaven and have lived carelessly, so please forgive us. Now, following the example of Jesus, who worked hard to fulfill the heavenly will, we will emotionally dedicate everything to You, so please bless us, loving Father, as we earnestly wish and desire. Father! From this day forward, please allow us to be those who can feel the heart of Jesus, who longed for heaven regardless of life and death. May we become those who resemble the heavenly character and will centered on new love, and may we live a heavenly life centered on love so that we can serve heaven.

I earnestly wish and desire this, Father. Now, even if we repent and shed tears, let it be on a global scale, and even if we dedicate our hearts, let it be on a cosmic scale, and even if we dedicate our wills, let it be universal, and let us be guided to be more than enough in dedicating our characters to the cosmic level. Who will bear the burden of fate caused by the fall in this lonely path of restoration where we cannot escape? At this time, when the appeals of grievances are penetrating heaven and earth, we earnestly wish and desire that You open the way for us to move forward. To walk the path that You guide us on, we must first find a place where our lives can rest, and then our hearts and bodies must become Your resting place, knowing that Your love must dwell in our hearts and bodies. O Father of mercy, O Father of love, O Father of kindness, who is working hard to manifest Your will among us! We come before You with our dirty and wounded hearts and bodies, but please accept us. If You do not accept us and do not become the standard for our path forward, there will be no one more pitiful than us. Father! The crowd gathered here is a group of children who have been worried and anxious while looking up to heaven, even if it means dedicating their entire lives to walk the path of life that heaven desires.

What remains in us centered on ourselves in terms of heart, will, ideas, and claims?

79 In the Bible passage we read today, it says, “Whatever a man sows, that he will also reap.” (Galatians 6:7). Therefore, Jesus carries the unresolved grievances in His heart, praying for a long time that God's original will be realized again on earth, and we must understand that He will surely return to fulfill this will. In this way, Jesus came for the sake of all people who are to be saved as the object of God's goodness. For this reason, He had the mission to come to this earth to defeat and eliminate Satan while realizing God's ideals as His representative. And Jesus had to walk a life that would bring joy to God. Thus, it was not by His death that Jesus fulfilled this will, but it had to be accomplished while He was alive. If that had happened, Christians would not have had to toil and plead for 2,000 years waiting for Jesus to return and live a life of prayer. Today, we must walk the path that Jesus walked in order to fulfill all the goals He established and the purpose for which He was born. Now, if we do not fulfill God's will even at the cost of our lives, then God cannot gather us as the fruit of goodness. God did not create humans to live only in the spiritual world but to have a substantial existence on this earth, harmonizing spirit and flesh. Therefore, you must understand that Jesus, who came to this earth as the embodiment of goodness after 4,000 years of history, cannot remain only as the spiritual King of kings after His death. In other words, while daily life may allow for direct and well-established relationships centered on oneself, if there is a person who cannot live confidently centered on themselves throughout their life, they cannot be offered as a good harvest to God. As long as there are responsibilities left to fulfill, you must overcome any difficulties and fulfill your responsibilities, and as long as there is a destiny to fight, you must be prepared to fight to the death. Now that you know what the purpose of goodness that Jesus aimed for was and how to reach it, you must live in a way that aligns your heart and body with the desires of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. As such, you must be able to stand with Jesus on your right and the Holy Spirit on your left, and before God, say, "Heavenly Father! I have fought and won against Satan to fulfill Your will." Then God will establish the ideals of Jesus and the Holy Spirit before the people of this earth through you, entrusting you with new work and enabling you to realize it. Thus, God will be able to complete His intention of resting Jesus and the Holy Spirit in the heavenly kingdom and establishing them on this earth. Just because someone is a witness among the people of the earth does not mean they are established as a representative being who fulfills God's will. First, Jesus and the Holy Spirit must rejoice through them, and they must be able to work for the mission entrusted to them. As long as there is a purpose to be achieved, that purpose must be represented by one person.
Since it is to be established from 93, if the intention that started from that one person can bear fruit to encompass the whole, it will be realized as one religion, and the prophets and sages will gather around that religion. In this way, if we can move toward the eternal and cosmic Canaan welfare following the chosen central figure of one person, it is fulfilling the responsibility as the chosen people of Israel. Only then will God be able to settle the cosmic resentment in this land and enjoy the joy of fulfilled wishes along with the spirit of Jesus, and instill the joy that God feels into all people. This will also resolve the resentment that exists within humanity. You wish to overcome a critical juncture in history and desire to resolve resentments, and you must advance to a position where you can give thanks and worship to God for those resolutions, becoming a substantial reality of goodness that transcends history. Thus, I hope you can become those who can take responsibility and settle the profound resentment of God, all creation, and humanity at the end of days, which is difficult to express. 

<Prayer> Father, who calls these little ones and works to find the cosmic fruit of goodness! Each of us is in a cosmic destiny that must be harvested as the fruit of goodness through your touch, yet we have not recognized this fact nor even imagined it. However, now we have realized that the fruit of goodness can only be achieved through that one being who can step forward without any hindrance to conscience after our hearts and bodies become one. I earnestly ask that you move their hearts, and I pray all these words in your name. Amen.

<What kind of resurrection do you wish to achieve?> 
1 Corinthians 15:35-44 

<Prayer> My Father! In the beginning, you had the will of goodness and created all things, and you were in an unchanging form as the standard of essential nature. However, because humans could not become the counterpart of your goodness, they could not fulfill your ideals, and they have become distant from the standard of good conscience. I know that this has been the groaning of heaven and all creation. Father, we have a providential path that we must seek the eternal standard of goodness with our lives, and we have a mission to walk this path to the end, so please urge us with your great power to walk this way. The evil elements that invade through the body are blocking the path of the heart that seeks goodness, so Father! Please guide our hearts that seek goodness in this struggle not to become defeated by the restraints of the body. May we be led solely by the power of goodness and the power of love, so that we can seek you and become an eternal being who cannot be separated from you, resembling your form, and may we live forever in your presence, my Father, I earnestly wish and desire this. Through the long historical process of fighting against sin, we have become wounded, and the roots of sin are embedded in our bones and flesh. We must remove this. 

We have the responsibility to achieve what kind of resurrection, but we are so inadequate. Father, who has the authority of life, Father, who has the authority of power, Father, who has the authority of creation, please stretch out your powerful hand once more to our insignificant hearts and bodies, and remove all evil elements that are captured in the shadow of death. I earnestly wish and desire that you may show us the direct work of heaven that can raise the heart of victory, stimulated by that one center. Thus, may you raise the power of resurrection from within myself, and allow us to be your sons and daughters who can raise the work of resurrection in place of that one center in the environment we are in, my Father, I earnestly wish and desire this. Please lead us not to be those who sigh because we are in a deficient position, but allow us to qualify as true children of the Father by winning in the battle against the enemy satans that block this path in the journey toward the perfect position. Guide us to be sons and daughters who can boast before countless satans. Thus, may we be allowed to bear the weapons that the heavenly hosts had, to fight and win against countless satans, my beloved Father, I earnestly wish and desire this. 

Father, at this time, a small group kneels and bows before you to confess their inadequacies. If there is anything unworthy in us, please give us a heart of repentance that can reflect on ourselves, grant us a heart of wisdom that can realize, and allow us to have eyes and hearts that can discern good and evil. So that we can see and realize correctly, I earnestly wish and desire that your direct work may be with us during this hour. Now this hour is a time to present offerings before you, so even if we have nothing to offer, please allow us to fully dedicate our original heart. Remove the evil elements from our bodies stained with sin, and allow us to honestly reveal ourselves before you, moving according to your commands and becoming bodies and hearts that are in accordance with your will, my beloved Father, I earnestly wish and desire this. 

On this evening, may the promised grace be uniformly bestowed upon the countless sons and daughters who are building lonely altars everywhere. As we approach the end, may the history of inspiration and influence, the history of power that can fulfill your will, be manifested wherever your children are. There are many sons and daughters who are building altars of prayer in solitude to find the true altar, so please command them to gather in one place quickly, so that they may become children who are not lacking in raising the banner of victory of the Father forever. In every place where we gather to worship at the heavenly altar during this hour, may your holy spirit's work be with us, and may the history of inspiration and repentance be manifested, leading us to become altars that can fulfill the mission entrusted to this nation at the end. I pray that the remaining time may be governed according to your will, and I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Word> The title of the message I will give you today is "What kind of resurrection do you wish to achieve?" Because Adam and Eve fell, we humans have remained far from God's love. However, before the fall, Adam and Eve did not know that if they fell, the God who once treated them joyfully would turn into a God of fear, and the God of ideals would become a God of judgment. For us, the descendants of the fall, there will surely come a time when we can face God as both a God of fear and a God of ideals. God's providential history has been repeated so that humans may correspond to that providence, allowing God to stand before humans as the God of ideals. However, to those under the dominion of Satan, God appears as the God of judgment and fear. Therefore, in order for us to regard God as the God of ideals, we must experience God's sorrow caused by human fallenness, becoming beings who can relate to God's sorrowful position and dwell with God. Otherwise, God cannot appear to us as the God of ideals, nor can He manifest as the protagonist of creation. 

In this journey towards embracing the God of ideals, we must go through the path of struggle against the satans that block this way. This is the path of indemnity and restoration that fallen humans must inevitably walk. In other words, if I do not have a path of struggle to rescue all of humanity from the fear of judgment while looking at the ideal, you must understand that you cannot find God's ideals. Resurrection is not achieved like natural laws; rather, it is realized through my own struggle to overcome fear and crush the forces of darkness. You must remember that only the spirit of resurrection that has triumphed over the sufferings of darkness can advance to the position of facing God's ideals. God has been working through the long span of 6,000 years to fulfill that one purpose. Therefore, we must become one with God to fulfill His ideals, equipping ourselves with the nature of truth as the substance of God's hope living on this earth, and unite with the resurrected beings who have fought and won against evil. 

If that happens, our hearts and God's heart will feel one love, allowing us to fulfill God's providence to restore the ideals of creation. Otherwise, the providence of God that has come down for 6,000 years will remain unfulfilled. That is why we are in a destiny where we must go through the path of struggle. In this path of struggle, since fallen humans cannot destroy the forces of Satan with their own power, God has sent Jesus Christ as the protagonist who can destroy them. That is why Jesus Christ, although He lived a short life of over 30 years on this earth, did not meet the days of peace and joy. In other words, if we trace His footsteps, we can see that His life was marked by tears shed in the struggle against Satan. Today, we must reflect on the sorrowful family life of Jesus Christ in our daily lives. We must become saints who earnestly pray before heaven while engaging in the struggle to repel the darkness of sin with our lives. 

The purpose of Jesus walking the path of suffering was to completely awaken humans who have been asleep in the bosom of Satan since the fall, leading them to a free environment governed by God, restoring them as true people, that is, original people, to establish a foundation of joy and glory. Therefore, all the feelings, shocks, and impulses He experienced through His senses during His life were not limited to one day or confined to a limited time. Even though His gaze and footsteps were within the bounds of a certain time, His purpose and ideals were connected to the eternal love in God's heart, and He lived with a heart filled with the sorrowful heart of God. You must understand that Jesus lived with a heart that experienced God's love and ideals, so all His knowledge and feelings were not separate from God's love and ideals. 

That is why He opened the path of struggle in His life centered on God's love and ideals, aiming to resurrect both spirit and body, going through the paths of restoration of growth and completion to find the unfallen original human form. Thus, Jesus fought alone against the forces of Satan. Jesus, as the protagonist who could face the cosmic ideals of God and embodied God's love, fought throughout His life to establish a standard that could resurrect the whole and offer it to God, but because the Israelite people did not believe in Him, He could not fulfill God's ideals of resurrecting humanity in spirit and body and returned. You must understand this. The life path from the moment Jesus was born on this earth until His resurrection three days after His crucifixion shows what will unfold in our life paths today, and it reveals that we must go through the end times in the cosmic historical process. Therefore, we too must walk the path of the cross like Jesus. We must fight as Jesus fought against Satan. If we do not inherit the ideals and love that Jesus desired, we will not be able to repel Satan, nor will we be able to fulfill God's ideals that He wished to enjoy through Jesus. 

Jesus was supposed to carry out the cosmic resurrection event on earth, equipped with the substantial reality of resurrection in spirit and body, commanding all people as the body of God. However, because He died on the cross, He is now working as the protagonist who only achieved spiritual resurrection. To realize the purpose of spiritual resurrection on earth, He is conducting the work of fulfilling this through the Holy Spirit. Therefore, in order for us today to surpass the standard of cosmic resurrection that Jesus desires, we must first unite with the Holy Spirit, who carries out God's providence on earth, to establish an eternal relationship with Him. And to re-establish the lost ideals of resurrection, we must fight the battles that Jesus fought, united with the Holy Spirit. Otherwise, we will not be able to cross the hill of the cross and reach the place where the resurrected Jesus received the gift of resurrection from God.
101 When Jesus comes again to this earth, He must not repeat the path He took 2,000 years ago when He came and died on the cross. The One who will come again must be the One who fights against Satan with the glory of resurrection and the authority of heaven, and must advance to a position where He is worshipped by millions of saints. You must understand this. After the resurrection of Jesus, the Holy Spirit has a mission to fight against Satan secondarily, alongside humanity, in place of Jesus, who fought against Satan on earth. This is why the Holy Spirit is working from the same position as Jesus. Until today, this has been the history of forming a global Christian shape through Christian believers. When such a history is realized, just as Jesus Christ bore the cross and fought against Satan to victory, the saints and the Holy Spirit will become one, and the Holy Spirit and the church will become one, enabling them to fight against Satan and achieve victory. 

The Responsibility of the Saints
We must not only resemble the image of Christ, who triumphed over Satan by offering our bodies as living sacrifices, but we must also become true Christians who can represent Jesus, who had to gather nations and the world with His living body to achieve victory. If we fail to do this, we cannot atone for the sin of having caused Jesus to die on the cross and cannot live to achieve victory. As we walk the path of resurrection, we must realize our shortcomings and lament, asking ourselves, “Can you, a mere individual, represent the global cross of the saints who have fought faithfully for 2,000 years, just as Jesus fought for humanity’s resurrection even to the point of being crucified?” 

When we stand before God at the end, if God asks, “What kind of life have you lived for the glory of resurrection?” we must be able to answer without hesitation. Otherwise, we will become individuals unrelated to God’s ideals. If we are to walk the difficult path of the cross, none among us will be able to confidently say that we will not repeat the path of the twelve disciples who, fearing the length, looked after their own bodies while following Jesus. 

In this historical process of the end times, we must coldly analyze how worthy our lives have been for our own resurrection and reflect on how much we feel God’s love and how we can fulfill God’s ideals and will. If we cannot have the confidence that we can bravely navigate the path of the cross that Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit walked to resolve the grievances of 6,000 years, in other words, if we cannot control our own bodies, if our bodies cannot control the environment, and if we do not possess the ability to block the fears coming from Satan with an eternal and unchanging appearance centered in our hearts, we must remember that we cannot fulfill the purpose for which Jesus Christ sent the Holy Spirit after overcoming the cross in His 30 years of life. 

So, what attitude should we have as we are to kick open the door of cosmic fear at the end? You must have the following resolve before heaven. First, you must become one who can represent the life of Jesus Christ. When we see the foundation of Jesus’ heart, who sought to achieve internal resurrection, we realize that He was born on this earth and lived for over 30 years solely to fulfill the will of God, and even until the moment of His death, He had no regrets about His life. Jesus did not fear death or blame Himself until the moment He passed away. Rather, you must understand that He maintained a humble heart before God even as He passed away. 

By giving up His life and returning to fulfill the will of heaven, He had the attitude of saying, “I will boldly walk the victorious path of death for the sake of my Father’s will,” and because He had such a heart, the responsibility for that death was taken on by God. When we, with the cooperation of the Holy Spirit who represents the image of Christ, seek to pass through the door of judgment at the end, we must understand that we cannot help but walk the path that Jesus Christ walked in victory on the way to the cross. Jesus never once asserted Himself before heaven while standing before God’s will and fighting against Satan throughout His 30 years. Even when He had joyful moments, He did not rejoice alone. And even when He achieved victories, He did not live with the notion that those victories were solely His own or that He alone was responsible for them. 

Jesus dedicated all of His time to God until the moment He died on the cross. He was consumed with the desire to fulfill His Father’s will, worrying that the mission given to Him by God would remain on earth until the moment He died. You must also understand that He felt the responsibility to save even His enemies and prayed for them. 

The Resurrection of Glory, the Resurrection of Shame, the Resurrection of Death
As we live our faith, even if we receive the gift of resurrection, we must have the heart of Jesus, who could not rejoice centered on Himself. You must also understand the many miracles that Jesus performed. So, how should we appear before the Lord, who has entered into the glory of resurrection after walking the path of labor? There are three forms. First, there will be those who, while being fully devoted and loyal, say, “I am unworthy and cannot dare to stand before the Lord. I deserve to die a million times.” In other words, there will be those who, while taking on the sins remaining on this earth, fight, weep, and devote themselves to the point of death, yet before God, they possess a humble heart that says, “I am unworthy to stand before You.” 

102 You must ask yourself, “What kind of resurrection do you wish to achieve?” And if there are those who, when looking at God, cannot dare to lift their faces, and who, with a trembling heart, only look to God’s disposition and do not desire the glory of heaven, God will turn their sad hearts into joyful ones, and even if they are lacking, He will comfort them instead of condemning them. Even if we have devoted ourselves fully to God and have become living sacrifices that can stand boldly before Him, if we bow our heads with a heart of concern acknowledging our shortcomings, God will bestow glory upon that concerned heart and provide comfort to that sad heart. In other words, only such individuals can receive the glory of resurrection. 

Second, there will be those who appear before God with the confidence that “I have done my utmost for heaven and walked the path for heaven, so I should be able to receive the divinity of the Father.” Originally, as humans walk the path toward heaven, they will increasingly feel their shortcomings. And it is only by recognizing their deficiencies and imperfections that they can find a way to supplement their shortcomings. However, there are those who, at one time, established conditions to boast before heaven and received recognition for their hard work for heaven, and they may appear before the Father saying, “I have followed the path that Jesus walked and have come before You,” lifting their faces with confidence. But the path that such individuals have walked is different from the path that Jesus Christ walked, so when they go to the other world, they will not be able to fully cross the door of the cross. 

Thirdly, there are those who cannot stand before heaven, cannot stand before people, and cannot stand before the countless saints and angels in the other world, who are in the position of enemies of heaven and have no relation to Jesus’ will. These individuals will also receive resurrection after death. Those who correspond to the first type will receive the glory of resurrection, those who correspond to the second type will receive the resurrection of shame, and those who correspond to the third type will receive the resurrection of death. At the end, there will be these three types of resurrection. 

So, what kind of resurrection path are you walking today? You must analyze yourselves. If you discover that there are conditions you need to settle, you must boldly settle them. And you must carry the heart that acknowledges your shortcomings and bow your head, feeling increasingly inadequate as you walk the path of sacrifice. Otherwise, you will not be able to inherit eternal happiness and enjoy the blessings of God’s creation in the ideal garden centered on God’s eternal love. When the first type of person stands before the Lord, although their heart may seem troubled, it will ultimately become filled with glory and hope. The second type of person, who approaches the Lord with a heart full of hope and glory, will ultimately become troubled, and the third type of person will receive the resurrection of death, unable to even mourn for Jesus Christ or hope for a connection with heaven. 

The Attitude of a Believer Who Can Participate in the Glory of Resurrection
After realizing what type of resurrection you belong to, what should you do? What kind of appearance should you take, whether joyful or sorrowful? You must become like the first type, even if you are to host the Lord whom you have hoped for and envisioned for 2,000 years, possessing a humble heart and shedding tears of gratitude. You must not become like the second type, standing before the Lord with a sorrowful position and bowing your head. And you must not become like the third type, standing in a position where you cannot even admire Jesus and God in your dreams. Such individuals, even if they have hope, will find that their hope begins and ends with themselves, and no matter how much they suffer in hell hoping for a resurrection beyond that, they will not be able to conceive of that ideal. 

When we think of this, we, who believe in the gospel of Christ today, that is, we who must fulfill the purpose of resurrection, must humbly bow our heads and possess a heart filled with awe, even if we are to participate in the glory of the Lord in the other world. We must carry such a heart and, with the compassion of the Lord and the love of the Father, fight against enemies to fulfill God’s ideals, hoping for the glory of Christ’s resurrection. If we do not complete this task on earth, we will be destined to atone for it even when we go to the other world. Therefore, today, as we live our faith, we must completely forget ourselves and become sacrifices, feeling our inadequacies, and even in the face of death, we must be able to admonish ourselves. 

We must understand that only by becoming individuals who boast of nothing before heaven can we fulfill the eternal ideals of resurrection in heaven. Those who live with such a heart will, when they receive gifts from the Father, worry that they might return sorrow and shame before heaven while trying to establish themselves in place of the Father. And the greater the gifts they have received, the more they will feel their own shortcomings in proportion to that, and the more they feel that the gifts they have received are precious, the more they will feel inadequate before the Father to the point of not knowing where to place themselves. If there are such individuals, Satan will not be able to test them. 

Thus, for the glory of resurrection, centered on the love of heaven, you must fully experience the ideals of heaven with your body and heart, and if you do not seek the day when you can express gratitude before the Father, you must realize that you cannot complete the ideals of resurrection that God desires and cannot live enjoying eternal happiness centered on God’s ideals and God’s love. Therefore, you must feel your shortcomings more and more as the days go by. You must deeply feel that God works the history of resurrection and the history of re-creation centered around such individuals. Only then can you go to the glorious place where no one else can go when the Lord returns. You must realize this and, from this moment on, with a new resolve and determination, stand in the position of a sacrifice to testify to the true light in this dark world and live a life that reveals the glory of Christ’s resurrection. 

7) Let’s Go Beyond the World of Sacrifice
Romans 12:1-12
<Prayer> Father, please guide us not to forget that today is the time when the purpose of Your providence, which You have worked for 6,000 years, weighs upon our entire lives. Father! This earth is the land where You have labored and shed blood, and it is also the land where humanity has walked the difficult path of the cross, the global Golgotha. Please lead us to realize what position we are in today. If we acknowledge that we are following the footsteps that Jesus walked for over 30 years, please guide us to clearly understand what kind of environment we are living in and what we should hope and wish for. Now, as the remaining battle of the cross approaches us, we must have a self-aware heart that can push away all this pain and resentment. O heaven, have mercy on us at this time. Lead us to feel our shortcomings and to recognize our inadequacies. 
March 10, 1957, Sunday, Former Headquarters Church.
109 Please allow us to be in a state of repentance for our own imperfections and to shed tears of sorrow before the Father. We earnestly wish for this time. Father! Please have mercy on this nation. Allow the powerful hand of the Father, who can lead us to the garden of light, to quickly manifest among the thirty million people. And awaken the slumbering humanity around the world, allowing the grievances of the countless saints who have assisted in the providential history through the course of history to be resolved through us. Loving Father, we earnestly wish for this. Father, at this time, we bow before You, so please allow us not to establish any claims centered on ourselves. Grant us the ability to kneel before You with the heart of a child, to hold onto Your merciful hand, and to be embraced in the arms of Your love. Allow us to worship You with a heart that yearns for such grace. By offering everything and laying everything down, lead us so that we leave no conditions for Satan's accusations. Father, we earnestly wish for this. Father! This day is a holy day, a day of blessing that You grant, so please bless the numerous denominations gathering on behalf of the nation, and grant a uniform grace to Your sons and daughters who are entrusted with the lonely altar, so that at this end time, they may all testify to the will of the whole. We ask You to oversee everything, and we pray in Your name. Amen. <Message> The title of the message I will deliver to you today is "Let Us Go Beyond the World of Sacrifice." It was the original human life to live a life of peace. However, there is no peace in the hearts of people today. Also, in the hearts of those who should live centered on freedom and in eternal ideals, there is no freedom or ideals that Heaven can enjoy together. Therefore, all humanity scattered across the world today hopes that at some point, complete freedom, ideals, and peace will be realized. This is the earnest desire of all people living on this earth. Such a world of complete freedom, ideals, and peace is the original hope of humanity, and it must be achieved by you yourselves centered on body and mind. Furthermore, it must be realized in your families centered on your individual selves, in society, in the nation, and in the world. Moreover, Heaven and earth must unite to sing songs of peace, songs of freedom, and to enjoy a world of ideal love. If such a world cannot be achieved, humanity cannot enjoy true joy, true liberation, and true glory. Then why has humanity found itself in such an unhappy fate? It is due to the consequences of the fall. Thus, today, humanity around the world must cross the peaks of conflict and struggle, the peaks of suffering and tears, and you must feel through your actual lives that you are living in a state of unresolved grievances like today. The distance between the world that humanity desires and reality is not only far, but while the heart aims for that world, the body cannot escape reality, so people cannot help but live in suffering. Even if someone claims that by establishing logical and ethical laws, they can help humanity repent and realize the ideal world they desire, it is merely theoretical and logical, and cannot actually realize the ideal world of happiness in the realm of life. The paths of countless prophets and sages prove this. Therefore, for us who are at the end time, there remains a path to walk and peaks to cross. That is the path of sacrifice that can achieve eternal peace, freedom, and ideals. To cross such peaks, a central being must appear that can bring eternal freedom to the heart, can replace the eternal hope of Heaven, and can represent the eternal peace of Heaven. If such a central being does not appear, then eternal peace, freedom, and ideals can never be realized in Heaven and earth. Then how does this six-thousand-year historical process unfold? It is centered around God, Satan, and humanity, establishing certain conditions, which is the peak of sacrifice. Looking back at the providential history of six thousand years, in the Old Testament era, the peak of sacrifice was crossed through all things, and in the New Testament era, it was crossed through the reality of Jesus Christ. So, what will be the basis for crossing the peak of sacrifice in the coming age of the New Covenant? It will be through the saints, that is, through you yourselves. When we see that the overall providential history is centered on sacrifice, we can understand that in the Old Testament era, it was necessary to cross the peak of sacrifice through all things, and in the New Testament era, it was necessary to cross the peak of sacrifice centered on Jesus Christ, the Son of God. However, in the present age of the New Covenant, you yourselves, who can represent the names of the bride and groom, must cross the peak of sacrifice. Until you cross such a peak of sacrifice, true peace, freedom, and an ideal world will not be established on this earth. The original heart of humanity aiming for the homeland. So what is the history of humanity that has traversed six thousand years? The form is large and the scope is wide, but this six-thousand-year providential history is ultimately God's effort to find and establish a true person who can enjoy complete freedom, complete ideals, and complete peace. You should know this well through the principles. Originally, humanity was meant to live in the Garden of Eden, enjoying eternal freedom, ideals, and peace centered on God, but due to the fall of the human ancestors, Adam and Eve, that original world was broken. Although they are the descendants of the fallen Adam and Eve, they have a heart that aims for the original world, so we have come forth toward the world that God desires, and our hope remains as an ideal that we cannot help but pursue and cannot help but act upon. So what is the center that God wishes to establish through His laborious providence? It is the true Adam and Eve who are not related to fallen nature. As you know through the principles, Adam and Eve, who were to become the true parents of humanity, could not become true parents due to the fall, and as a result, they became the ancestors of fallen humanity without any relationship to the original history. Because we have become a fallen lineage due to the fallen Adam and Eve, we must welcome a day when we can break that bloodline and receive the true parents of our nature. If that day does not come to Heaven and earth, in other words, if a central being who can move Heaven and earth does not appear, and if beings who can move together centered on that central being do not appear, then true freedom, peace, and ideals will not be realized on this earth. If that happens, humanity cannot escape the historical process of cosmic destiny and indemnity restoration. If you wish to receive God's love, you must understand that the six-thousand-year providential history has been a history of labor, and you must also recognize that you must walk that path of labor yourself. Furthermore, if the overall providential history is a historical process to cross the peak of sacrifice, you must also cross the practical peak of offering sacrifices, just as in the Old Testament era when sacrifices were offered based on all things. After that, you must cross the peak of the blood that Jesus Christ shed when He came to this earth as a sacrifice. Then, you must place yourselves as conditions and cross the peak of sacrifice. Because of this situation, God cannot come to us in glory. He cannot come to us in peace, freedom, and ideals. Instead, He can only come to us while placing the peak of sacrifice before us. Most believers today do not understand this fact. When Jesus Christ came to this earth, the people of Israel did not believe, and as a result, Jesus lived in a position lower than any of the people or wicked individuals of that time. Jesus hoped that instead of the people of Israel offering all things as sacrifices, they would believe in Him and the entire nation would come to God, but because the people of Israel did not understand the providential will and disbelieved in Jesus, they strayed from the path of providential destiny, and this grievance has reached us today. The peak of sacrifice we must cross with hope. What position must we be in for God to be able to come to us? First, we must strike the material things that represent all things. Therefore, Jesus said that the gospel is preached to the poor. Next, we must be able to strike even our beloved sons and daughters, and ultimately, we must be able to offer our own bodies as sacrifices. This is the peak of sacrifice we must cross. When we cross this peak of sacrifice, Heaven will finally come to us and establish a connection with us, which most believers today do not understand. When God places you on such a path, you must confidently cross that path. The six-thousand-year history is not a simple history; it is a cosmic history of restoration and a personal history of restoration. Therefore, if you do not have an unchanging form to stand in the center of the universe's history and represent Heaven, you cannot be one who has crossed the peaks of history and cannot stand in a position that conforms to the laws of providence. Look at Abraham of old. Abraham was in a position where he had to leave behind all the familiar living environments he had known in Ur of the Chaldeans, the land he loved, according to God's word. In other words, he was in a position to suffer material pain centered on his flesh. However, Abraham did not lose heart. If Abraham had lost heart in such a position, his descendants would not have been able to receive God's blessings and grace. Today, in order for you to welcome the God who has been guiding the history of restoration for six thousand years, you must have the wisdom to take on the conditions of restoration and to cross them. Just as there have been peaks of providential history that Heaven has crossed in the historical process up to now, there are also peaks of providential history that we must cross at the end time. Therefore, you must pave the way for Heaven to move freely and for the Lord to come freely by indemnifying all the conditions of sacrifice from the six thousand years of history in your lives. If you forget this, you cannot become the sons and daughters of God, nor can you be people who stand before God. Abraham was able to cross the peak of four hundred years on behalf of the nation because he walked the arduous path of labor and sacrificial suffering until he entered the land of hope, Canaan, leaving Ur of the Chaldeans. Abraham was able to give up all his possessions, even his wife, and even the son he had received at the age of one hundred, Isaac, as a sacrifice to God. Moreover, standing on the unified standard of faith that could even offer himself, he became the ancestor of faith for humanity. The Bible also records the life of Job, who walked the path of sacrifice. Job was within the blessing rights to receive blessings from God, so he received material blessings and blessings of children from God. However, Satan protested to God, saying, "How can Job receive blessings?" So God allowed Satan to test Job. Thus, Satan first struck all of Job's blessed possessions. Then he struck his children. After that, he struck Job's own body. As a result, all of Job's friends and neighbors mocked and ridiculed him, and even his beloved wife criticized him. You should consider the position of Job, who lost material possessions and beloved children, and was betrayed by friends and criticized by his wife. Job, who was in such a state that he could not endure without scraping his body with a potsherd, did not blame God but quietly meditated, and he was able to empathize with God's heart for the sick beyond his suffering. Because Job was such a person, he was able to regain all that he had lost, including his possessions and children, and received even greater blessings from Heaven. When Jesus Christ also set out on the path of spreading the gospel, He first abandoned all His circumstances. In other words, He left behind the family environment in which He had lived for over thirty years. Next, He abandoned Himself, who was in the position of God's only Son, who could stand as the eternal true parent of humanity. In this way, Jesus did not lose heart on the path of the cross, where He had to abandon His body, His family, His lineage, His nation, and even His hopes. Jesus, looking only at the path that could fulfill the will that God had set before Him and the providence promised to Him, walked the path of Golgotha with hope. God, who establishes principles and governs providence. Abraham was able to receive God's blessings for his descendants because he went out hoping for the land of Canaan while giving up everything. Similarly, Jesus also abandoned all His beloved parents, relatives, nation, and country. Therefore, after a certain period of time, there will be a day when all of that will be restored, and that day is the "day of the Second Coming." Therefore, you must understand that on this day of the Second Coming, the Lord who returns will restore all of this. Many prophets throughout the historical process and Jesus walked this path, so what should we do? First, as those who bear responsibility for history, we must become the symbolic body of God that can represent history. And in this end time, as we seek Heaven, we must do so for the nation, the church, and the whole earth and the world.
116   Let us go beyond the world of offerings. Like Jesus, who walked the path of sacrifice, or like Abraham or Job, we must take responsibility for the entire history and walk the path of indemnity. <Word> The title of the message I would like to share with you briefly is ‘We Must Have the Keys to Heaven.’ I will speak to you with this title at this time. 

The Purpose of Proclaiming Jesus’ Words
Humans on this earth have long hoped for heaven. Throughout the course of history, they have lived in anticipation of the realization of the ideals of heaven in every aspect, whether environmentally or globally, during their time. God has also been working providentially in anticipation of heaven being realized. Therefore, the heaven we must achieve is not only God's hope but also the center of human hope and the center of hope for all creation. We must realize this. However, we find ourselves in a position where we must lament over ourselves, even though we must achieve the eternal ideal and the center of eternal hope, which is heaven. The further we are from heaven, the more we become immersed in the elements of evil that oppose heaven, so even if we admire the ideals of goodness, those ideals cannot relate to us, and even if we admire the nature of love, we cannot relate to that nature. Furthermore, even if we have a strong desire to do good, we cannot relate to heaven. Thus, if heaven is not a world excluding God but a world centered on God, we must inevitably establish a connection with God to achieve heaven. Moreover, if God is working providentially to fulfill the ideal of heaven that can harmonize with all creation, He must also establish a relationship with humanity. However, if the hopeful heaven is far from us and the world we live in is a world of sin, a world of evil, a world of hell, we do not have the ability to establish a relationship with God, even if we desire to do so. Nevertheless, if we hope for heaven to be realized by establishing a relationship with God, the connection between heaven and us is an inseparable bond, not limited to our time but an eternal bond that transcends time and place. From the fact that humans have always felt the ideals and concepts of heaven, we can understand that the eternal heaven, which will be realized centered on God, has already been connected with us. What was the purpose of Jesus Christ coming to this earth and proclaiming the words while shedding tears and walking the path of sorrowful suffering for over 30 years? First, it was to restore the connection between humanity and God, and secondly, it was to introduce heaven to humanity. In this way, when Jesus introduced heaven, He did so through words, intending to introduce heaven through truth. God has given humanity the words to establish the ideal of heaven on this earth, intending to establish an eternal and unchanging connection with humanity through Jesus Christ. He aimed to reveal the true truth through Jesus. Therefore, Jesus came to establish the relationship between God and humanity and brought the truth to testify to humanity about the heaven that God, humanity, and all creation hope for. However, although Jesus proclaimed the truth to restore the connection between God and humanity, the purpose of His proclamation was not fulfilled because the people of Israel, who were to establish that connection with the truth, disbelieved Him. From this, we can see that the true words of truth proclaimed by Jesus were not fully conveyed to humanity. This is because the humans of that time disbelieved Jesus, and as a result, He could only introduce the truth to them through parables, symbols, or hints. Therefore, countless humans living on this earth have sought the hidden gates of truth throughout history, mobilizing much knowledge. Now, as we reach the end of history, the time will come when the spiritual and the true will meet, and many people will stand as true believers in Jesus, and the truth hidden in Jesus’ heart will be fully revealed. So, what path have you, who are seeking heaven, entered? Until now, the systems of external truth and internal truth have been established in different directions, but now is the time when those two truths can unite around one focal point. In this way, God's providence centered on truth has been synchronized with the development of history. 

Three Movements for the Construction of Heaven
So, what will happen when the history of re-creation that humanity has long hoped for is completed? First, a center of truth equipped with a universal connection that can realize the ideal of heaven desired by all creation and humanity will appear. Thus, heaven will be constructed centered around that. If such a center of truth does not appear, the entire ideal of heaven will not be constructed. Then, a movement of truth based on that center of truth will arise, and after the truth is found, what kind of movement will occur along with that truth? A movement of life will manifest. This movement of life will be marked as a history of unity centered on life, indicating a divine power that can realize one heaven, directing all creation toward that world. After the true truth appears, a unified movement of life will occur, and after this unified movement of life, a world of unified love will be established. If this does not happen, the heaven we hope for cannot be constructed. So, what kind of world is the heaven we desire? It is a place where God can take pleasure, where Jesus and the Holy Spirit can take pleasure, and where countless saints can take pleasure. At the same time, it is a place where all creation can harmonize. Therefore, that place is a world that harmonizes around love, a world that harmonizes around life, and a world that harmonizes around truth. You must understand this. For this reason, what was the first movement God initiated through humanity to construct such a heaven? It was the movement of the restoration of truth. It was the movement of the restoration of truth through the word. This movement of the restoration of truth must occur through the word because only through the word can the work of life be accomplished, and only through life can the movement of love be manifested. When Adam and Eve fell, they fell by disbelieving the word. Because they fell by disbelieving the word, they lost the life that is the foundation of the word and the love of God, which is the foundation of life. This is the mistake that Adam and Eve made. Therefore, unless we create an opportunity to universally and completely settle the mistakes made by Adam and Eve at some point, we cannot find the heaven we hope for, the ideal garden we desire. To achieve this, the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit have been working through long ages. Among these three divine persons, the Holy Spirit is working to lead humanity to the truth. Thus, it is written in the Bible, “When the Spirit of truth comes, He will guide you into all truth…” (John 16:13). In this way, the Holy Spirit is working with the mission of truth. What mission does the Son, Jesus, hold? He is working as the master of life. That is why He said, “I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me” (John 14:6). Jesus came to establish this life-giving purpose. So, what is the ultimate thing we must find through the path of seeking life through truth? It is love. We must reach not only the love of the Holy Spirit and the love of Christ but also the love of God. From this perspective, if we symbolically represent the nature of the three divine persons, the Father can be represented by love, the Son by life, and the Holy Spirit by truth. Therefore, when Jesus asked, “Who do you say I am?” Peter answered, “You are the Christ, the Son of the living God” (Matthew 16:16). This answer from Peter speaks to the existential reality of Jesus’ true nature. It symbolizes that Jesus is the anointed one, the living God, and a being that possesses both body and heart. In this way, by saying that Jesus is the Son of the living God, we can see that Peter understood not only Jesus’ inner heart but also the overall inner heart of God, and that he could stand on a standard that could relate to God’s laws. That is why Jesus entrusted the keys to the kingdom of heaven to Peter. If we symbolically represent God, humanity, and all creation, God can be represented by love, humanity by life, and all creation by truth. 

The Substance of Love and Life that Possesses the Key of Truth
So, how should we, who must seek the true truth, proceed? Above all, we must possess the keys of truth that can resonate with Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and the heart of God. If you do not have this key, you cannot be incarnated. You also cannot establish a relationship with the Holy Spirit, who is the spirit of truth. What has been the purpose of believers seeking the true truth until now? It has been to find the keys to heaven. Therefore, you must understand that humanity must first seek the keys of true truth. Today, it seems that there are many truths on this earth, but there is no true truth that can serve as the key to open the door to the truth of heaven. If there is someone who possesses such truth, if someone knows this truth, then naturally, God’s love will be poured into that person. Furthermore, if any one of us remains in a position where God’s truth can pour in God’s life and God’s love, all creation cannot establish a relationship with God apart from that person. Therefore, when a being stands in the center of true truth, true life, and true love that can relate to God, that being becomes the center of hope for all creation and the core existence that God desires, so all creation will not deviate from that central being. 

In this context, if we speak of God’s truth, that person can testify to the life of God that has substance, can manifest the love of God that has substance, and can reveal the truth of God that has substance. In this sense, when Jesus said, “I am the way, the truth, and the life,” He was expressing that God has been working to establish a central being who can fulfill His hope of realizing heaven. Therefore, the one who will be established on this earth by God will first receive God’s truth, life, and love, and then will stand as the substance of love, life, and truth. God has been working through long history to establish a being who has completed the standard of humanity centered on God’s love, truth, and life. If you cannot meet such a central being who appears as a substantial entity representing God, you will have no relationship with the heaven that God is trying to realize. Moreover, you must understand that the heaven that all people on this earth desire and that all creation hopes for cannot be constructed. Today, we live in an era where it seems there are many truths, many lives, and many loves; that is, this seems like that, and that seems like this, making it difficult to discern good from evil in a chaotic time. So, what should we do living in such an era? 

Now is the time for you to reveal yourselves before all creation. Until you reveal it, you cannot recover and grow your true nature. If there are elements of evil in your hearts, now is the time to bear fruit, so you must reveal and remove those elements of evil as they are. Only then will a new foundation emerge from there. And if there are elements of goodness, you must pursue those elements of goodness even more to grow your true nature while establishing a relationship with God. To do so, you must make strenuous efforts. However, the closer we get to the end times, the more we humans tend to want to know many things. That is, we want to know everything on earth, possess everything, and do everything, which is a natural increase in desire due to the development of human knowledge and the elevation of reason and wisdom.
