Regarding the flow of electricity, you may think that the current flows from the positive to the negative, but in fact, it flows from the negative to the positive. 

132 We must possess the keys to the kingdom of heaven. This principle is why all created beings are destined to seek God and establish a connection with Him. Therefore, the severed connection between God and humanity cannot be reestablished from God's side first. Thus, God has taken a position to push us indirectly. Jesus and the Holy Spirit are working, but they cannot come forward and pull us. They are loving us in a way that pushes us, and we must receive that love. This is something that humans do not understand well because it is invisible. 

Now, as the end times draw near, you must not be anxious even if the end is approaching. At that time, even if your life conditions are good and you are in a position of luxury that others envy, you must understand that your mental anguish will increase in inverse proportion. So, what should we do as the end times approach? When the center of the universe appears, you must prepare your heart to welcome Him. In other words, you must be able to hold the Christ, who is the center and the starting point of the universe, in your heart. When you truly hold Christ in your heart, the feelings you experience within Him will become the pillars of eternal life, the foundation of eternal truth, and the base from which you can raise the torch of love. The center of truth is not somewhere else; it is within our hearts. 

Is there anyone among you who desires to have the Lord's heart? If you are prepared to abandon a position you have held for ten years in an instant, and to give up all the efforts you have made throughout your life in a moment, then you will be able to escape the fear of judgment at the end. Our teacher is not elsewhere. Heaven is not elsewhere. Our hearts are the teachers of truth. We must realize that what is closer than Jesus is our own hearts. Even if we have nothing, when we possess the truth that represents the universe and historical tradition and live by that truth, God will dwell in our hearts and rejoice, and we too will find joy. Therefore, we must strive to possess that truth. If we fail to do so, we will not be able to welcome God. 

133 When we approach all things from God's perspective, we enter a realm where we can experience the universal life, truth, and love. If you feel this truth, you will be able to know the ultimate content of truth, the essence of life, and the ideal stimulation of love. And when we accept the gospel that Jesus conveyed, the truth that Jesus taught, and the elements of Jesus' life, and firmly establish them as the unchanging foundation of our hearts, we will be able to repel any cosmic elements of evil that may invade us. If we can do that, then our sighs and pains will not be a problem for us. Even if we still have sighs and pains within ourselves, we will be able to overcome them sufficiently. 

The standard of a heavenly citizen—truth, life, love—nothing on this earth can repel God's life and God's love. The closer we are to the truth, the more immersed we become in it, and that truth will become a center that no one can take away. Even if the earth is in chaos a million times, even if the universe is suddenly destroyed, a person who has firmly established that center in their heart will never change or be shaken. However, if you are not prepared to accept such a center in your heart, no matter how true the truth may appear, you will not recognize it; no matter how true life may manifest, you will not know it; and no matter how true love may appear, you will not be aware of it. 

From this perspective, if today's Christianity seeks true truth, true life, and true love, it must become a religion that completely abandons itself and establishes a center of the heart that cannot be taken away until the end. Until now, the earth has been thought to be expanding with the discovery of new continents, but in reality, it is becoming narrower day by day. In other words, when civilization was not developed, the world felt vast, but as history flows and civilization develops, the world feels increasingly narrow. 

134 We must possess the keys to the kingdom of heaven. The ideal world that will be realized through the history of truth is a universal era where everything establishes a direct relationship with me. Therefore, the standard of heavenly citizens, which must bear fruit in your hearts, namely the life and love of heaven, must be realized within yourselves. Truth, life, and love are like a family; therefore, truth must be accompanied by love and life, and love must also be accompanied by life and truth. The same applies when we consider life. Love and truth must also accompany life. 

Why are truth, life, and love so interconnected? As you know, for an existence to exist, there must be an up and down, front and back, left and right centered around that existence. Anything that exists cannot escape this triad of circles. This is the basic form of existence. While these three points come together to form a unified shape, if the force proceeds in reverse order, a different force will manifest. Therefore, although God is originally the God of love, life, and truth, when fallen humanity cannot form a balanced triangular shape of love, life, and truth, God cannot exercise providence. You must understand this. 

However, by choosing Abraham and uniting the three points into one, that is, by arranging the three points in a straight line, a point was established where God could come. And when Jesus and the Holy Spirit appear in place of love, life, and truth, that point becomes closer to the whole earth. In other words, when remaining in a straight line, the distance is far, but when bending and forming a curve, the distance becomes closer. In this sense, Jesus and the Holy Spirit serve as a bridge connecting God and humanity. 

What is the good news in the movement for the return to heaven? It is the fact that humans, who could not directly encounter God's grace, can now come closer to God’s grace through the coming of Jesus, as the linear relationship between God and humanity has become curved. Jesus has enabled us to have the practical content through which God can operate, allowing humanity to become one with God and become the external manifestation of God. The one who came for this purpose is Jesus. 

135 When we think about this, for humans who must look at the ideal of heaven from a distance, the love of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, who are close in every direction, is undoubtedly the universal gospel. When anyone grasps the most valuable power in the universe, the life force that can connect with the universal power according to the principles of the universe will be bestowed upon that person. Thus, they will be able to feel the touch of love that connects all directions as a hopeful being. Love acts to unite and form a unified body. 

Therefore, until now, we have looked at the Holy Spirit, who has appeared as the God of truth, Jesus, who has appeared as the God of life, and God, who is the God of love, from a distance, but from now on, we must invite them into our hearts. So how can we invite the Holy Spirit, Jesus, and God into our hearts? This is the question. To invite God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit into your hearts, you must abandon your self-centered, selfish stubbornness. You have had many tendencies to cling to your self-centered stubbornness until now. This is your enemy. It is time for you to repent of this. 

Until today, humans have thought that the enemy is outside, but the greatest enemy is within yourselves and your family members. We must walk the path of destiny left to us, so we must establish a connection with heaven through our own center, passing through our environment, nation, and world. We must go this path, whether in life or death, and we are bound to this destiny, even if it takes thousands or millions of years. 

How can we escape from such a destiny? We must fulfill our responsibilities on this earth. And do you still have any elements of evil, envy, or jealousy remaining in you? If you have such things remaining, you will never be able to settle your own sins and escape from that destiny. So, what did Jesus Christ do for over thirty years? He grew up in a carpenter's family and lived a humble life in silence. What kind of struggle did He engage in? Although Jesus helped Joseph in Mary's household and fought for their livelihood, this was not a struggle for mere survival; it was a struggle to perfect Himself in the inner realm. 

From the Gospel of John, we can see that Jesus did not live according to human will but according to God's will. Now, do you have the weapons to fend off the invading enemies of Satan as you seek resurrection? This is an important task for you. However, on your own, you cannot fend off those Satans. You are powerless, which is why you are always in crisis. 

How can you fend off the invasion of enemies now? You can fend them off through Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Jesus and the Holy Spirit not only help you but also hope for your independence. Thus, Jesus and the Holy Spirit desire to connect heaven and earth through you, and they are saddened because humanity today cannot fulfill this. When all things are unified, the entire universe can establish relationships in all directions centered around humanity, and humanity can be liberated as a motive. However, because humanity has failed to do this, a heavenly resentment has filled the universe until now. 

If you feel something, it is the heavenly resentment. And you must fight against sin to resolve that resentment. The time will come when you must abandon everything; that time is the end. How will God's will manifest at that end, and where will God's truth, love, and life appear? That place is the hope of all humanity and the center we must seek. Therefore, if you do not know that place, you must establish and cultivate your heart in preparation. If you are prepared in this way, even if you do not try to go there, you will naturally be able to go there at some point. 

137 Then, how can we discern what is true and what is false? At this time, God cannot teach us what is true or false. After God teaches us something as true, He must then teach us the opposite as false. Therefore, humans must discern for themselves, decide for themselves, and establish for themselves. Thus, you must learn the meaning of the biblical passage where only the five wise virgins, who prepared their lamps, welcomed the Lord among the ten virgins. If you have not yet prepared such a heart, when the center of truth appears on this earth and tells you to abandon everything, you must be able to abandon everything except your true heart. 

When you establish such a center, heaven will come to you. In order to seek the truth, you must not listen to just anyone's words. You must only listen to the words of true truth. So, what are the words of true truth? If there is a word that, when heard by anyone, unknowingly brings forth a heart of repentance, draws them in unknowingly, and cannot be erased even if they try to erase it, that word is the word of truth. That is the word of truth through the principle of heaven. 

When you hear the words of Jesus, you must believe those words as the words of truth representing the heavenly principle and engrave them deeply in your heart. Those words become the words of life for you. However, when you hear those words, sometimes they are accepted as words of life, and at other times, they may seem unbelievable. Therefore, at the end times, you must be able to face the center of universal truth, universal life, and universal love with your original heart. This perfect center was none other than Jesus.

Just as Paul said, we must recognize that being able to become the light of the world is due to the love of God within us. Truth possesses an eternal and unchanging center. You may know much through the words of the Bible, but leaven is a substance that harmonizes and transforms something. If we hold a heart that cannot harmonize with others, we must train our hearts to be able to match with everyone one hundred percent. Until we achieve this purpose, we cannot enjoy complete freedom, nor can we fulfill any other hopes. Therefore, humans must completely resolve their fallen nature and, by offering everything of themselves, equip themselves with the essence of love and goodness that can connect with the universe, and await a time when they can act within the will of God, uniting love and goodness simultaneously. In other words, they are hoping to complete the ideal of love in their lives and become perfected individuals before one truth. Today, humans often wish to govern this vast and great universe, but that is self-destructive. That is why I have long made the motto "Before aspiring to be the master of the universe, complete self-mastery" my guiding principle in life. In truth, this motto is of utmost importance to Christian believers. When there are saints who possess the character capable of governing the universe, that is, when they acquire the subjectivity to govern the universe, only then can the shortcut that God can tread upon be established. When this standard is fulfilled, it can be said that one has the value of original creation. That is why Jesus said, "What will it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses his soul?" You must not forget that today is a historical time when true individuals with such value must emerge. Do not think, "That person is like this, so I can be like that too," but you must be able to set conditions that surpass Jesus. Also, even if you possess the full authority of heaven and earth, you must be able to relinquish it in an instant for the sake of the will. It may seem like it is being thrown away at first glance, but in reality, it is a way to find everything and gain something greater. The enemies that invade us prevent us from realizing the truth and block the path to life and love. However, such enemies are not elsewhere; they are within yourselves. Therefore, even if there are wrongdoings, before blaming others, you must consider that such things happened because of your own mistakes and take responsibility for yourself. Even if you have lamentations within yourself, you must strive to resolve them yourself, and you should have the heart to come forth and resolve not only your family's lamentations but also those of the nation. If there are three million people among thirty million who can feel the difficulties of our country as their own and shed tears, our nation will survive. We must be able to say that the state of our country is my responsibility and that the state of the whole world is my responsibility as well. We must recognize that we are in a position to fulfill God's hope for the entire world to become Christian, with the number of Christians exceeding ten million and even reaching a billion. You must be aware that you are in a position to fulfill such hope of God.

If such shepherds and sheep appear on this earth, a new history of heavenly principles will unfold centered around them. Furthermore, movements of truth, life, and God's love that replace heavenly principles will arise through them. Today, such movements of truth must emerge among our Korean people. If we ourselves step forward with such a mental standard, God will not be indifferent. After living such a life, we must strive to discover our own character and value through others. 
141   We must hold the keys to heaven. Jesus and the Holy Spirit walked such a path on behalf of humanity. Therefore, we must become true saints who live by emulating the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Otherwise, we will bear the fruits of evil, cannot sever our relationship with Satan, cannot complete our character, and God cannot establish you as His true children. Friends, Jesus was a pitiful person. He can be seen as the most unfortunate man on this earth. He came to this earth as the crown prince of heaven but was subjected to all sorts of schemes and slanders by the unbelieving Jews, and eventually, He was crucified by them. Considering this fact, there can be no place where your heart and body can be at ease. If you cannot feel the sorrowful circumstances of Jesus with your heart and body, you cannot claim to believe in Him. If you understand God's sorrowful heart, you will feel that even a million years of tears are insufficient. Moreover, if you feel God's anguish at losing Jesus, you will realize that even a lifetime of tears will not reach God's heart. We are indebted to God in terms of heart. In this situation of being in debt of heart, many shameless people think, "He is my Father, so He will forgive me," despite having made mistakes. God may forgive and accept such people, but on the other hand, He will feel anguish. Therefore, before you seek forgiveness for your mistakes, you must be able to feel ashamed and possess a humble heart. If you empathize with God's painful heart, He will forget His anguish and accept you with tears. You may be seeking the path of heavenly principles and the path of truth with hope, but God is concerned for you. For such you, the gifts of God's love and life will descend. If you have not lived such a life, you must be concerned about that self. Friends, do not blame your brothers and sisters. Do not blame the world and God. If you are to blame, blame yourself. Before blaming others, before blaming God, you must blame yourself. 
142   Such a heart was embodied by Jesus Christ, who, after enduring over thirty years of suffering, carried the cross on Golgotha, yet did not blame God even in that position, but rather had a heart that was concerned with fulfilling His own responsibility to accomplish God's will. That is why God resurrected Jesus. Such a heart is something that cannot be found in the world of Satan, a level of heart that Satan cannot even dream of, and because of this, Jesus became the center of this world. The same goes for you. In your journey of faith, you must be better than anyone in the world of Satan; you cannot be at the same level as them. When comparing your internal heart and character, you must possess a heart and character of such high quality that they cannot dare to follow. Based on that condition, you can enter into the realm of resurrection. Jesus prayed for the nation while on the cross, and not only did He have the heart to fulfill His responsibilities even if it meant dying, but He also transcended death to be concerned with God's will, which is why God was able to resurrect such Jesus. Therefore, Satan could not dare to accuse the resurrected Jesus. If you become a being of such value as Jesus, Satan will not be able to accuse you. 
143   You will become a center of universal truth when you become such a person, and when the center of that truth appears, you will naturally become one with that center of truth. Today, you may be aware of the value of the responsibilities you hold within your individual environment, but you may not be aware of your social, national, or global responsibilities. You may not even realize that you carry a global mission. So why are those who have received missions and responsibilities from heaven unable to unite? It is because they try to approach heavenly principles centered on themselves. 9) Let us untie what is bound
Matthew 18:15-20 God's love operates where there is harmony among each other. In my individual being, God's love operates above the harmony of the heart centered on the body, and around such a self, brothers and comrades harmonize, and furthermore, families and families, nations and nations, and the world and heaven harmonize with each other where God's love operates. If all creation had established a standard of goodness that could enjoy God's love eternally, there would have been no barriers among all these creatures. In the human world, because there was no harmony centered on God's love, individuals could not harmonize their hearts and bodies, and furthermore, neighbors, tribes, and nations could not harmonize, and nations and nations, the world and heaven could not harmonize. The purpose of God's providence of restoration is to establish a being who can harmonize this created world that could not harmonize, and to expand the realm of heavenly love centered on that being, to untie the barriers that have been bound between individuals, families, nations, the world, and heaven. The purpose of the providence of restoration is to establish a being who can harmonize before all creation. As a fruit of the restoration history, or as a standard of love before all creation,

148 Let us untie what is bound. The one who came to untie what is bound between heaven and earth is Jesus. Therefore, all humanity can only untie the original sin caused by the fall, that is, the conditions of the fall, through Jesus. The reason is that humans have bound the conditions of the fall on earth, and they must untie it themselves, but fallen humans cannot untie it by themselves and can only do so through the Messiah. Humans were to unite with Jesus to resolve the grievances of heaven and earth bound by Adam and to return joy to heaven. However, by killing Jesus, his will has remained unfulfilled on earth, and even after his death, Jesus has consistently sought to resolve this situation through each of you for the past 2,000 years. The movement of each of you, who is the hope of Jesus, must not be seen as merely the movement of an individual centered on your own self, but rather as the historical fruit that must resolve the grievances of heaven that have been bound for 6,000 years. You must understand that there are the grievances of the prophets, Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and the infinite lament of God bound before you as individuals, and you must recognize the hope of Jesus, who represented God's grievances over 4,000 years, and the hope of the Holy Spirit that has continued for 2,000 years. Therefore, if my individual self cannot untie all the barriers of lament bound between brothers and brothers, and furthermore, between nations and nations, and between the world and heaven, the historical lament bound to Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and God will not be resolved, and God cannot love or rejoice through me. You must have a firm determination to resolve the historical mission of untangling the circumstances bound in heaven and earth through your life and entire lifetime, and even to conclude it by raising descendants. The one who taught us how to untie the circumstances bound in heaven and earth was Jesus. Jesus knew that he was the being who had to untie God's grievances over 4,000 years and spent a life of earnestness to untie all circumstances bound in heaven and earth. Moreover, Jesus's life was not centered on himself but was entirely devoted to resolving all circumstances bound by Adam. Jesus had the mission to restore even Satan, who fell from his original position at the same time as the fall of humanity, because he understood that Satan had sinned on earth and could not be restored without being returned to the earth. Although humans fell due to their wrongdoings, God is still providentially working to establish them again as children who can receive His love. And the day of judgment is not the day to cast the unbelieving sinners into hell, but the day to restore even the sinners, who are the objects of grievances of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, back to heaven, and this is God's providence and the task left for the new era. You must bear this entire mission together with Jesus, and to do so, you must be able to empathize with the earnest heart of the living Jesus, who bore the grievances of God's 4,000 years, and the earnest heart of Jesus and the Holy Spirit that has continued for 2,000 years after his resurrection. 
6,000 years of history must bear fruit, and if you do not work harder than the efforts of Jesus and the prophets, you will never be able to find your original position that must be established before heaven. This is because God spent 4,000 years searching for one Jesus, and it took 2,000 years to establish one bride, so to find your individual self, you must embody the entire circumstances of God's labor, who has lived in sorrow for 6,000 years. Thus, to find your individual self, you must fight. And in fighting, you must first fight against yourself. Jesus struck himself before Satan could strike him, and by doing so, he was able to strike Satan as well. We must strike ourselves before Satan strikes us and then fight against Satan. To walk this path of trials and sufferings, you need a comrade who can recognize you even if the whole world abandons you. Even when humanity abandoned Jesus at the critical moment of the cross, God and the Holy Spirit were in a position to recognize Jesus, and even when he was in a fate of being abandoned by God, the Holy Spirit was in a position to recognize him. You too will have times when God may not recognize you, so at that time, you need a comrade who can recognize you in the place of the Holy Spirit, and when humanity abandons you, you need a being who can recognize you in the place of God, so you must be able to serve such beings. This is why Jesus said that if two people pray together, the Heavenly Father will accomplish it. Just as God entrusted that mission to Jesus and was at ease, you must also reassure Jesus and the Holy Spirit by taking on their will. For God to be my Father and for Jesus and the Holy Spirit to be my Jesus and Holy Spirit, you must become the main character entrusted with the heavenly mission by taking on their earnest circumstances and be able to reassure them. It is difficult to completely reassure a brother by taking on his burden, let alone take on the burden that God has borne for 6,000 years. However, heaven has longed for such a main character to be established on earth, and Jesus and the Holy Spirit have waited for it, and all creation has hoped for it. Therefore, where these two main characters pray together, God cannot help but be present, and the more such main characters there are, the more that nation will become a nation that receives a great mission from heaven and will become a blessing institution for the entire world in the end. Amen. <Message> The title of the message I want to think about with you is 'The Lord is My Good Shepherd.' I will speak briefly on this title. Due to the fall, humanity has lost the master they should serve. Even all of creation has lost its master. Among the ideologies and assertions of humanity today, there is not a single one that comes from the true master. Because humanity is in such an imperfect state, they are trying to break free from it and seek something perfect, trying to escape from anxiety and find peace. 

Jesus, who came as the center of love, life, and hope, has been lost to humanity due to the fall. The original purpose for which God created humanity was for them to live in the eternal garden of love, centered on eternal life, singing of eternal ideals. However, humanity lost this due to the fall, and thus God has been laboring through a long history to restore this to humanity. 

Moreover, all humans are destined to become the true owners of their hearts by making their bodies follow their hearts, but this does not happen naturally. They must go through the history of various sufferings and struggles, prepared to face death. 

So how should we break through the path of destiny that is universally blocked? This path of destiny is a painful peak that humanity has been unable to cross until now. Before crossing this peak of destiny, humanity cannot find the true master, the protagonist of goodness, love, and ideals. 

The Lord is my good shepherd. Therefore, God, who is such a protagonist, has been carrying out the providence of salvation for 6,000 years, trying to lift fallen humanity to enjoy and live together with the original humanity centered on the ideals of God. We, who have longed for the original ideal garden centered on God, must recognize that we are in a state of inadequacy and incompleteness, and that we are walking the path of struggle to reach the perfect standard. Furthermore, we must be able to see the many Satans and wicked people around us who are blocking us. 

Moreover, we must recognize God's painful heart, who is working internally and externally to lift us from darkness, and by overcoming the forces of evil, we must become those who can resolve the sorrows and grievances of the whole. Otherwise, we will not be able to go through the path of restoration, and without going through the path of restoration, we will not be able to face the Father who comes as the true protagonist at the end. 

God has the responsibility to lead fallen humanity to that one garden where all humans can meet the eternal protagonist. Therefore, God sent Jesus Christ as the center of life and as the center of hope and love to weak and imperfect humans. Not only that, but God has made it possible for us to meet that center of hope not at the end of historical hope, but in our daily lives, breathing new life into us and fulfilling God's hope. 

We must unite before God's grace, which has established the center of hope and life in our lives, and serve the true protagonist, fulfilling God's will. If we do not hold onto Jesus Christ, who is the cosmic protagonist and the center of cosmic life, we will not be able to find hope, nor life, nor ideals. 

To become one with Jesus, who is the center of hope, love, and life, we must connect with the internal and external circumstances through which God has been working and fighting to fulfill His will. Otherwise, we cannot become one with the true protagonist, Jesus, nor can we become one with the Creator God. 

You must think about the path of suffering that Jesus walked to find each one of us, to become the protagonist of life, love, and ideals. Jesus was born into this world in a pitiful state and lived a life of suffering. He faced unspeakable scorn, fought against the forces of evil, and left this world without gaining true companions. Furthermore, even after His death, He has been fighting against Satan, who has tormented humanity for thousands of years. You must understand that Jesus is enduring a sorrowful heart that we cannot even imagine. 

The value of the suffering that Jesus endured is symbolized in the scripture we read, where the shepherd separates the sheep from the goats, indicating that the time of final judgment is coming when God will distinguish all nations, placing the good on the right and the wicked on the left. On that day of judgment, on what basis will He separate them? We must understand that the conditions of judgment will be based on the entirety of Jesus' life from His birth to His death. 

So what should we, who wish to become one with Jesus Christ, do? We must follow the path He walked throughout His life, empathizing with the internal and external feelings He experienced, thinking what He thought, and making His hope our hope. If we do not do this, we cannot become one with Jesus, nor can we call Him our protagonist. 

Moreover, if there is no one who can act on behalf of Jesus, who is the protagonist of all humanity and bears the responsibility of the historical battle against Satan, then God's will to send Him as the Savior of humanity will never be fulfilled. In that case, humanity will not be able to regard God, the Creator, as their parent. Fallen humanity can only meet God through Jesus. 

Also, when we consider ourselves living under the dominion of the fall, if the life path that Jesus could not complete and the historical destiny we must overcome remain with us, we will not be able to regard Jesus as our master, nor can we regard God as our eternal Father. 

The scripture we read speaks of Jesus' hunger, thirst, being a stranger, being naked, being sick, and being imprisoned. And it foretells that when Jesus returns, He will say to those on His right, "You helped me when I was in such difficult circumstances." This message is not just for the disciples who followed Jesus during His lifetime but is a warning for Christians who will face judgment at the end. 

When He says He was hungry and thirsty, it symbolizes the unspeakable sadness He felt. Jesus spoke of being a stranger because He felt an indescribable loneliness, and He spoke of being imprisoned because He suffered unjustly. The life path of Jesus, who foretold that He would face such circumstances at His second coming, was a path of sorrow, sadness, and pain that no one could imagine. You must understand that He lived a life of suffering from birth. 

We must establish a direct relationship with Jesus, who endured such suffering, and we must feel the sorrow and loneliness He experienced. Otherwise, we will be in a position completely unrelated to the one who walked the path of divine life. On earth, Jesus walked a sorrowful, lonely, and painful path for over thirty years, and even after His ascension, He has walked a sorrowful and lonely path for two thousand years. 

However, Jesus did not walk this path for His own sake. He willingly walked the path of suffering to find fallen humanity and restore them before God. Jesus experienced hunger, thirst, sickness, being a stranger, and imprisonment. He felt these difficult circumstances not only externally but also internally. 

Having inherited the will of God, which has been in providence for four thousand years, Jesus felt the depletion of God's life and hope among the people of Israel, who were to fulfill that will. To take responsibility for this, Jesus wandered throughout Israel as a solitary stranger, searching for the Jewish people. Originally, the Jewish people were meant to walk this path. However, because they did not walk this path, Jesus walked among those who would not welcome Him, seeking to find true sons and daughters of God and establish true life and love. 

Moreover, because the people of Israel, who should have been in a position of suffering and imprisonment, had forgotten this fact, Jesus took their place and suffered and was imprisoned. 

We must understand that Jesus, who walked this life and died, has been coming to us with the same heart even after His resurrection and ascension. In other words, Jesus is not enjoying glory with a joyful heart or living freely; even now, He is in extreme hunger and thirst, feeling compassion for the poor humans on this earth and worrying about the saints who are wandering in search of the true path of life, enduring infinite suffering, and being in a position of bondage for the redeemed saints. 

Therefore, even though He is in heaven, He cannot rejoice with God even for a moment. You must understand the position of Jesus, who cannot be at peace until the sorrows of all humanity are resolved. When Jesus shared bread and wine with His twelve beloved disciples, saying, "I will not drink of the fruit of the vine until I drink it anew with you in my Father's kingdom," it signifies that until the sorrows of all humanity are resolved, Jesus cannot be at peace. 

We must understand this situation and ensure that because of us, Jesus does not become even lonelier, suffer more, or be bound. We must empathize with all these circumstances in body and mind, understand Jesus' situation, and fight against Satan on His behalf to alleviate God's concerns. If we cannot become those who can care for humanity on behalf of Jesus, we will not be able to face Jesus when He comes to this earth at the end. 

The sorrowful circumstances of Jesus, who has endured a life of suffering for over thirty years and a long providential path for two thousand years, must not stop with Him. We must take on those sorrowful circumstances and comfort Jesus. If we do not become such people, we cannot approach Jesus, nor can we call Him Lord. Therefore, we must dedicate our entire lives to living in connection with Jesus' circumstances, both in heart and body. You must understand that this is of utmost importance. 

Although Jesus came to this earth as the true master, He has not been fully received as the master by humanity. Although He is working to fulfill God's will, He is in a position where He cannot govern all creation with joy. This is because humanity is still bound in sorrow, pain, and loneliness, and God's will has not yet been fully realized. Jesus cannot govern all creation with joy unless He is in a glorious position by completely fulfilling God's will. 

So how can we welcome the true master of glory and joy? We must first become those who can alleviate the sorrows of the Lord, who is burdened by the history of providence. Otherwise, Jesus cannot govern us. And if Jesus cannot govern us, then God also cannot govern us. 

If we do not receive Jesus' governance completely, we cannot establish a perfect bond of love with Him, and therefore we cannot regard Him as our true protagonist. If there are elements within you that make Christ sorrowful, lonely, and painful, then on the day of His second coming, you will not be able to stand before Christ. 

If you cannot establish a center that can take responsibility for Jesus' sorrows on behalf of history, you will not be able to stand before Jesus, who is carrying out the historical providence as a creature. If Jesus has a desire to govern even one person like you, it must be a cosmic desire, and if He has a purpose, it must also be a cosmic purpose. Furthermore, even if He desires love and glory, it is not just for His own sake but for cosmic love and glory. 

Now, do you have sorrow in your life? Do you feel loneliness and pain? Are you perhaps in bondage? It must not be the case that the cosmic protagonist suffers sorrow, loneliness, or pain because of you. Because we are connected to Jesus, even if it is a small sorrow or pain of one person, it does not end with that one person but extends to Jesus. 

When my sorrow becomes intense, it becomes the sorrow of Jesus, who governs all creation, and if I feel loneliness, it becomes the loneliness of Jesus, the Lord of all.

11) Who Do We Live For?
John 14:1-20 We humans cannot live without forming relationships with others. An individual exists by taking a position where the heart and body relate to each other and care for one another. This caring position develops further to care for families, nations, societies, and ultimately the entire universe, leading to a life of 'caring.' This life of caring, religiously speaking, is a life of caring for God. We must find a standard that can care for ourselves in a flat manner and, furthermore, establish a three-dimensional relationship to find a standard that can care for one center. After that, we must live in a way that can connect with that center on a family, national, global, and cosmic level. Without this central standard of care, we humans cannot attain satisfaction and happiness. We must find that central standard of care, which possesses the overall value that history is responsible for and that the universe aims for, and establish a vital relationship with it. We must connect with the fundamental source of power centered on love, absorbing infinitely and being infinitely absorbed, and become those who can be validated even before all surrounding environments.

Humans, having gone through a long history, must find that eternal and unchanging center to which they can entrust themselves. 164 Who Do We Live For?

The Purpose of God's 6,000 Years of Labor
God has been unfolding inner and outer battles through the course of history, which we cannot even imagine because of humans. In the invisible world, He fights against Satan, and in the visible world, He is engaged in battles through people on the side of good and those on the side of evil. Now, if we have the responsibility to understand God's will while looking toward heaven and to know His inner circumstances, we must bear the history of God's inner and outer battles on behalf of God. If we do not, you must understand that this entire battle will not be victoriously concluded through humans as God desires. 

What must we do to become the heavenly chosen ones who fight on behalf of God's will? First, we must unite around the thought centered on God's hope. What is the purpose for which God has been working and fighting for 6,000 years? It is to elevate us, who are living in the world of sin, to a position of glory like God. You must deeply feel that God has been governing and caring for us, sacrificing numerous prophets and saints to achieve that will. Without this understanding, we cannot know God's circumstances. 

Then, what is the center of the hope that God desires, the overall situation that He wishes to find in humans? It is to elevate all people to a high position on His behalf. For this purpose, God has been laboring until now. The hope of God, who has been governing through a long history while forgetting His own difficulties to save us, who have fallen into sin and are caught in the temptations of Satan, is to find and establish a true individual who can inherit God's will to govern all things with the nature of God. We must feel this heart of God in body and mind. 

Establishing a true individual who can inherit God's will is the center of the overall situation of God's desired will, and all humans are ultimately walking to fulfill this one center. Such an overarching purpose remains with us. Therefore, we must be grateful for this will of God throughout our lives and maintain unwavering loyalty to it.

Let Us Become God's Chosen Ones
In the world, if someone endures all hardships and sacrifices their life for the success of a friend, that friend will consider that person a lifelong benefactor and will never forget their gratitude until death. God has been engaged in inner battles for us, insignificant humans, to bestow the glory of success upon humanity, whether we know it or not. In other words, you must realize that God has gone through all kinds of hardships and worries throughout the course of history to elevate each one of you to a glorious position governing all things on His behalf. 

Thus, you must be connected to the center where God's inner battle becomes your inner battle, and God's outer battle becomes your outer battle. Otherwise, you must remember that you cannot become God's chosen ones. We have repeatedly acted rudely before God, who has been engaged in this cosmic battle. Today, you may be willing to make any sacrifice for yourselves. However, when reflecting on how much you have sacrificed for the countless beings and humans, or for the many spirits in the spiritual realm, you cannot help but realize your own shortcomings. Therefore, we, who have a heavenly relationship, must have the heart to sacrifice ourselves for all things and all people, both internally and externally. 

The one who became the model of sacrifice for humanity is Jesus. You must know that the one whom God sent to this earth as a central being for these ignorant humans was none other than Jesus Christ. Jesus Christ, who represented God's inner circumstances, had His hope centered on God alone. In other words, Jesus sought to embody the heart of God, who has endured much for humanity, and to reflect God's public content, which does not work for His own glory, so that He could bestow love on all things and all people on behalf of God and manifest the authority of the heavenly kingdom. 

Moreover, Jesus did not wish for the joy He could feel, the hope He could have, or the glory He could receive to be solely His own. He desired that His hope and glory be realized and manifested in all fallen humans, and He labored for over 30 years for the fulfillment of that work. Therefore, we must take on the image of Jesus Christ, who appeared as the central figure for the construction of the heavenly kingdom, and accept all of His thoughts as our own. If we cannot move toward eternity by emulating Jesus' love, the hope that God desires will not be connected to us. You must keep this fact in mind. 

If our destiny is to traverse the path of battle as heavenly chosen ones and reach the end of history, we must navigate this path of destiny. However, various adverse conditions will block our way as we do so. There will also be countless invisible works of Satan, and we will encounter opposition from many humans on the ground. Nevertheless, if we are God's chosen people who must fulfill our responsibilities with the autonomy granted by God in this battlefield, we must establish ideological unity externally while also being able to endure and overcome any hardships we encounter, just as God has endured and Jesus Christ has endured. 

We must have the hope that our souls can be filled with joy, dispelling the anxieties that surround our bodies through a moment of joy. We must not stop at the connection of a single day; we must maintain our connections, even if they are for a single hour, forever. We must have the expectation of an unchanging connection, like the unchanging relationship established between God and Jesus, and we must carry that unchanging center as our unchanging goal. To do this, we must possess unwavering patience. 

Let Us Become God's Chosen Ones
Now, before us lies the path of suffering, and this path has become an unavoidable one. Jesus Christ came to this earth and devoted over 30 years to overcoming this path, not even considering death as a problem, and we must emulate that character of endurance. Furthermore, God has faced all kinds of hardships and sorrows over the long span of 6,000 years to find each individual, and even while giving His beloved only Son to the cross, He did not cease His providential work in the battle against enemies. We must emulate God's endurance. 

Also, Jesus Christ, having taken on the will of God, who has endured both internally and externally, was able to qualify as the protagonist of endurance in the face of infinite suffering, which is why He could pioneer this path of purpose even while prepared for the cross. You must understand that if Jesus Christ had become someone who succumbed to suffering on the cross, the path of the cross would not have appeared to us as the way of life. 

Jesus knew that He was the heavenly chosen one who represented 4,000 years of history, and even if it meant losing His life, He was someone who could endure all hardships, even if it meant crossing the path of death. The suffering that Jesus endured was not because God intentionally pushed Him into it. Because Jesus fully understood the heart of God, who had labored and endured for 4,000 years for Himself, He did not seek to escape the hardships of death, even if it meant losing His life. 

The Attitude and Posture of the Heavenly Chosen Ones
In emulating such a Jesus, we, who must become the heavenly chosen ones, must not avoid the many sufferings that come our way but must become people who can endure and overcome those sufferings.
175 In the future, we will face battles that we must fight with a hundred people, and there will also be battles that we must fight on a national level. Furthermore, there will be battles that represent heaven and earth, and as we stand before such battles, the attitude we must have as the soldiers of heaven is to possess the patience to overcome any hardships that may come our way by understanding God's heart, which entrusts this battle to us. If we cannot do this, we cannot stand as God's co-workers who achieve victory through the historical journey of labor. This is something we must keep in mind. Today, you must reflect on whether you have become individuals who can bear the responsibility of the suffering that remains in the universe, just like Jesus. Jesus Christ, standing before God's will, walked the path of suffering due to countless people who opposed God's will. And to ensure that the suffering would not be passed on to future saints, Jesus took that suffering upon Himself. Even though we are at the end of days, and despite the cosmic suffering and cosmic battles blocking your path, just as Jesus Christ, who bore the responsibility of history and the fate of future generations, struggled to overcome the cosmic suffering of His time, you too must bear the cosmic suffering and fight with the conviction that you will not leave this suffering as an inheritance for future generations by clearing away all conditions that Satan can accuse. If you cannot do this, you must understand that you cannot stand before God as His soldiers or as glorious victors. We must be able to endure while also being able to abandon ourselves. Now is a time when we must endure more than ever. We must not have stubbornness or claims centered on ourselves. If we have claims to make, they must be for the purpose of fulfilling the one will that God desires. Therefore, as soldiers of heaven who must lay the foundation for eternal victory, we must learn to abandon ourselves.

176 Let us become soldiers of God. When Jesus came to this earth, He received permission from God to enjoy all glory. However, before God's will was fulfilled, before God blessed Him, and before all humans on this earth were blessed, Jesus could not enjoy glory. Therefore, Jesus, who could not fulfill all His will and is now in the spirit world, has been carrying out the providence of salvation in the spirit world to fulfill the will that He could not complete on earth. In this way, we must understand that Jesus is not one who lives for Himself. Even during His thirty years on earth, and throughout the spiritual life that has continued for two thousand years, He has not lived for Himself or to elevate Himself. Jesus' hope was to bring all of humanity before God and to celebrate the day when all humanity could rejoice. For that purpose, Jesus sacrificed Himself and dedicated His entire life. To qualify as victors at the end of days, we must, just like Jesus Christ, who fought for justice for two thousand years while sacrificing all of Himself, abandon all personal matters and establish the laws of justice so that we can be offered as a sacrifice that God will delight in. Otherwise, you must understand that you cannot stand on this earth with the qualifications of a victor who inherits Jesus' hope. God has been fighting against Satan internally and against evil people externally, but this is not a rude fight, nor is it a fight that goes beyond the law. In other words, God never fights outside the principles of heaven. Jesus Christ also did not fight outside the principles of heaven. Therefore, even when we must engage in cosmic battles at the end of days, we must understand the laws of heaven. Thus, we must become people who can fight centered on this law. You may not know it, but Satan also cannot fight outside the laws of heaven, which means he cannot establish rude laws. Therefore, when we set conditions for restoration and fight against Satan, if humans deviate from God's will, Satan will accuse them. Jesus is not an exception. When we deviate from the law, Satan will accuse us without mercy. For you, who must go through the fight for restoration, if you do not clearly know the laws of heaven, you will not be able to receive the glory of victory as the soldiers representing God and Jesus. The two thousand years of Christian history since Jesus' death prove this. Jesus and the Holy Spirit are spiritually fighting against Satan while establishing the conditions of heavenly law that can communicate God's internal circumstances. However, among the humans on earth, there are no warriors who can represent heaven in this fight against Satan and who can be recognized by God. In other words, there is not a single person who can fight on behalf of heaven and Jesus according to the laws of heaven, which is why Jesus is lamenting. Jesus was able to comfort the heart of the Father in the spiritual world and could entrust the four thousand years of fighting against Satan to Jesus because He and the Holy Spirit understood God's internal heart and circumstances better than anyone else. Thus, while Jesus is responsible for this spiritual fight, the external fight must be taken on by the saints on earth. Therefore, we, who must take responsibility for this fight, must have a shield of victory that can fight according to the laws of heaven, just as God and Jesus were able to establish conditions for victory in their fight against Satan according to heavenly law. Otherwise, neither God nor humans will be able to achieve eternal victory in the fight against Satan. Furthermore, you will not be able to withstand the forces of Satan that have been fighting against God's law in the invisible world for six thousand years. If we cannot withstand this Satan, you must understand that we will ultimately be defeated in the fight against the Satan on earth.

177 Therefore, we must establish the standards by which God fought against Satan and the laws that Jesus and the Holy Spirit established in their fight against Satan. However, if we do not become those who can fight according to the laws of heaven in our fight against Satan, first, God will not be able to recognize us, and furthermore, we will not be able to receive recognition from Satan. It is because He hopes for us to become individuals with a cosmic personality. For six thousand years, God has been working and providing for the search for such individuals. If you understand God's circumstances today, you must equip yourselves with the character that can stand at the forefront of this cosmic battle against Satan. 

We are ministers for the liberation of all people. After acquiring such a character, you must elevate your family members to the position of heavenly lineage in your actual lives, and furthermore, you must position your nation before God's will and, beyond that, establish yourselves as representatives of all humanity and countless saints. Therefore, you must have a firm conviction that you are responsible for fighting to liberate those poor souls and elevate them to the glory of God, dedicating every hour to the Father. Meanwhile, all creation is also longing for the end of the six thousand years of struggle and for the appearance of true children who have received God's glory. You must feel the heart of all creation. Thus, when you fulfill God's glory, you must also involve all creation in that glory. Furthermore, you must realize that there are countless spirits in the spirit world who are sighing and grieving, and by establishing the standards of victory, you must enable them to receive the benefits of having established their own standards of victory. To complete this responsibility, you must endure infinitely. You must have the resolve in your heart that says, "Even if Jesus Christ cannot endure, even if God cannot endure, I will endure." Luke 23:50-56 The day of resurrection is the day that God has hoped for since the day humanity fell until the day Jesus comes. Furthermore, not only the Jewish people but all of humanity and all creation have been eagerly awaiting that one day when they can escape the state of fallenness and be resurrected. In other words, God has longed for the substantial day of resurrection to come to this earth for 4,000 years, and Jesus also wished to welcome that substantial day of resurrection. However, due to the ignorance of the people of Israel, Jesus was crucified and could not fulfill His mission of substantial resurrection. Thus, even after 2,000 years have passed, this substantial day of resurrection remains a hope before all humanity and creation. How many people truly understood the historical fact that the entire responsibility of God's providential history over those 4,000 years and the cosmic mission rested upon Jesus? It was not a hope centered on oneself, but rather the fulfillment of God's historical and cosmic hope that was one's own hope. Did anyone truly grasp the heart of Jesus, who lived for over 30 years with the hope that heaven and earth would sing a song of resurrection before God, never forgetting that hope for even a moment? Jesus, seeing that the people of Israel did not believe in Him, came forth, sacrificing His entire life to give them the glory of resurrection, which is a historical and cosmic hope. Yet, no one knew this fact. If you do not understand how much effort and anguish Jesus put into that one hope of resurrection from the moment He was born until He died on the cross, then the value of His resurrection will have nothing to do with you, and you will not be able to thank Him for the grace of that resurrection. When Jesus looked at ignorant humanity, He knew that they would have to walk a difficult path due to their disbelief. Therefore, Jesus, forgetting all His own hardships, walked the path of difficulty that all people must walk, the path of death, with a sincere heart, hoping to establish a time of resurrection before them so that the difficulties would not extend to future generations. However, all of humanity did not understand this situation at all. Jesus' hope was not to conclude His entire life upon Himself, but to see His desired will bear fruit on a cosmic level. Although humanity did not know this journey of Jesus, the angels in heaven, the spirits of the faithful, and God knew it, and at that time, the only one who understood Jesus' heart was God alone. However, the friends Jesus hoped for were not friends from heaven but human beings on earth. Why then did heaven become His friend instead of humans? The people of Israel should have stood in the position of friends who understood Jesus' heart, but since they did not, heaven had no choice but to take the position of a friend. You must understand this situation and become true people who can represent Jesus' heart on earth, fulfilling His hope of wanting a true friend on this earth.

Through Jesus' resurrection, all creation received the joy of welcoming a new master, humanity was given the path of a new beginning, and Jesus could experience the joy of victory in spiritual struggle. God, who had been slandered by Satan for 4,000 years, was able to taste the joy of being freed from slander, at least outwardly, through Jesus' resurrection. You must understand that there was joy in heaven and earth because of Jesus' resurrection. However, the joy of Jesus' victory over Satan was a joy that should have been experienced while He was alive, not after death. The joy of God resulting from Jesus' resurrection should have been a comprehensive joy of both internal and external victory, not just an external one against Satan. Therefore, the greater joy that God and all humanity should have received due to the death on the cross has remained a subject of longing until today. Thus, you have the mission not only to offer a greater cosmic joy to heaven but also to be able to feel that joy yourself. The joy of Jesus' spiritual resurrection did not become the joy that all creation, humanity, Jesus, and God should eternally possess; rather, it was a joy that contained sadness and was merely a partial joy. Now, you must establish this partial joy as a cosmic joy and transform the joy accompanied by sadness into an eternal joy without sadness on this earth, so that God can rejoice even more through your resurrection than through Jesus' resurrection. Only then can you truly taste God's joy through the joy of Jesus' resurrection. If this is to be your individual hope and duty, you must take Jesus' hope for the world as your own hope and Jesus' duty as your own duty. To do this, you must reflect on the path of effort that Jesus walked until His resurrection before rejoicing in the day of resurrection, and you must think of the path that God has walked for 4,000 years, so that by walking that path yourself, you can fulfill the hope that remains before God and live a life of faith that can return eternal joy to God.

That standard is not knowledge or learning. It is each person's original heart. And now, in this time close to the end, it is a time when anyone could invade and violate my life and my eternal hope. 192   O sleeping world, awaken. Countless ancestors of ours and central figures of providence have labored through a long historical process to find the true heart that can represent heaven, but they have not yet found it. Furthermore, the standards that can correspond to that heart, harmonize with it, and serve as elements of eternal ideals to be enjoyed have not been relatively established. Thus, there are still barriers of darkness obstructing this land. You must understand this. Therefore, you must seek all of this to establish one heart, the center of an unchanging heart, and break through all the barriers of darkness that are blocking you. However, the most serious problem in current religious life is the conceptual contemplation and faith. For example, people usually try to pray by imagining the pain and horror that Jesus felt when he died on the cross for us. But you should not do that. You should pray, but first, you must awaken your true heart and cultivate the attitude of heart that allows you to pray. When that happens, the divinity of the Father, Son, and Holy Spirit can relate to us through the foundation of that heart. If such a relationship is established, our bodies will naturally respond graciously to it. So, if we, who have awakened first today, are to do something for the world that is still asleep in darkness, what should we do? We must first awaken the hearts of all people who are asleep. Do you have a great teacher in your life? Even if you think someone is a great teacher, he may be a temporary teacher, but he cannot stand before the eternal heavenly principles and introduce the divinity of God on behalf of your eternal life. Moreover, he may be a good teacher in some temporal process for an individual, but he cannot be an eternal life guide who leads you to become a human with true life through his own character and nature. In this way, you must realize that the teacher you are currently facing or the standards he teaches do not allow you to establish an eternal relationship with God. Therefore, you must find your true heart, listen to the call of heavenly principles through the ears of your heart, see divinity through the eyes of your heart, and feel the heart of heaven through the sensations of your heart. If you cannot do this, you will have no choice but to repeat the 6,000 years of historical processes that have passed. Until now, we have truly thought that the only precious thing is heaven, but it turns out that our hearts are equally precious. You must realize this and become those who establish a high value standard that can relate to God, and you must be those who seek the core of the heart. If you cannot become such individuals, you cannot stand before heavenly principles. Those of you gathered here may say that you have been living a sincere faith life until today, but if asked, "What do you have to boast about?" few would confidently answer, "I have something to boast about." Even if there is someone among you who has something to boast about before heaven, God wishes for that to be boasted through the true heart. If you think and live with a heart of compassion that can prove eternal ideals on behalf of heavenly principles, you will never go astray. 

Today, those who practice faith often seek comfort from the conceptual world and its counterparts. However, although fallen, humans originally possess a nature that can connect with the eternal nature, and within each heart lies the elements of the ideal of creation. Therefore, humans can shed sin, achieve completion, unite with God, and live a life of infinite joy. This fact is not known to today's believers. What is the purpose of our prayers, or what is the purpose of Buddhists seeking the state of no-self through meditation? It is to awaken the elements that can become the core of the heart. If you establish such a standard and set the center of your heart that sees, hears, and feels before heavenly principles, you will be able to worship God and give glory with Hallelujah. However, among today's people, there is no one who seriously delves into finding their true nature to reach such a state, even though they desire this state. There is no one who is willing to give up everything to awaken such a heart. Today, people know how to give up everything for a certain ideology or thought, but they are unwilling to give up everything for the truth that awakens their more important hearts. Even if there is someone who gives up everything for a certain ideology or thought, if it is not for the purpose of finding the truth that awakens their heart, they cannot establish any value-related relationship with heavenly principles. So, what must you do to wash away the defiled heart inherited from your ancestors through the bloodline of sin for 6,000 years? As Jesus said, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your mind. This is the first commandment," you must stand in a position where you can give your all. In whatever situation you face, in whatever problem you encounter, you must be someone who can risk your life. You must do so in the place where you reside, in all matters centered around your hopes, and even at the crossroads of life and death, you must give your heart and body. If you do not become such individuals, you must understand that you cannot awaken the core of the heart that moves forward with the purpose of giving your all. 

So, how much effort must we make today to awaken such a heart? Throughout the 6,000 years of human history, countless prophets and many loyal subjects, virtuous women, and filial sons and daughters have come and gone. However, no matter how much they devoted themselves, their loyalty, and their devotion, they have not yet been able to awaken the center of the heart that propels us toward the complete realization of the ideal world of creation. This shows that their loyalty, filial piety, and zeal have not brought about the conclusion of the providence of restoration. Therefore, you must become those who can dedicate your sincere heart, strength, and loyalty to establish a standard that surpasses the goodness pursued by the loyal subjects and filial sons and daughters who have worked hard to save humanity until now. Furthermore, if our Korean people are to awaken the world and greet a new morning with a mission, they must dedicate their hearts to God more than any other nation. Also, if you here feel a global sense of mission and responsibility to pioneer a new path of faith, you must live a sincere life that does your utmost more than anyone else in the world to fulfill that mission. 

Can you be more loyal and sincere than the ancestors who have been faithful and dedicated before heaven? This is the question. If we are to become loyal subjects and filial sons and daughters who have never existed in history, giving our all in heart, will, and loyalty, and if such people exist among our Korean people more than any other nation in the world, I can assert that this Korean nation stands closest to heaven on behalf of heavenly principles. Therefore, if you, as a new group, are determined to carry the new torch of faith and take on the overall mission and responsibility, you must lead in heart and sincerity and stand in a higher position of faith than the righteous who have come and gone in history, and you must become more genuine than they were. So, do you have a voice to convey to this society today? Do you have any power to stimulate it? Now, those of you gathered here, have you heard a new word? If so, what is that word? In my view, what you have heard is merely what you have heard with your ears. Have you seen any new facts? That too is merely what you have seen with your eyes. Nevertheless, the fact that you were able to see and hear even partially is because those things were already promised. If you have seen and heard even a little of the facts here, from now on, you must firmly establish the center of your heart that can see, hear, and feel everything anew. If you cannot become such individuals, when heaven calls out, "Arise for the world and all people," at the end, you will not be able to rise. 206   Why must the Lord go and then return? I earnestly hope and wish for this, beloved Father. Now, centered on the gathered sons and daughters, please manifest the grace you have granted us.
