I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. <Message> The title of the message I would like to reflect on with you for a moment is, “Why must the Lord go and then return?” I will speak on this title. 

Jesus, who was rejected by the Jewish people, came to this earth, was crucified, and after His resurrection ascended, thus He is in a providential destiny that requires His return. Among the Israelite people, who have long upheld the will of God’s providence, the chosen Judaism had a mission to fulfill God’s will and establish a foundation for victory. This was God’s desire in choosing them and their own hope as well. 

In order to fulfill this will, God sent Jesus, His only Son, who could believe in Him and carry out the entire mission of realizing the ideal of creation. Therefore, God had to present Jesus as the Lord before humanity to fulfill the blessings He intended through Israel and to conclude the historical providence of God’s salvation. However, why was it that Jesus could not establish the ideal garden where the will of providence could be fulfilled and the glory of God could be sung before leaving this earth? This is undoubtedly a matter that brings us sorrow today. 

The path Jesus took from His coming to His departure was not the same as the life path of humans living on this earth today. He went through a position more difficult than anyone else, a life lonelier than anyone else. Moreover, Jesus was the one who embodied both God’s will and human ideals as a single being within a generation and a time. Yet, there was not a single person on this earth who recognized the value of such Jesus as heaven did. Furthermore, humanity could not welcome Jesus as the center of love who could connect God’s love to all humankind. 

Because of this, Jesus lived an indescribably miserable life. He could not set even one person as a friend to express His sorrow. You must understand today that Jesus lived a life more pitiful than anyone else. The purpose of Jesus coming to fulfill God’s will and for the glory of God should have been a joy for the Israelite people, a joy for the Jewish community and all of humanity. And the only begotten Son of God should have appeared as the protagonist of all humankind. However, why did Jesus live a life of hunger and sorrow? 

Times have changed and history has passed, but you must become people who can feel the sorrow and loneliness that Jesus experienced during His lifetime. If you cannot become sons and daughters who can glorify God by fighting against Satan on behalf of heaven and earth, there will be no way to resolve the grievances of Jesus, which are bound in sorrow and loneliness. 

The hope of Jesus was not to fulfill His own desires but to realize God’s ideal of creation even at the cost of His own sacrifice. Because humanity, established as the center of the created world, had fallen, God had carried out the providence of restoration for 4,000 years, and Jesus appeared, taking responsibility for the mistakes of fallen humanity and making God’s will His own ideology and goal. However, the Israelite people did not know such Jesus. Not only that, but the Jewish people did not realize that Jesus’ incarnation represented the historical hope while simultaneously representing God’s overall will at that time. 

Jesus was a solitary individual who could represent history, reality, and the eternal ideals of God, but the Israelite people and the Jewish community, who upheld God’s will, did not recognize Him as such. Therefore, they not only failed to cooperate with Jesus’ path but openly obstructed and persecuted Him. 

What was the sorrow of Jesus as He looked upon such Israelite people and humanity? It was not merely sorrow over the visible environment of that time. The sorrow of Jesus was the sorrow that represented God’s aching heart, who had carried out the providence of restoration for 4,000 years since Adam’s fall, and the sorrow that represented the struggles of countless prophets and sages who had labored through the long historical process of 4,000 years. We must feel that Jesus was such a being today. 

So, how great was the sorrow of Jesus? Because He bore the sorrow of God for 4,000 years and the sorrow of countless prophets and sages in heaven, the sorrow of Jesus was known by God and the countless saints and angels in heaven. The sorrow of Jesus was not for Himself but for the Israelite people who killed Him, for the Jewish community, and for the global path of providence. 

After understanding the heart of Jesus, the Israelite people and the Jewish leaders should have reflected and repented, but none of them understood the sorrow of Jesus. Thus, the sorrow of Jesus deepened because the Jewish community, which should have welcomed Him as the Messiah, could not embrace Him, who came with the historical heart of grievance and the longing for earthly humanity. Furthermore, the Israelite people and the Jewish community, who were to fulfill God’s will centered on Jesus, forgot the hope of God and stood in a position of betrayal against Him. Therefore, we must understand that Jesus had to live a life shedding endless tears of sorrow on behalf of God’s tears for over 30 years. 

Jesus, filled with hopeful desire, had to endure overwhelming sorrow during His three years of public ministry, fulfilling His mission to introduce the Father’s circumstances and heart, while being driven from the Garden of Gethsemane to the summit of Golgotha, experiencing a miserable and tragic sorrow. You must understand this fact. 

So, what was the reason Jesus earnestly prayed in Gethsemane, “My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; yet not as I will, but as you will” (Matthew 26:39)? It was because He was concerned about who would bear the sorrow of God and the sorrow of countless saints and all humanity, and He knew that if He died on the cross, many saints who followed Him would also have to walk the path of death. Thus, the sorrowful heart of Jesus overflowed, leading Him to make such an appeal before heaven. 

Jesus, who bore the sorrows of God and humanity, and the sorrows of all future generations, went to the cross with a heart full of grief. You should not only view Jesus as the historical Jesus but also become successors of Jesus who can reveal His image in this world, which may again be in a similar situation as that time. Otherwise, the grievances and sorrows of Jesus, which have been bound in history, cannot be resolved. 

Until now, the saints who believe in heaven have been striving to become such successors of Jesus. Furthermore, we must resolve the sorrows that Jesus has endured and the sorrows that will continue for future generations. This current era is the ‘end times’ that everyone speaks of and many prophets have foretold, and it is the ‘time of the Second Coming’ when Jesus, having been rejected by the nation and the community, will return. 

So, what should you do in this time? You must be able to comfort the returning Jesus and become people who are more earnestly concerned about the will of heaven than the Jewish community and the Israelite people during Jesus’ time. 

Saints of the end times, who must bear the historical sorrows of the 4,000 years that Jesus took responsibility for, as well as the 2,000 years of sorrow that have passed since His death, must become those who can inherit the great enterprise of heaven that was severed due to Jesus’ death. As those who face heaven, we cannot live our own lives outside of historical connections. 

We must be those who can bear the sorrows of heaven, the future, and the countless saints and angels, and who can feel the sorrows of humanity as they remain in the fallen realm, looking forward to the day of God’s judgment. We should also be able to say to Jesus, “I understand your sorrow and the reasons for your death,” and become those who can empathize with the heart and circumstances of Jesus, who was anxious to fulfill His mission of atonement for humanity. 

Unless we become such people, we cannot welcome Jesus, the protagonist of history, the universe, and the ideals of the future, nor can we resolve His sorrows. What you must understand today is that Jesus was trapped in the sorrows of 4,000 years and walked the path of death on behalf of all humanity and future generations for over 30 years. 

Therefore, you must walk this historical path, looking up to heaven and crying out, and strive to reach the realm of the ideal of creation by establishing a new standard of faith that can even sacrifice your own life. Otherwise, you will not become beings of eternal value. 

So, what kind of attitude should we have as believers? Just as there was a representative Jewish community that took on the central mission among the chosen Israelite people, there will also be a representative religious group that will undertake the mission of the global Israel centered on Christ today. 

That is, since history unfolds with simultaneity, God cannot help but establish a religion that will bear the mission of the end times and conclude the providential history. As those who have reached the end times, we must seek such a representative religion. If we are to seek such a religion, we must reflect on the historical mistakes made by Judaism during Jesus’ time as a historical lesson. 

They were caught up in excessive authority and prioritized human thoughts, becoming overly entangled in consciousness and regulations, thus living contrary to the laws of heaven. Such things will occur even today, in this end time. 

And what we, who are in the global end times, must understand is that the Lord who is to return will walk the same path that Jesus walked, and will come again to this earth after overcoming the global sorrows. Just as Jesus walked the path of suffering due to the opposition of the Israelite people and the Jewish community, ultimately being driven from the Garden of Gethsemane to the summit of Golgotha, the returning Lord will also pass through the opposition of the global Israel and the Jewish community, overcoming the global Golgotha. 

Today, you must feel God’s sorrow in various aspects. You must feel the sorrow of God as He looked upon the Israelite people and the Jewish community, the sorrow of God as He looked upon history, and the sorrow of God as He worries about the future. Only by becoming such people can the Christ, who is bound in sorrow, come to you. 

Furthermore, you must be able to resolve the historical sorrows of the entire 6,000 years that have passed since Jesus. Otherwise, you will not be able to cross the path of Golgotha with the returning Lord. 

When Jesus appealed to heaven from the Garden of Gethsemane, the three disciples who were unable to hear that voice and were dozing off, and the disciples who laughed and obstructed Mary Magdalene when she poured perfume on Jesus’ feet and wiped them with her hair, confirming the glory of the resurrected Lord, did not realize that such feelings of Jesus became His grievances until today. 

Jesus Christ walked a lonely path that no one acknowledged, feeling the sorrowful heart. However, only Mary Magdalene was able to comfort and care for Jesus, empathizing with His divine inner feelings that represented the past, present, and future, and thus Jesus blessed her and was able to place her before God’s will. 

What kind of heart should we, who are in the end times, have? Just as Mary Magdalene went to the tomb with a heart full of sorrow to find Jesus’ body, forgetting her own position, prestige, and face, we must have an even more earnest and sorrowful heart than Mary Magdalene. If we do not become such people, even if we seek the Lord, we will never be able to welcome Him. 

Therefore, to meet the Lord and embrace Him in the fullness of His love, singing the glory of God in the garden of love, you must possess a heart that can comfort the sorrowful heart of God over the 6,000 years and the heart of Jesus Christ, as well as the hearts of countless saints in the spirit world. Although Jesus came to this earth with the love of heaven and the connections of heavenly relationships, He experienced an unprecedented sorrow and loneliness in the historical course. Today, you must at least recognize and comfort that heart of Jesus. If there is someone who feels such a heart of Jesus and lives in unity with His circumstances, that person can connect with Jesus’s heart with a single phrase: “Oh! Lord!” or “Father!” However, until now, there has been no such person. Therefore, you must become that person. To do so, you must transcend history and environment to empathize with Jesus's lonely heart. The Lord is a lonely person, the protagonist of sorrow, and the prince of sorrow. He was an incomparably pitiful being. You must understand that there is no one more pitiful and lonely than Jesus, no matter how pitiful or lonely anyone else on this earth may be. God has been saddened by the fact that there is no one who can grieve on behalf of Jesus or feel His sorrow, and He has been even more saddened by the lack of someone who truly believes in Him. Therefore, you must keep in mind that we have the mission to empathize with the heart of Jesus, who came to fulfill His purpose but could not achieve it, and to take on the heart of God. You must also be able to sympathize with the pitiful Jesus by reflecting on the image of Jesus who worked hard to fulfill God's will. Until now, we thought that after Jesus ascended, He was only at the right hand of God in glory, but in reality, because He could not fulfill His purpose on earth, He is in the spirit world as a redeemer bearing the sins of all humanity, praying for us. We must believe in, follow, and welcome such a Jesus in our daily lives. Therefore, you must live in a way that can replace the pitiful Jesus, who experienced global sorrow and loneliness, and you must become those who can live together with Jesus. Now is the time to reflect and discern whether you have become such a person. Then, how should we, who are to inherit the eternal will that Jesus sought to establish on this earth and achieve God's ideal of creation, proceed? What are the essential conditions required? A community, apostles, and families that can welcome the Lord, who comes to conclude the 6,000 years of history stained with disbelief and sin, must emerge. Therefore, if we are to fulfill God's will today, we must establish a new standard for a community that can replace historical faith in today's reality, transcending past community ties, and we must create standards for apostles and families that can carry out future evangelical missions, thereby establishing a foundation for eternal victory and fulfilling God's ideal garden. When Jesus came for humanity and the world, He was betrayed by the world, nations, communities, and even the chosen disciples, but you must become friends of Jesus today and comfort His circumstances. Jesus, who grieved over the betrayal of the world, community, and tribe, should have had parents who could empathize with His heart, but He did not. As it is written in the scripture that was read earlier, when someone told Jesus, “Your mother and your brothers are here,” He replied, “Who is my mother, and who are my brothers? Whoever does the will of my Father in heaven is my brother and sister and mother.” Through this statement, we can see that Jesus did not have parents and siblings who could truly comfort Him. Jesus was in a sad, lonely, and pitiful position because He had no true parents and true siblings, and He was forsaken by His own tribe. He even experienced betrayal from John the Baptist, who was supposed to prepare the way for Him, leading Jesus to harbor an indescribable resentment. You must empathize with such feelings of Jesus, understand His circumstances, and inherit all of His ideals. Although Jesus's family and tribe were astonished by the miracles and signs that occurred at His birth, they could not recognize Him as the Messiah due to their ignorance of God's providence. They should have realized Jesus's mission as the Messiah and prepared the way for Him, becoming the foundation for fulfilling the providential will. If they had done so, Jesus would not have needed to seek out apostles later. Jesus, who was established through over 60 generations from Adam to Joseph, could have had His family and tribe form a lineage that would fight against the disbelief of communities, nations, and the world. If that had happened, Jesus would never have found Himself in a sorrowful position. 

The Family Environment the Lord Will Seek Upon His Return
So, what will Jesus seek when He returns to this earth? Since Jesus lost the familial environment to fight against the world of Satan, when He returns, He will first seek a familial foundation that can protect Him from His sorrow and pain. Therefore, you must unite your heart with Jesus and fulfill the role of such a familial fence. This is because the lack of such a familial fence has become the source of Jesus's resentment. If there had been true children of God who could have taken on the heart of Jesus and said, “Jesus is truly my Lord,” then His resentment would not have arisen. Therefore, you must become those who can serve as the familial fence for the returning Lord. If there had been brothers who could comfort Jesus's sorrow, then through those brothers, Jesus's resentment could have been resolved. Moreover, if the Jewish people had centered around Jesus's tribe and become His disciples and collaborators, the gospel of Jesus would have spread beyond Judaism to the world at that time. If that had happened, the gospel of Jesus would not have needed to be spread from the Gentiles. However, Jesus did not have such tribes and nations. 

When the sorrowful Lord returns, how should we respond? When the Lord returns to fulfill God's will, we must become the familial and tribal foundation for Him, regardless of the difficulties we face, even risking our lives. This is the mission of the saints at the end of time. Unfortunately, today’s saints do not realize this. Now you must be able to pray, “Heaven, please entrust me with the resentment of 6,000 years. Please entrust me with the sorrow of Jesus. Please entrust me with the sorrow in heaven!” The heavens are still seeking someone who can empathize with the historical sorrow of God and the lonely heart and circumstances of Jesus, and you must understand that they have longed for such a person yesterday, the day before yesterday, a year ago, a thousand years ago, and even two thousand years ago. Therefore, you must be able to possess the parental heart and stand in the position of a parent, just as Jesus did not blame the disbelieving nation that led Him to walk the path of sacrifice through the Garden of Gethsemane and the path of death on Golgotha. You must also feel the position of the bride and groom, as well as the position of the heavenly family and heavenly tribe. When that happens, Jesus will return to this earth and build a family and tribe centered around you. That time will be the end time. The hopeful family that God has desired since the beginning of creation, the ideal family that He envisioned, has not yet appeared on this earth. Only when a being who can fully empathize with the sorrowful hearts of God and Jesus appears on this earth will the resentment of God and Jesus be resolved. 

So, what is the mission that you, who have gathered here, must undertake? When the Lord came 2,000 years ago, the Jewish law scholars, priests, and the family of John the Baptist disbelieved and led Him to the cross. You must take on the mission of believing in and welcoming Him, moving away from that position. When Jesus was crucified, He was a pitiful and sorrowful being. We, who are at the end of the 6,000 years of history, must be able to empathize with such feelings of Jesus to rightly welcome the returning Lord. What kind of standard of life did Jesus establish to fulfill God's will? Jesus established a standard of life that could abandon everything that was not aligned with His will. Therefore, you must also establish a standard of faith that can forsake your own ideals or desires that do not align with the will, or any conditions of the world. What do you think is the best thing you have today? However, if it is not proven to be good eternally in heaven, it cannot truly be good. Therefore, you must be willing to forsake everything that is not aligned with the will on this earth to possess something of eternal value that will remain in heaven. You must also be able to give up any habits that do not align with heavenly principles, and even if everyone calls you a bad person and rejects you, like Jesus who walked the path of Golgotha alone, you must become sons and daughters who walk the path of God's will with your lives on the line. There may be times when you are rejected while walking the path of the will. You must be prepared for that. This is because this world is a sinful world, and it is a principle that the connection of heavenly relationships cannot begin in a place that aligns with this sinful world. Therefore, you must abandon this sinful world, and that will be the time you are rejected by the world. 

In this way, there is a historical path of tears, a historical path of Golgotha, and a global path of Golgotha in the process of reaching the shortcut that aligns with the heavenly laws and leads to heaven. As we seek that path, even if we are rejected and forsaken by the world, church, and family, we must be able to cherish hope, thinking of it as persecution and ridicule that replaces the 6,000 years of history. Beloved gathered here, do not be sorrowful because of persecution. Even if you cry, do not cry only for yourself. Rather, you must be able to pray before heaven, “I will go forth regardless of any pain to resolve the resentment of Jesus and the global sorrow!” You must also be able to pray, “I will not mind even death in the face of global pity! For this, I will forsake all my desires!” If you cannot discover a new self that can pass through the laws of heavenly relationships over the hills of human relationships, that is, if you cannot embody and act out the heart of God that can replace the glory of resurrection, you cannot return to being a human who has completed God's ideal of creation and has the nature of a true human being. The greater the mission you have received from heaven, the greater the responsibility you must bear in the great fight against the evil world. Beloved gathered here today, you must not try to measure the eternal heavenly principles with the faith concepts you have had until now. Just as the Jewish people, who longed for the Messiah who would appear in place of the eternal heavenly principles, could not accept Jesus when He came as the Messiah, if you establish the standard of eternal ideals based on a Judaic faith and the doctrines centered around the Torah, you will unknowingly fall into the pit of death like the Jewish people. Therefore, you must remember that Jesus said, “Anyone who loves their father or mother more than me is not worthy of me, and anyone who loves their son or daughter more than me is not worthy of me.”
220   Why must you go and return? "He who loves father or mother more than me is not worthy of me..." (Matt 10:37) We must keep this in mind. If Jesus had lived a life only looking after Himself without walking the path to Golgotha after more than 30 years of life, He would not have been able to fulfill God's providence of salvation. So what kind of time is today, the time of judgment at the end? Today's era is like the time when Lot lived in Sodom and Gomorrah. Therefore, you must become people who can entrust everything to heaven and live according to heaven's commands in this end time of history. If not, you will find yourselves in the same situation as Lot's wife, who was swept away in the judgment of Sodom and Gomorrah. Furthermore, you should not take the position of Jewish believers who disbelieved in Jesus or the Jewish people. You must not yield to Satan even for a moment, and you must not forget that even at this moment, a battle for life and death is unfolding. 

True Faith in Welcoming the Lord of the Second Advent
So how can you prevent Satan from attacking from above, below, front, back, left, and right in this battle against Satan? You must stand in the position of parents and siblings who can empathize with Jesus' sorrowful heart, weep together, and comfort one another, and you must become comrades who can share in the overwhelming grace of heaven. When there are difficulties, you should take them as your own, and when there is joy, you should share it with your parents, siblings, and friends. Just as Jesus loved humanity, you must be those who understand your brothers' difficult circumstances well. To forgive greatly is possible only when one fully understands the circumstances of the person. God forgives humanity because He knows their circumstances. Therefore, you must not only understand your brothers' situations but also understand Jesus' circumstances well, creating a heavenly family that loves and cares for one another, forming a tribe that fulfills the world of goodness that Jesus sought to restore on this earth.

221 Today, the chosen saints on earth must unite to form a heavenly family, a heavenly tribe, and a heavenly nation. Just as Jesus represented the nation and 4,000 years of history, if we can appear to represent the world and 6,000 years of history beyond the national dimension, God's judgment will be withdrawn. When such a thing happens and your families, tribes, and the whole become one, the Jesus who has gone will be able to manifest in glory. To achieve this standard today, we have established the Unification Church. And we call each other family. Like this, we are family. We are forming Israel, which is responsible for the heavenly principles, as brothers who are not just brothers and tribes that are not just tribes. We must walk the path of pioneering while empathizing with Jesus' sorrow and go through the journey of fighting against Satan to reach the position of fulfilling God's will. Only then can we joyfully welcome the Jesus who went with sorrow. You must keep this in mind.

Matthew 21:33-46

224   Let us become the people who possess the kingdom of heaven
This hour, we entrust everything solely to you, and we earnestly ask that the Triune God preside over us as we pray in your name. Amen. <Words> The title of the message I would like to share with you is "Let us become the people who possess the kingdom of heaven." I will speak for a moment under this title. You all know better that the world that everyone desires, especially for fallen beings like us, is the kingdom of heaven. This kingdom is not only desired by fallen humans. God also longs for the time when the kingdom of heaven can be realized, where all humanity can enjoy and live in an eternal relationship of love centered on the original ideal of creation. You also know that God has been working through the Triune God until now. 

The Completion of the Ideal of the Kingdom of Heaven and Jesus Christ
The kingdom of heaven that we truly desire today is not only the hope of humanity but also the hope of God. Therefore, the ideology that can achieve this kingdom must be able to transcend the individual and embody universality and worldliness, aligning with the heavenly principles. Thus, unless this kingdom is built on this earth, God's providence of salvation cannot be completed, nor can our faith goals be fulfilled. Therefore, this kingdom must be realized by God, who has the responsibility as the Creator who created humanity, and fallen humans must also take responsibility to find and realize the kingdom, even at the cost of everything. When we think about this, we can see that God has longed for a person who can realize the ideal of this kingdom and boast of it on behalf of humanity through a long historical process, but that person has not yet appeared on this earth. 

Therefore, from the creation until today, the ideal of the kingdom that God has sought to find through humanity does not end as an individual ideal but is an eternal ideal pursued by all created beings, simultaneously becoming an individual ideal and a global and cosmic ideal. You must remember that God has endured for 6,000 years, going through the paths of patience, labor, and suffering, hoping for the time when such an ideal can be established. So how can God and humanity establish a connection? It can be established centered on the ideal of the kingdom of heaven. It is through the standard of the kingdom being built that the ideals of humanity and God's creation can be fulfilled. 

Therefore, after the long history of 4,000 years since Adam, God, who has been providentially working, desired to establish a person at some point who could communicate the internal heart of God and the external ideals. The central being established for this purpose was Jesus Christ. That is why God sent John the Baptist, whom He had chosen before sending Jesus Christ to this earth, to proclaim to the nation of Israel, "Repent! The kingdom of heaven is at hand!" However, through whom can that kingdom be realized? It is not through John the Baptist but through Jesus Christ. Therefore, John the Baptist had the responsibility to unite all of Israel and lead them to Jesus. However, because John the Baptist did not fulfill that responsibility, the ideal of the kingdom he proclaimed became irrelevant to Jesus. Thus, the cry of John the Baptist, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand," did not end as an ideal of the kingdom relevant only to that time but remained as an ideal of the kingdom that would be proclaimed through those who have a John the Baptist-like mission in any era of history after John the Baptist, and thus God's laboring hand has continued. 

And we must not forget that for 2,000 years after Jesus, many prophets have labored to introduce God. John the Baptist cried out, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand," but Jesus Christ, who came to actually introduce and realize that kingdom, ended up dying on the cross. Therefore, until today, the ideal of the kingdom, which is the eternal hope of God and humanity, has not been established on earth and in heaven through humanity. The loss of Jesus by the nation of Israel ultimately resulted in the loss of the protagonist of the kingdom, who could help them overcome the trials that came flatly before them, along with the loss of the ideal of the kingdom that John the Baptist had foretold. Therefore, Jesus must come again to reclaim and complete the lost ideal of the kingdom. 

The Content of the Ideal of the Kingdom Desired by God
The kingdom that God desires is not a kingdom that exists only in the spiritual world. The kingdom that God desires is one that is first established on earth and then in the spiritual world. Since the spiritual world, made up of spirits after human death, and this earthly world cannot be separated, in order for you to embody the ideal of the kingdom with a victorious reality, you must stand before both the heavenly principles and human principles and demonstrate the ideal of the kingdom through your sphere of life. Furthermore, the ideal of the kingdom must become not only a personal ideal but also a family ideal, a social, national, global, and cosmic ideal. This ideal of the kingdom must be able to manifest through you. If not, like the nation of Israel, which did not understand or listen to the words of John the Baptist, who cried out in the wilderness, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand," even if someone appears today to proclaim the ideal of the kingdom, you will not be able to hear those words. Moreover, you will find yourselves in the same position as the nation of Israel, which could not accept the new blessed words of the kingdom of heaven that Jesus Christ proclaimed while being chased from mountain to mountain during his three years of public life to establish the substantial ideal of the kingdom. 

Therefore, I say again, unless you can introduce the ideal of the kingdom through your nature to all people and can proclaim a new ideology like that of John the Baptist through numerous sects, and unless you can draw the ideal of the kingdom into your sphere of life and live according to those words, the kingdom of heaven that you desire and the ideal of the kingdom that God seeks will never be realized.
227 Until today, the heaven that humans know is not the original heaven that God desired to find beyond creation. When we look back at the 2,000 years of the restoration path centered on Jesus, who has worked hard to build the spiritual heaven since Jesus, we see that what Jesus Christ could establish was not heaven but paradise. Therefore, the ideal of heaven that humans who have believed in Jesus have hoped for is also paradise. Thus, you must understand that the ideal of heaven that today’s humans possess is not the original ideal heaven that God and humans can accept simultaneously, but a conditional heaven that is part of the process of building God’s heaven. That is why the noun "paradise" has emerged. Therefore, if you have truly been called as heavenly soldiers to realize the ideal of Jesus' heaven, you should not only keep Jesus Christ as the protagonist of paradise but also open the gates of paradise together with all spirits in the spiritual world and all people living on earth, so that Jesus Christ can also be the protagonist of heaven. The responsibility to establish Jesus as the protagonist of heaven does not lie with God, nor with Jesus himself or the Holy Spirit, but with all humanity on this earth. Unfortunately, humans are unaware of this fact. When we think about this, the path for humans walking the restoration course is a distant and difficult one. No matter what other sad paths humans may take, none will be sadder than this. This is because this path is the way of restoration where we must walk again the path of struggle of the prophets and sages, experiencing their sorrow as our own. Even if the numerous prophets and sages have traversed the rugged mountains and the path of Golgotha, we cannot follow the path that Jesus walked without living a life that surpasses all the difficult paths they walked. The path you are taking today, your life of faith, is not easy. Your life cannot be solely for yourself. The people who are to inherit the kingdom are living for the spirits in paradise, and furthermore, you have the mission to fulfill the kingdom on earth. You may have experienced much sorrow and made many vows for your personal life, but you cannot fulfill even your own will for the sake of your individual life alone. This earth does not allow you to walk your path alone. This is because this earth has become a land ruled by Satan due to human fall. Thus, for 6,000 years, Satan, who has opposed God, has been blocking your path.

The Responsibility of the Saints
In such difficulties, what kind of path must we take? It is the path of overcoming the rugged peaks of Golgotha and liberating this earth ruled by Satan to establish the kingdom. However, to walk this path, humanity, which has longed for this path consistently, must also walk the path of indemnity, just as countless people have walked the historical process of indemnity. Therefore, if we are chosen people, we must have a tremendous resolve. Even if you desire the kingdom that God wishes for and are responsible for working to establish that kingdom with your whole life, if you think like John the Baptist, you will ultimately perish, just as he did after crying out for the ideal of the kingdom for over 30 years but ultimately failed. John the Baptist failed because he centered his hope on his individual self. To avoid repeating his mistakes, your actions must not be limited to serving your individual self. There is a satanic nature that seeks to keep you from walking the ideal path that heaven desires, dominating your daily life and life itself to live only for your own circumstances. You must feel this deeply in your bones. The path of realizing the kingdom is an inevitable path of universal destiny that we must seek, and it is the will of the heavenly principles that remain as the ideal of creation. Therefore, we must not think of this path as merely our own. God has been responsible for historical destiny and has prepared the eternal destiny of the heavenly principles. This is to relate you to the historical efforts of countless prophets and sages who have walked through the internal heart of God, through the hearts of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Thus, your individual cry can resonate with the countless prophets who have come and gone in the past, and Jesus and the Holy Spirit can welcome it, and God, who has labored for 6,000 years, can also lay the foundation for you to win in the confrontation with Satan. Therefore, you, who have been called first in the face of such divine will, must realize the gravity of your responsibility and mission and fulfill your duty. If you do not take responsibility for these matters at this critical time, who will bear the historical sorrow of God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit until now? This sorrowful situation of God must be borne by humans. For this purpose, God has chosen this one nation among many nations of the world. However, we must remember that during Jesus' time, the nation of Israel did not accept Jesus' will and, due to disbelief, began anew centered on Christianity in the Gentile world. Now, a global time of tribulation is approaching us. A time of persecution and opposition is coming upon us. And we are faced with a time when all religions of the world must come to an end. In such times, we must exert all our strength to fulfill the historical mission that this nation has been given. In the future, those who have religions will face fear due to ideological conflicts. Moreover, Satan, who has opposed God for 6,000 years, will make a final desperate attack against you. You must always be aware that there are Satan and evil spirits lurking around you, seeking your life. You cannot fend off their invasion with your own strength. To become victors who represent the past, present, and future in the battle against them, you must understand the reality of Satan, who has dominated history, the reality of Satan who dominates the present, and the intentions of Satan regarding the future. To do this, you must walk the same path that Jesus walked, who went up to the Mount of Olives alone, representing the nation of Israel, praying and establishing the standard of suffering that represents history, reality, and the future while confronting Satan, who obstructs the heavenly will. Each of you has trials ahead on your journey. As those who must become offerings, we have the responsibility to resolve our own grievances on behalf of Christ and also to resolve God's grievances. We have the responsibility to fulfill the purpose for which Jesus Christ came to this earth and to fulfill the wishes of countless prophets. By fulfilling these responsibilities, we can bring joy to them, and when such achievements are revealed before the heavenly Creator God, before all creation on this earth, and even before Satan, we will be able to escape from the long influence of Satan and create an environment where we can respond within the heavenly principles.

The Value of Individuals Who Can Realize the Kingdom
Thus, if we cannot find the kingdom, the foundation of victory where we can rest forever, then neither the God we have believed in nor Jesus, nor the shepherds or angels we follow can escape from the suffering caused by Satan. Those of you who are connected to heaven must know what kind of existence you have been established as before the Father and what kind of historical mission you have. We possess infinite heavenly value that allows us to stand before God. Therefore, you must become victors who can inherit the internal suffering of God, who has labored for 6,000 years, and also inherit the suffering of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, so that you can overcome all historical suffering. God has been seeking such victors for 6,000 years. Therefore, if you do not become such victors, you cannot find and fulfill the ideal of the kingdom that God is trying to reveal. If, on this land of grievances, a certain being can stand in place of heaven and earth and on behalf of humanity to establish the ideal of the kingdom, that being will become a valued existence that can bear the purpose of God's labor and the overall labor of Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and countless prophets and saints. That valuable being will save many ancestors who have betrayed God while looking back and will rescue many people living in the world of sin from sin while simultaneously constructing the eternal kingdom of God. The kingdom that transcends history, the kingdom that God desired to realize by sending Jesus to this earth, and the kingdom that future humans can completely realize on this earth will hope for the emergence of a valuable being. God, Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and countless prophets and saints have labored until now for the emergence of that valuable being. If such a being appears on this earth, God will have the responsibility to protect that being forever. This is the principle. An eternal nation and world must be established on this earth centered on such an individual. Our unfortunate nation, looking back, has nothing. We have nothing to boast about. We possess no value that can be revealed to the world. However, if we pour all our sincerity into serving countless humanity beyond the nation and people, it is not that the kingdom will first be realized in America, England, or any other country; we, as a poor nation, can approach God and find the kingdom as our own before anyone else. If that happens, countless nations seeking the kingdom will not be able to approach God without passing through this nation. Then, what mission and role must we take to realize this kingdom? Throughout the long history, we must strive to ensure that the kingdom, which has been called out, comes to be realized through us, despite the paths of struggle and death we have walked, crying out, “O kingdom, come quickly!” If we realize such a kingdom individually, in other words, if a personal kingdom where the Father can be present is realized, then we must also establish the kingdom in our families, and further expand it to social, national, global, and cosmic kingdoms. You must first feel a sense of responsibility to establish such a kingdom. Throughout the historical process until today, many saints and prophets have come and gone, but God has not been able to properly teach His internal circumstances to humans through them. However, if a person appears on this earth who can fully reveal God's internal circumstances and possesses the keys to the kingdom that can open even the treasure chamber located at the very center of the kingdom, then God will have no choice but to be present on this earth through that person.

The Life of Loyalty and Filial Piety of Jesus Toward God
Now, you who have gathered here, who have set out for the path of tribulation and the path of the cross, regardless of life and death, seeking the internal circumstances of God that have not been spoken for 6,000 long years! Have you truly set out to become God's loyal sons and daughters? Have you set out to become faithful and virtuous people? If you truly set out to be such people, then what have you sought, what have you felt, and what have you presented to God until now? This is the crux of the matter. From this perspective, you must all become successors of Jesus Christ. Even if there was a center on this earth, there has been no center greater than Jesus, and no one has endured more difficult circumstances than Jesus in overcoming challenging environments. Jesus was the one who prayed, “Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they are doing!” while crossing the difficult peak of death because of humanity. This path is unique to Jesus, one that no one else has walked until now. When we think of the path that Jesus walked, it was not a path taken for himself. Furthermore, Jesus did not seek to represent God's will through the biblical perspective of his time, nor did he seek to represent God's will centered on the nation of Israel. Jesus was always preparing to present new claims and new divine will. Thus, he taught humanity the path of personal truth and helped them realize a new understanding of life and death. The path Jesus walked was a sad one personally, but it was a path walked while experiencing the love of God that humanity on earth had never experienced. Additionally, Jesus grieved that the God who created all things could not enjoy glory from the perspective of the Lord of all creation due to the habitual faith attitudes of the Jewish people. Although He personally created humanity and all things and is the Lord of the universe, God is in a position where He cannot command or govern humanity and all creation according to His will. Today, many believers think that God, being omniscient and omnipotent, governs humanity and all creation freely, but that is not the case. So, who will enable this God to receive glory from all creation as the God of original ideals? Because the fall of Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, caused God to be unable to fully govern His creation, it is humanity's responsibility to restore that. Therefore, Jesus stood at the crossroads of eliminating the conditions of Satan that caused humanity to fall, representing all the historical doctrines and thoughts, and to fulfill that responsibility, He abandoned His tribe, His nation, and ultimately even Himself, but due to human disbelief, that will was not realized. Thus, God is sorrowfully unable to restore the position to fully govern His creation. You, who are at the end of days, if you know that Jesus Christ walked the path of struggle for over 30 years to fulfill the kingdom that God desires and idealizes, you must also inherit Jesus' victory and stand before God, being concerned about God's dignity and glory.
234   Let us become the people who occupy the kingdom of heaven. We must become Christians. Even though there are countless people and nations on this earth today, there are no individuals who genuinely care about God's dignity and honor. In such times, if there is a nation that can feel God's inner heart and earnestly appeal to restore His dignity and honor, God will turn His gaze, which He has withdrawn from the world, toward that nation. Just as God was able to see the Jewish community, the Jewish people, and the world through Jesus Christ, today He will establish you, who possess the inner heart of Jesus, to repel the forces of Satan. Jesus, as God's champion, fought against Satan on this earth, knowing that good does not perish even if the nation and the world betray Him, fulfilling His responsibility to establish God's dignity with unwavering faith. Therefore, Jesus took on the task of exposing the sins of Satan that caused the loss of God's honor, and the Holy Spirit also took on this responsibility. Moreover, He sought to build a kingdom where humanity could establish God's dignity and honor. 

Restoration of the Relationship between God (Father) and Humanity (Son) Originally, the relationship between God and humanity was an unchangeable father-son relationship, living and dying together, but due to the fall, humanity has lived for 4,000 years without establishing a father-son relationship with God. Among all, the one who was most saddened by this fact was Jesus. He came to this earth to establish a perfect father-son relationship with God, fulfill God's will, and save humanity. Therefore, Jesus is our human father and ancestor. You must also establish the dignity and honor of Jesus. It is the heavenly principle that all humans must completely establish a father-son relationship with God. However, if one person on this earth does not accomplish this first, humanity will not be able to establish a father-son relationship with God. Now we must meet such a person, accept God as our parent, and feel God's sorrow as our sorrow, the Father's pain as our pain, and the Father's injustice as our injustice. Only then can we establish a father-son relationship with God. 

Until now, even if humanity has earnestly appealed to God with a heart full of sorrow, they could not find Him because humanity, due to the fall, has not established a father-son relationship with God, and the heavenly love connection has not been formed. Therefore, we must understand the causes and contents of humanity falling into such a position and must clearly reveal the truth of Satan to restore our original position. A father-son relationship established by words or merely by reservation is unnecessary. When we dedicate our hearts and strength to fulfill the Father's will, and endure and triumph even in the pain that melts our bones and flesh, we can restore the father-son relationship with God. Thus, for the glory of the Father, we must establish the Father's dignity and honor, and just as Jesus carried the cross and overcame Golgotha for the Father's glory, you must also be able to overcome the global Golgotha path. Otherwise, you will stand in the same position as the archangel who has betrayed God's ideal of the kingdom for 6,000 years. You must understand that God is close to you and cares for each one of you more than anyone else. While the world believes that familial love is the greatest, you must know that God's love is greater, deeper, and more profound than any human love in this world. You must be able to call out "Father" while embraced in the arms of God's love and become true sons and daughters who can say, "I understand the Father's sorrow." If you become such sons and daughters and possess the kingdom where God dwells, that kingdom cannot be taken away by anyone. 

Next, you must be able to take responsibility for God's suffering and resolve it. And you must have the indignation toward God's suffering. 

235   Let us become the people who occupy the kingdom of heaven. Jesus also had the heart to feel the pain that God feels through heaven and earth. Among you, if there is someone who, like Jesus, calls upon the Father to comfort Him even in difficult circumstances, that person will be able to establish the kingdom of heaven, and the path that such people take cannot be blocked by anyone.

If that happens, the ideals of the kingdom of heaven will naturally connect on this earth.

In this way, the visible world exists in a corresponding relationship with the invisible world. In the future, human history will inevitably go through a religious position. If you become such a person and create an environment where you can praise the Creator, then, just as smaller powers are drawn to greater powers, Satan will naturally submit before your universal power. Until now, our nation has been a nation that has fervently believed in religion more than any other nation in the world. Thus, unless you form the kingdom of heaven from your heart and lifestyle, and build the universal kingdom of heaven, the ideal of creation that you and God desire cannot be realized through you, nor can such an ideal of the kingdom of heaven be instilled in the world before humanity through you and this nation.

Amen. <Message> Based on the scripture, “But rejoice inasmuch as you participate in the sufferings of Christ, so that you may be overjoyed when his glory is revealed.” (1 Peter 4:13), I will speak under the title ‘We Who Are Seeking Our Original Homeland, Eden.’ 

The Original Eden Garden
You may know a lot about the Eden Garden, the original garden of creation, through the word. You also know well that before the fall, Adam and Eve lived in that Eden Garden, sharing and discussing with God. However, you also know that because Adam and Eve fell, the Eden Garden, which God hoped to achieve through Adam, was not fully realized. Therefore, the original Eden Garden we must seek now is a world unrelated to the ties of the fall, and that world is both the world of our hopes and the world that God has desired to seek since the creation. God, who desired to see the glory of ideals in the Eden Garden through people, lost that hope when He lost humanity. Thus, for God, that garden remains a garden of hope even to this day. Furthermore, we humans, who have inherited the bloodline of the fall, are also seeking this garden as an eternal hope through the journey of life and history. However, if we humans cannot find this garden, you well know that we cannot relate to the true happiness we should enjoy, the true life we should seek, the true love we should have, and the heavenly ideals we should possess.

243   We Who Are Seeking Our Original Homeland, Eden
Then, what is the purpose of God establishing our individual selves and carrying out the providence of restoration? It is to recreate the Eden Garden centered on you. You must feel this. God does not desire an Eden Garden that only He enjoys, but rather an Eden Garden that He can enjoy through you, and you must understand that He has fought against Satan for six thousand long years. Because we lost this garden of hope due to the fall, we are now on a fateful path to seek that garden of hope again. And that fateful path is a heavenly and humanly destined path that we cannot avoid. You desire that all your actions and movements manifest only through your individual selves, but everything that manifests must connect with the whole. This must also relate to the laws of humanity and the laws of heaven, allowing you to connect with the ideals of the Creator. Today, each of us has the responsibility to return infinite happiness and glory to the Father on behalf of history and the universe, while also having the responsibility to return infinite life and love to the Father. If you do not understand this responsibility, you will have no relation to the original Eden Garden you desire, nor will you be able to relate to God. 

Then, what kind of garden was the original garden, the ideal of creation, that was to be manifested through humanity? That garden was one where God could enjoy it, humanity could enjoy it, and all created beings could enjoy it together. Thus, that garden was a garden of happiness. What is it that people today, without exception, seek? It is happiness. Then, what can that happiness guarantee for us humans? That happiness must guarantee eternal joy and eternal gratitude. 

244 Furthermore, what kind of garden was the original Eden Garden? It was a garden of life. And it was not merely a garden of life that remains within a certain timeframe, but a garden of life that manifests centered on eternity. If that garden of life had been realized on this earth, humans would have been able to have gratitude and eternal joy for the gift of God's life as beings with life. Furthermore, the original Eden Garden was a world where humanity could manifest the light of life from the position of being the masters of all life. In that world, each individual's life could manifest as the substance of eternal hope before God, while also shining as beings of infinite value. Moreover, that original garden was a garden of love and a world of peace, where everyone harmonizes around God's love, creating a world of unity. Therefore, we must realize this original garden and give glory to God through our happiness, our life, and our love. That glory is only received by God with joy when it manifests as a substance of beauty that is better than anyone who has come and gone over the six thousand years of historical providence. Therefore, for all humanity to give such glory to God, we must manifest as such a substance of beauty. 

Then, what kind of beauty is that? It is a beauty that can be expressed through laughter, song, and dance, a beauty that serves as an eternal value to give glory to God. The original Eden Garden was precisely this world of beauty. The original garden we desire to seek, like the world of the substantial world and fallen humanity, is a garden of happiness and a world where we must give praise and thanks to God. Furthermore, that world is a world of hope centered on life, where the values of peace and unity centered on life and love are realized. And that world is one where all human values are combined and manifested as beauty, where each individual praises God's life and eternal love through song, laughter, and dance. Moreover, it is a world where all creation moves and rests in harmony as humans move. God desired to realize this original world of creation through humanity. However, this ideal world of God, the original garden where humanity should live, was blocked and shattered due to the fall of human ancestors. 

So, what kind of world are we, who cannot escape the shackles of the fall, in today? We are in a world of unhappiness, not happiness; a world of sorrow, not joy; a world where we do not live in gratitude but in resentment. Now, you must realize this. If you cannot overcome such an unhappy world, happiness will never come to you. How can you know that you are in an unhappy state? You can know through your heart. Is there not an unbearable sorrow in your heart? This is evidence that Satan is our ancestor. Do you not have feelings of hatred and resentment towards others? This is like Satan placing a barrier over our hearts to prevent us from moving towards the original Eden Garden. 

And what kind of world do humans live in today? It is a world of death without life, a world of despair and darkness. Humans were originally in a position to sing the value of life and were supposed to live in harmony with the eternal ideals of God centered on life. Yet today, humans are living in despair, having lost the hope to stand before God's ideals. When humanity is placed in despair, God also remains in despair, and when humans on earth are captured by Satan, a world of darkness ruled by Satan remains in heaven. If you do not discern these, you will have no relation to the original garden.

Do you have envy and jealousy in your hearts as you seek the ideal garden of heaven? Do you have feelings of conflict and division? If these remain, you will never find the original ideal garden. The Purpose of Jesus' Coming
You must keep in mind that today's world of Satan has formed in a shape that is contrary to the ideal garden. You must establish a connection with heavenly happiness and move towards the original ideal garden. Furthermore, you must establish a connection with heavenly life, love, and glory. Otherwise, even if the original garden comes before you, you must remember that it will have no relation to you. The one who came to bridge these two worlds, the world of Satan and the world of original creation, was none other than Jesus Christ. So, what did Jesus fight for when He came to this earth? Jesus fought not to achieve heavenly happiness, ideals, love, life, and glory, but rather to fight against the evil elements that obstruct these, and you must understand that He took responsibility and worked hard as a vanguard in that battle. 

Moreover, you must understand that Jesus, before seeking His own happiness, attacked the stronghold of Satan, broke its power, and took on the heavenly responsibility to lead the unhappy humanity bound in that world to the world of God's good sovereignty. Therefore, Jesus came to those who were filled with unhappiness and sorrow, giving them a heart of higher happiness from God, and if they had that heart of happiness, He established conditions that could overcome even greater elements of unhappiness. Because such conditions could remain as elements of heavenly happiness, you can establish conditions of happiness by overcoming unhappiness through the process of Jesus, and you can also establish conditions of life, love, and glory within the eternal sovereignty of God. 

So, what has caused many people living on this earth today to be filled with unhappiness, sorrow, and resentment? It is the result of living only for oneself. The essence of the world of Satan is to live for oneself rather than for the nation, country, or world. In other words, the essence of the world of Satan is to center everything around oneself. Thus, fallen humans, whenever they find themselves in an unhappy position, grieve and blame others while centering on themselves. However, when Jesus found Himself in an unhappy position, He did not consider Himself unhappy but instead represented God's heart, worrying about this world and overcoming that unhappy position. If Jesus had any resentment, it was against this evil world. Therefore, you must understand that the direction of human resentment and Jesus' resentment is fundamentally different.
249 Therefore, after passing through a world of sorrow and resentment, we must kick open the door of unhappiness and seek the original garden of happiness. What we must first do is to seek Jesus and divinity. In other words, Jesus mourned on behalf of God, worked on behalf of God's will, and lamented the world of Satan while being in a disadvantaged position. If you truly understand the circumstances of Jesus, you should be able to take responsibility for all of His intentions on behalf of all creation. Only when you can do this will you be able to enter the eternal garden of happiness.

Jesus earnestly prayed, “My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me” (Matthew 26:39), and “My God, my God! Why have you forsaken me?” (Matthew 27:46) in order to save a world doomed to death and to realize God's hope on this earth. He was placed in a position of abandonment despite knowing that God's great blessings would be upon Him, and at the end of His life, which was filled with great hope, He faced the despair of having to bear the cross. However, even in such desperate circumstances, Jesus regarded His suffering and trials not as the result of His own life but as trials and pains endured on behalf of all humanity. Furthermore, Jesus was concerned that God might despair because of Himself.

Moreover, in order to atone for the elements of evil such as jealousy and resentment, Jesus became an infinite sacrificial offering to atone for all elements of Satan that oppose the essential element of love from heaven, praying for His enemies. In other words, although Jesus felt a resentment towards Satan that humans cannot fathom and had a desire to judge the enemies on earth, He forgave them and rose above resentment and judgment.

As the builder of the original Eden, Jesus was determined to liberate the pain and sorrow of humanity, which was caught in sin and suffering, and therefore was able to overcome the mockery of those of us who are seeking our homeland, Eden. He was also able to prevent the conditions of Satan's accusations against all humanity. Furthermore, because Jesus endured everything with a heart of compassion greater than anyone in the world of Satan, and because His heart for heaven and the universe was profound, God resurrected Jesus, who represented His sorrow.

Now, if we are to follow in the footsteps of Jesus and move toward God's original garden of Eden beyond the path of the cross and suffering, we must take responsibility not only for our own unhappy circumstances but also for the world's unhappiness. Therefore, you must become a sacrificial offering, and even if you encounter difficult paths or unhappy environments, you must not become someone who is bound by sorrow or the hindrances of Satan. Even if you find yourselves in unfortunate situations, you must maintain a heart of joy, happiness, and gratitude. And this heart of gratitude and joy should not be momentary or individual, but should be everlasting and holistic. In other words, you must adopt a sacrificial attitude that seeks to create an environment where you can eternally be grateful and joyful on a global scale.

To make God's garden of happiness a holistic one, you must keep this fact in mind. If there were to appear a being on this earth who could comfort the heart of the Father and bring Him laughter, joy, and happiness, the Father would rejoice. Therefore, even in an environment of despair and sighs, you must be able to manifest the value of heavenly victory, heavenly hope, and the light of heavenly life, and in a world filled with strife and division caused by jealousy and envy, you must become a harbinger of peace and unity centered on God's love. 

And in this land, filled with grievances, lamentations, sighs, hindrances, and tears, you must become those who can sing praises to God's glory with laughter and joy on behalf of all creation. If you cannot become such people, you must understand that you will not be able to escape the world of Satan. Is there anyone among you present who still harbors elements of evil, the nature of Satan that opposes the ideals of the new Eden? When we appear before the Father, we must do so in a joyful manner. God desires us to appear with the utmost joy that no one in history has ever experienced, along with gratitude.

Now is the time for you to stand in the historically highest position where those on the side of Satan cannot dare to follow in your hope, life, love, and glory. Therefore, even if you bear the cross, you must bear the highest cross. And even in the worst position of misfortune, you must go through a path that allows you to proclaim the glory of heaven, so that Satan cannot dare to accuse you. Rather, you should be able to boldly stand before Satan and laugh at his power and all elements of evil on earth. Just as Paul said, “Who shall separate us from the love of God which is in Christ Jesus?” you must be able to laugh at all elements of evil on earth.

You must also be able to represent the past, present, and future of suffering, sing of the original happiness, love, and glory as the original human form, and be a being who can say, “O God! Forget Your 6,000 years of sorrow because of me!” If such a being does not appear, the resentment of Christ's cross will never be resolved on this earth, and all the feelings of sorrow that Christ had when He came to this earth will not be able to be reconciled.

The True Life that Raises the History of Re-creation

So how should you, who are seeking the original Eden, live from now on? You must emulate Jesus. You must find the elements of cosmic and heavenly happiness by following Jesus and become true people who can manifest glory before God, while also introducing God's happiness, love, life, and glory wherever you stay, and educating many people to give thanks to God.

What do we, who are seeking our homeland, Eden, represent? We represent the Word. The fall appeared as a result of disbelief in the Word, and the resurrection of life also appears through the Word. Therefore, you who are seeking the heavenly city, the original garden of Eden, must cherish the Word given by God in the beginning and become people who can introduce heavenly happiness, love, life, and glory through that Word.

Today, while living on this earth, you have often made unhappy people even more unhappy by saying the wrong word, made those in sorrow even more sorrowful, and made those in resentment even more resentful. You have also often driven those in despair deeper into despair and led those in confusion further into confusion. When Jesus was in Gethsemane, fighting against evil and appealing with God's sorrowful heart to fulfill God's will, humans should have appealed with three times more sorrow than Jesus, yet Peter, John, and James did not even try to feel one-third of that sorrow. You gathered here must not become such people. If Jesus labors once, you must labor three times as much, and if a representative of heaven labors once, you must labor three times more than that. If a representative of heaven worries once and suffers once, you must worry three times more and suffer three times more than that. However, at that time, the crowd following Jesus did not even try to labor one-third as much, leading to the destruction of that nation, selling the only begotten Son Jesus, and betraying God. Today, you gathered here, do you truly wish to follow the Unification Church? 

272 Do you wish to become participants in the glory of the Lord? At this time, when history reaches its conclusion, you must shout toward Satan, who has caused 6,000 years of resentment, saying, "How can I allow you to boast of your authority!" and become glorious sons and daughters who can show God the results of having fought and won against Satan alone, bringing forth hope before the entire universe. You must not think, "It will be fine to just let it pass." You must be prepared to face death in your faith life. You may not realize it yourself, but today we stand in a serious position. If we say that the path we are on is true, we must have a serious resolution. This is because the outcome will differ depending on our resolution. When Adam and Eve fell, God had to take responsibility as the Creator and save them, so there was a glimmer of hope. However, in the last days when the Lord of Glory returns, if humanity cannot take responsibility, He cannot carry out the providence of salvation again. Therefore, if we do not complete the providence of salvation, there will be resentment greater than that which remained after the fall of the ancient Adam and Eve. As we face this fearful time, if we can represent God's heart and the will of heaven, receiving recognition from God, we may not know, but if we cannot, we must stand in a humble position. Jesus was humble even though He knew God's will, and those who do not know God's will must be humble. If there are such people, they will fall into the pit of death. The disciples and the multitude who followed Jesus 2,000 years ago did not know Jesus' sorrow when they were joyful. Therefore, today you must pledge not to stand in such a position. You must call upon the Father with such a heart. The Father will respond because He is alive. Also, if you devote yourself to the earth with such a heart, you will be moved to God's side. 

You must now understand that you bear a double and triple responsibility to resolve all the resentment left by Jesus on this earth and to establish Him not as a dead sacrifice but as a glorious living sacrifice to build the paradise on earth. However, why did Jesus die? It was not because He had no attachment to the world. Jesus loved this earth more than anyone else and was a person full of affection. However, He knew that there was a heavenly will that could not be fulfilled without Him, so He moved in a different direction than humanity and ultimately walked the path of the cross. Jesus could not rejoice when they rejoiced, could not walk the same path as them, and could not express His sorrow. Thus, the path Jesus walked was different from the path humanity walked. Now, as we look forward to the final day of glory, what path must we take to stand before heaven and say, "Please set me before all creation!"? In a word, we must pass through the path of death. This is the orthodox path to heaven. You must walk the same path that Jesus walked. Jesus did not walk the path of the cross on Golgotha for just one day. Jesus, looking toward God's will, fought for over 30 years, consistently establishing the standard of the cross. He did not prepare for the death of the cross for just a few days. He lived for over 30 years, responsible for the providential history of 4,000 years, anticipating, "If things go well, it will be like this, and if things go wrong, it will be like that," and never once lived outside the sorrowful heart of Golgotha. You must understand that it was because of this foundation of preparation that Jesus could leave behind His beloved disciples, nation, and denomination, and walk the path of the cross, having resolved to offer Himself as a sacrifice.

273 You must feel the conditions of victory that Jesus established on Golgotha throughout His life. He hoped to hear such voices throughout His three-year or thirty-year life, but when that hope disappeared, what do you think Jesus' heart felt? You must understand this heart of Jesus. What do you think Jesus' heart felt when He saw this? After Jesus died on the cross, He was a pitiful figure. When Jesus resurrected, not a single disciple was guarding the tomb; it was guarded by the Roman soldiers, His enemies! Even today, there are many cases where Christianity fails to guard Jesus' tomb, and enemies like Roman soldiers are guarding it. Is there not a group on this earth that longs for Jesus' tomb? Even if there was no such group back then, there must be many among us today.

Therefore, Jesus appeared to them. The reason Jesus appeared to them was so that they could testify to the apostles about His resurrection. You must reflect on whether you might be standing in the position of the Antichrist. Now is not the time to criticize others or interfere in others' affairs. The problem is yourself. The denomination is not the issue. You must worry about whether you might become Satan in the last days. Those who have been concerned about others have gone through a historical process of losing themselves. 

Do you wish to joyfully welcome the glorious resurrection that the entire universe desires in the new Eden? If so, you must feel the heart of Jesus and shed tears together, taking on responsibility together. Only such people can receive the glorious resurrection. The time is approaching the last days. Therefore, those who have reached a certain level of spiritual standard feel a sense of urgency. Even if they have received grace, they do not rejoice, nor are they satisfied with the experience of injustice. That is why people are trying to leave the church. The results of human fall and the purpose of the restoration providence. Originally, humans did not need to long for welfare. You must clearly understand that the purpose of the restoration providence is to find one person who can remove God's sigh, that is, to block the history of sin that originated from the human ancestors who caused God to sigh for 6,000 years and to eliminate that history of sin, thus removing God's sigh.
