You have reached the position to raise the flag of judgment based on the 6,000 years of history that our ancestors walked through suffering, and you are in the position to inherit the mission of Joshua and Caleb, who called for the Israelite nation to cross the Jordan River. Be strong and courageous. If we say that we will take on such responsibilities and missions, what will God emphasize to us? Just as God told Joshua, who inherited Moses's mission in the wilderness, to "Be strong and courageous," He will emphasize to us, "Be strong and courageous." Now, as we look toward the global Canaan welfare and hope to enter it, we must realize that we are in the wilderness and become like Joshua and Caleb in body and mind. 

So how should Christians today live? They must appeal to heaven for a being like Joshua and Caleb to appear and lead Christianity on this earth. Christians today must clearly realize that it is time for a being like Joshua and Caleb, who can guide and present the direction to move forward in this wilderness age filled with confusion and chaos, to appear. This is not a matter of one's denomination. We must understand this. Revelation 11 prophesies about the two olive trees. What does this signify? It foretells that a being like Joshua and Caleb will appear before the journey of global Canaan restoration begins. Just as Joshua and Caleb appeared to lead the Jewish nation into the land of Canaan in place of Moses, today, people like Joshua and Caleb, carrying the gospel of Jesus Christ, will appear to lead God's people toward global Canaan welfare, a new hope. 

Moreover, just as those who followed Joshua and Caleb into Canaan destroyed the seven nations of Canaan, you have the responsibility to destroy Satan. You must be those heavenly warriors and remember that you have the responsibility to walk that path. And even if a Joshua and Caleb, who assert new words, appear anywhere on this earth, we must be those who open our hearts and listen to those words and can work for heaven. The path that Joshua and Caleb walked was a path of adventure. The path they walked was a difficult pioneering path and a path of battle. Everywhere they went, they had to fulfill the mission of pioneers on a difficult road. Sometimes they had to fight against trials that came personally or environmentally. Just as Pharaoh tried to kill Moses when he attempted to lead the Israelite nation toward Canaan welfare, and many among the Israelites disbelieved and opposed Moses, similar things happened to Joshua and Caleb. God, who knows this well, told Joshua and Caleb, "Be strong and courageous." What does this mean? It means to transcend all human conditions. 

Thus, Jesus also overcame all human conditions through three major temptations. Therefore, you, who are living today, must be strong and courageous on the path that transcends all human conditions. Joshua was placed in the position of Moses, who had to walk the path of victory until the last moment, so God advised him to "consider the individual you face as an enemy, consider the nation you face as an enemy, and consider the land you face as the land of enemies." We must clearly understand this today. If we are in the position of Joshua today, there will be personal enemies everywhere we go. The environment will strike us. Nations and countries will strike us. However, if we, the chosen ones, unite and become the second Joshuas who are prepared to face death and fight to the end, and if we can follow Jesus Christ, prepared to take responsibility for world Christianity, we can overcome any path of battle that unfolds before us. Therefore, God desires us to be strong and courageous.
293 So what should we do about ourselves? First, we must be strong and courageous, and we need to be able to see ourselves clearly. If there are mistakes in our lives, we should be able to criticize ourselves. Also, let us not just think of ourselves as individuals who have lived for 30 or 40 years. We must recognize ourselves as living beings in the present. 

The Meaning and Mission of Human Existence

So what kind of beings are we? We must understand that until today, God has labored for 6,000 years through a global struggle to bring us into existence. We are the result of God's efforts. Therefore, you must not forget the grace of God who raised you. You should also feel that you are a sacrifice that represents God's labor. 

Moreover, we must recognize that there has been a path of suffering, a difficult and arduous struggle, through which God has come to establish us, and that there have been countless sacrifices of blood from our ancestors. Additionally, we should become sons and daughters who can feel God's heart of love that has labored to save us. 

Now, when we pray to God, we should be able to say, “Let us be able to understand the heart of the Father from 6,000 years ago and the heart of the Father today, 6,000 years later. And let us be able to represent the image of the Father.” We should also have a determination to be a sacrifice whether we live or die, and be able to pray, “We have already offered ourselves as sacrifices, so Father, let Your will be done.” 

Throughout thousands of years of history, our ancestors have built altars of blood. Jesus also became a sacrifice on the cross, and for 2,000 years after Jesus, Christian believers have continued to build altars of blood. Therefore, we must realize that we are those who are placed upon such altars. 

From that standpoint, we should be able to call upon the Father, hear the Father's voice, and appeal before the Father on behalf of humanity to save them.

294 Let us be strong and courageous to restore the lost welfare. We should also become children who understand God's sorrow and resentment as He has governed history for 6,000 years and comfort Him. All of these matters are issues that you yourselves must judge and act upon. 

In this position, what should we do now? We must uphold the traditions established by countless ancestors to conclude God's providential history of salvation, and we must feel that there is an enemy, Satan, who seeks to destroy the conditions under which God can operate, and we must become sons and daughters who feel a sense of responsibility to mobilize even the tiniest particles to defeat him. 

If we call upon God from this standpoint, we will realize that God is not just the God who dealt with Moses in the past or only with Israel, but He is the God who is with us today. That God is the Creator of heaven and earth, the God who dealt with our ancestors throughout history, and the God who must deal with me today. In particular, God could not help but be with Jesus when He made the final decision in the Garden of Gethsemane to be offered as one sacrifice. And the spirit of sacrifice of Jesus, who loved all mankind, has been passed down to future generations, leading to the revival of Christianity. 

So what should the believers who believe in the words of truth left by Jesus, who represented 4,000 years of history, do? We must become sons and daughters who possess the image of heavenly warriors who can save humanity trapped in the net of Satan. We must also correctly understand God's will so that we do not repeat the mistakes of the ancient Israelites, who failed to understand God's will and became prey to Satan in the wilderness. 

You must take the determination that Moses had, who devoted himself for 40 years in the wilderness until he could stand before God again, as the root of your faith, and emulate the tenacious and strong character of Moses, who held onto God and appealed for 80 days on behalf of Israel. You must also recognize that you are the second Israel, a chosen people who must fulfill the ideal of the worldwide return to Canaan. 

Therefore, you should think about these things and be able to declare, “Father! Even if the entire struggle of the 6,000 years of providence manifests in my life, I will overcome it.” Furthermore, you must be able to shout toward the satanic lineage that dominates this land, “I am a bomb. I will explode your hearts!” 

From this perspective, we must take the words God spoke to Joshua, “Be strong and courageous,” as our lesson. You know well through the principles that the Israelite nation went through the history of reparation centered around the 12 apostles because they did not understand the meaning of those words. Therefore, if we today cannot fulfill such Joshua-like responsibilities, the Lord, who comes to build the ideal of the Kingdom of Heaven, will have no choice but to walk the path of suffering together with you. 

Hope for God's Welfare

What will happen if you, with a strong and courageous heart, engage in a decisive battle against the enemies, prepared to face death in place of the 6,000 years of providential history? Only then will we finally meet a day when heaven and earth can rejoice, and the resentment that our ancestors have expressed to heaven for thousands of years will be resolved. Furthermore, the joy of the Creator will manifest, and countless saints will enjoy within the eternal and unchanging realm of God's love, and all people on earth will also rejoice. Moreover, God will set you before Satan to boast about you, and your ancestors will also set you before them to boast, and you will be able to boast to each other as brothers. 

Therefore, there must be a being among you who can say to God, “He is Your son, so please love him.” If such a being does not appear on this earth through true truth, then human joy, joy in the spirit world, God's joy, and the joy of heaven and earth cannot be established. You must keep this in mind. 

Then today, we must settle the sins of resentment accumulated over 6,000 years for that day and restore the lost welfare. 

“Sky, please look upon me with joy. Please resolve the resentment against me. Please let me meet a day when You can finally smile for the first time since the creation.” Also, we must become beings who can say, “Ancestors in the spirit world, since heaven is joyful, please respond with us.” Only then can we restore the global welfare of Canaan that has been permitted. Thus, we must become those who can introduce God's love to humanity by casting off the resentment of 6,000 years due to the fall and placing it upon the satanic realm. 

Only by becoming such beings can we replace Jesus Christ in the global welfare of Canaan, can we replace the 70 disciples, can we become the sons and daughters that God desires to find, can we become families that God can rejoice in, can we become nations that God can trust, and can we restore ourselves as a nation that God can trust. From here, the garden of eternal happiness and the ideal welfare will be established. You must understand this clearly. 

Today, this era is the time to conclude the providential history of 6,000 years, so we must make the final decision and advance toward the will. We must not become those who look back. When Sodom and Gomorrah were destroyed, Lot's wife, longing for her old hometown and the friends living nearby, looked back and became a pillar of salt. 

The Israelite nation that left Egypt to follow Moses also, when they faced hardship in the wilderness, longed for the old Egypt and could not enter the welfare of Canaan, collapsing along the way. When they found themselves in the wilderness with no place to stay or food to eat, they complained to Moses, saying, “If we had been in Egypt, we would have eaten bread and sometimes meat…” The ones who complained and reminisced about the past among the Israelites at that time were those who had been wealthy in Egypt and had dominated others. 

Therefore, you must not follow the same path as the Israelite nation today. Taking this as a lesson, what should you look toward at this moment? Is it your house where you live? Is it the friends you associate with? Your house and friends are not what you should be looking toward. If there is a place where you should stay, it should be a wilderness-like desert, and if you have friends, they should be the brothers wandering in the wilderness. 

Thus, as you walk the path to heaven, you must separate everything from individuals to families, societies, nations, and countries, casting aside all worldly things and replacing them with heavenly things. In other words, you must cast off the worldly self and seek the heavenly self, cast off the worldly family and seek the heavenly family, cast off the worldly lineage and seek the heavenly lineage. You must cast off the worldly nation and seek the heavenly nation, and establish the heavenly nation by casting off the worldly country. 

To establish such things, you must advance with a strong and courageous heart, putting forth all your effort and sincerity. A person like that will be able to be grateful even if an individual collapses in the pursuit of finding individuals, and will be able to be grateful even if a nation or country collapses in the pursuit of finding nations and countries. 

Today, we must prepare ourselves with such determination to fight for individuals, families, nations, and the world, and we must cultivate the courage to say to the Satan that dominates this land, “Get away!” 

If there is someone who possesses the determination toward heaven and continues to advance until the end of their life, even if they die, they will resurrect and appear in that welfare to enjoy glory, and if they do not die, they will be able to live in the welfare garden permitted as the second Israel. You must keep this in mind today. 

<Prayer> Loving Father! Please allow those gathered here today to become emotional sons and daughters who can hear the cries of Abel's appeals. We thought the footsteps of the countless prophets and ancestors who have come and gone throughout history were their own, but now we realize that those footsteps are the footsteps we must also walk today. Today, we must be strong and courageous on behalf of the nation, just as Joshua was strong and courageous in the past, and we must be strong and courageous on behalf of the world, and we must be strong and courageous on behalf of the land. 20) Let us be victors for God 
Luke 19:8-44, 22:39-46, 23:44-49 

<Prayer> We acknowledge that Jesus Christ, sent by the Father who has labored for 4,000 years since Adam, came as the embodiment of the Father, bearing tears, sweat, and blood, to fulfill the mission of replacing the Father’s tears, sweat, and blood, and to resolve the Father’s resentment. As we reflect on how Christ walked the path of tears on behalf of heaven, the path of unceasing labor on behalf of all people, and the path of sweating through His public ministry, we sincerely ask You, Father, to allow us to reflect on whether we are in a position to meet such a Christ. 

Please lead us to be able to trace the footsteps of those countless prophets and ancestors who have labored for 4,000 years and to find the reality of Christ who came to us through the altar of blood. 

When Jesus carried the cross and ascended toward Golgotha, He saw the weak women mourning for Him from a distance and said, “Daughters of Jerusalem, do not weep for me, but weep for yourselves and for your children.” Please allow us to feel the earnest heart of Christ at this moment. 

We know that those who do not understand the scene of the cross cannot receive salvation from the cross, and those who cannot feel the heart of Jesus when approaching the cross cannot stand in the place of truth. Therefore, Father, please have compassion on the sons and daughters gathered here at this time. 

June 30, 1957 (Sunday), Former Headquarters Church.
300   Let us become victors for God. Even if we have nothing to offer and nothing to give to our Father, may we engrave in our hearts the lonely figure of Christ in the Garden of Gethsemane, and may we be allowed to fight against the invading enemies and become watchmen of goodness. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this. As we cry out today to this desolate world, echoing the final plea that Jesus made in the Garden of Gethsemane, it is time for us to transcend the global Golgotha. Please guide us not to become sons and daughters who live for ourselves while distancing ourselves from Christ, Father, we earnestly hope and desire this. Now, may you take responsibility for these numerous lives gathered here, guiding them to walk the path of restoration they wish to go with pure hearts, and grant them fiery gifts in this place. Father! Is there anyone among the children gathered here who does not know your will, or who is buried in death and cannot feel your heart? Father, may you manifest yourself with the fire of the Holy Spirit, and may the history of the resurrection of Jesus Christ be revealed, allowing that resurrection to manifest in us at this time, Father, we earnestly hope and desire this. Father! We thank you for calling us among many people. However, we are worried that we may not fulfill the mission you have entrusted to us. Father! May the sons and daughters who are prostrated here take responsibility for the difficulties they face in place of Jesus Christ, and may they also take responsibility for their own sadness when there are sorrowful matters. Even if they must suffer and fall, if it is the will of heaven, may they be allowed to endure and fight on. May not even one of the lives attending here today be led away by Satan, and since we have come this far to find a way to live, please do not abandon us, Father, we earnestly ask. At this time, may the heart of the speaker and the heart of the listener become one, so that our hearts and bodies may move in accordance with your heart. Thus, may we be able to unite with you and be recreated as offerings that you joyfully accept. At this time, there are sons and daughters scattered everywhere, building lonely altars and praying; may you work uniformly in them with your grace, and we ask that Satan may not find an opening. We pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. <Message> The message I would like to share with you today is 'Let us become victors for God.' I will speak on this topic. You are well aware that due to the fall of humanity, God, who created the heavens and the earth, has never had a day of joy and glory with all the created beings throughout the long history up to today. In other words, God has not been able to meet a day of victory that He can rejoice in. However, the reason for not meeting such a day of victory lies not with God, but with the human beings who were created as the protagonists of all creation. Therefore, the day of victory cannot be found solely through God's efforts; it must be sought through the combined efforts of humanity. Otherwise, neither God nor creation can meet the glorious day of victory. God's hope and Jesus So, what is the purpose of the Creator God in creating all things? It is to see all creation, centered around humans who have achieved the purpose of goodness, singing of God's love and giving glory to God, and to have God rejoice in that. However, because God's purpose of creation has not been fulfilled due to the fall of humanity, God has gone through a long history of struggle for 6,000 years to restore it. Thus, God, who has not met a day of cosmic victory since the beginning of creation, is hoping to meet that day through earthly humans. Therefore, if earthly humans do not find that day, they will not only be unable to deal with Satan, who is violating humanity on this earth, but they will also be unable to defeat the forces of Satan that accuse humanity before God in heaven. 
302   Let us become victors for God. Therefore, God has come forth as a shield for each of you, regardless of any effort, sacrifice, or struggle, to establish you as individuals. From this, we can understand what God's hope is. God is establishing each of you to discern the enemy Satan, who caused humanity to fall, and to end the evil history governed by Satan. We must fulfill such a hope of God and become people who can stand confidently before heaven and all creation, giving glory to God for the victory. Only then can the purpose of God's providence, which He has labored for, be realized. Humanity has sought this day of victory through a long historical process but has not yet found it. However, God has sent one person who can find such a day of victory, and that person is Jesus Christ. He was the one who came as the representative who could win the battle against Satan and who understood the inner heart of God, who has been working for the salvation of humanity through a long historical process, as well as the unjust circumstances of all people. Therefore, you must inherit the achievements of the life of Jesus Christ, who stood as a historical representative of creation, fighting bravely against Satan, who stands in the way of fulfilling God's providence and the desires of humanity. If you do not practice the hope that He desired in your daily lives, you must realize that not only the sorrow of Christ but also the sorrow of God and the sorrow of all humanity will again be bound on this earth. Then, what kind of life path should we, who have the responsibility to fight to meet the day when God and humanity can rejoice, walk? Today, this is the most important question. The life of Jesus was not lived for His own sake. He lived a life that quietly fought with the standard of that one day when God's will would be fulfilled, taking full responsibility for all creation, both above in heaven and below on earth. 
303 Jesus did not discriminate between places or between night and day. He did not care about all the visible persecutions of the world, and moreover, He fought with the overall responsibility to defeat Satan, who blocked His path in the invisible realm. Therefore, today we must all take Christ as our vanguard and, following His will, go where He goes and fight where He fights, that is, we must develop the struggle to fulfill the will of God and the desires of humanity while sharing joys and sorrows together. Furthermore, Jesus came to take responsibility for the 4,000 years of history, for nations and the world, and even for countless lives in the spirit world. Thus, He did not fight for His own sake. He did not fight only for nations or only for the world. He fought to fulfill God's will, carrying the mission of heavenly principles that transcends history and the universe within His one body. This struggle has continued through Jesus' more than 30 years of life and has continued even to this day, 2,000 years after His death. Humans may have times of rest, but He has fought tirelessly with the Holy Spirit to find and establish the day of hope that God desires and the day that humanity longs for. It is heartbreaking that He came to this earth to save humanity and died on the cross due to human mistakes, and even after His death, He has borne the sins of humanity, walking the long path of the spiritual Golgotha of the cross for 2,000 years until today. We must reflect on how we have believed in such Jesus until now. The motivation for Jesus to walk the path of suffering So, who is Jesus? He is the only begotten Son of heaven, the prince of heaven, the savior of all people, and the glorious Messiah, who has nothing to do with suffering. It is only natural that God should rejoice in such a Messiah, and all people should have praised and rejoiced in Him. However, because the people of Israel disbelieved and cursed Him, that joy turned into sorrow. Who should bear this responsibility? It is you who know the will who must take on this responsibility. The formation of the global Christian realm today is due to the standard of tears and efforts that Jesus shed for humanity during His more than 30 years of life, and the 2,000 years of sorrow and unresolved history that has continued since His death to save humanity. Now we must follow the path that Jesus walked while shedding tears on this earth and take responsibility for the mistakes of the people of Israel that made Jesus sorrowful, developing the struggle for revenge against Satan. And you must not think that He merely meditated during the period of preparing for His public ministry. For 30 years in the household of Joseph, Jesus shed countless tears in silence. Neither His brothers nor even Joseph and Mary, who should have understood Him best, knew of Jesus' sorrowful circumstances, so He walked a lonely path with a sad heart that He could not share with anyone. Jesus took on the responsibility to end the history of sin over 4,000 years and fought against Satan with a firm belief in His purpose and an unchanging demeanor to resolve God's sorrow and humanity's sorrow. Therefore, if we emulate such a practical life of Jesus, we can set the standard for a victorious life. Why did Jesus walk the path of life that shed such blood tears? It was because Jesus knew that the long history of 4,000 years was a path of tears. Jesus knew that God had come through a history of tears and that many prophets and ancestors who have upheld God's will also walked this path of tears. Therefore, He thought that in order to fulfill God's will, He too must walk such a path of tears, and He understood that His life would have a significant impact on the future. For this reason, Jesus felt the responsibility to atone for all the historical tears shed by God and the prophets and, in order to bring hope to all humanity, voluntarily walked the path of suffering that brought forth blood tears. 
305   The end-time saints must complete the historical path of suffering. Today, in order to establish a day of cosmic hope and victory, we cannot avoid the path of struggle against Satan. Therefore, the greater our mission, the greater our responsibility. Thus, in order to achieve victory on this path of struggle, you must go through a greater valley of tears. Jesus lived without any sin, without any shortcomings, and without any hope beyond being the Son of God, yet He went up to the Garden of Gethsemane alone, without even His disciples, to make a tearful appeal before God. What does this mean? You must feel the heart of Jesus, who walked such a path of blood tears. And today, as you hasten for heavenly victory, you must reflect on whether you are truly prepared to cross the cosmic mountain of tears with Jesus. Since humanity's history has continued with tears after leaving God's embrace due to the fall, we must walk the path of tears to escape from it. This is true not only in the providential path of God but also in the path of a nation or a state. We call those who shed tears for their nation and embrace their people while weeping prophets. A nation does not simply come into being; it is established through the tearful, tumultuous history of victories achieved by such prophets. Similarly, you cannot meet the day of victory without crossing this historical mountain of tears. Just as Jesus shed blood tears while crossing the path of Golgotha for over 30 years, if you are people who have the responsibility to fulfill God's will and to resolve the grievances of Jesus Christ, there must be unspoken blood tears welling up in your hearts. 
306   Let us become victors for God. If there are apostles of heaven who shed tears for their brothers, for the world, and for heaven, tears that cannot be stopped, then a condition for victory is established here. Jesus once looked at Jerusalem and was overwhelmed with sorrow. However, there was no one on this earth who understood that heart of Jesus. Because there was no friend to weep with Him during such sorrow, Jesus had no choice but to die on the cross. Today, we are the descendants of fallen Adam and Eve, and we have the responsibility to resolve the sorrow of fallen Adam. We must also resolve the sorrow of Jesus Christ, who came as the second Adam to settle the sins caused by the fall. The history of the past is a history of resurrection and growth, so we could stand before the will with partial responsibilities, but today, at the time of completion, we cannot fulfill our mission with such partial responsibilities. To fulfill the mission of the time of completion, you must exert yourself a thousand times more than those who have come before you. And you must embrace the painful heart of God, who could not let go of this earth and has been sorrowful, shedding tears more than anyone else, regardless of whether it is cold or hot, day or night, or whatever circumstances you find yourself in. Today, in order for this nation to establish the law of unification, there must be an exchange of tears between those above and those below, ascending to God. If this happens, this nation will not perish even if it is told to perish. Likewise, if we understand God's sorrowful circumstances and the heart of the Father who loves this land, we will never perish. Therefore, we must become those who shed tears. In the end, whether it is tears of sorrow or tears of joy, humans will shed tears. And just as Jesus faced the barrier of darkness before the suffering cross in the Garden of Gethsemane 2,000 years ago, we too must face the end-time barriers of the cross that lie ahead.
307 Moreover, Jesus shed tears on behalf of God in secret, so the apostles who lost Jesus, His people, and all the nations of the world cannot escape the path of tears. Just as there are tears that must be shed for God's will and the world, the people of the end times will inevitably face the mountain of tears they must overcome. At that time, we will stand at a crossroads, asking whether we will weep for heaven or for ourselves. At this moment, Satan targets those who seek to fulfill personal ambitions by blocking the providence of heaven. Therefore, if you shed tears for yourself in a place where you should be shedding historical tears, you become a possession of Satan. Conversely, if you hold onto the will of heaven and shed tears, you become a person on heaven's side. The reason Jesus was able to move heaven and have all creation welcome Him is that the tears He shed were not just for Himself or His people, nor just for the world; they were tears shed with the hope of God's eternal desire. Thus, Jesus' tears were shed for all creation in a place where they resonate with God's hope, the hope of all people, and the hope of all things. Since Jesus lived and died shedding tears, we who must receive Him cannot help but experience the cosmic sorrow that He felt and shed tears, and all creation cannot help but feel sorrow alongside us. Jesus shed tears for His people, the world, and heaven; what about you today? If you wish to stand in front of the will, you must walk the path of tears centered on the individual, the path of tears centered on family, nation, and the world, and then take on the resentment of the heavenly spirits and fulfill your responsibility to shed tears. Do you now wish to stand in the garden of hope that heaven desires? If so, you must not become a victor for God by appealing to heaven with a heart centered on yourself to escape from suffering.

308 If you do so, you will be caught in Satan's net. If you sincerely wish to enter the realm of the heavenly family, you must take responsibility for your family beyond the individual and build an altar of tears in place of Jesus. If you wish to enter the realm of the heavenly tribes, you must shed tears for your tribe in place of Jesus, and if you wish to enter the realm of the nation, you must shed tears for your nation in place of Jesus. You must also stand before God, establishing the face of Jesus, who took responsibility for the earth and heaven, and always be able to worry for God's will. For two thousand years after Jesus' death, how has God led humanity throughout history? He has made humanity shed tears. Therefore, the path of Christians has been a path of tears, and without tears, the providential history could not have unfolded. After Jesus' death, through the apostolic age, the 70 disciples built altars of tears in Rome for a long time, expanding from the individual to the family, and from the family to eventually form the global Christian landscape of today. However, among the history of Christianity, while there have been those who wept for themselves, there have not been many who sincerely shed tears for the world in place of Jesus. Now, as we are in the end times, we must overcome the global Golgotha of tears. Therefore, the time has passed for weeping for the individual, the family, or the nation. God has been working for thousands of years, hoping that we would become saints who shed tears for the world while holding onto God's will. There have been no saints on this earth who have realized this and shed tears for God, so we must take responsibility and shed tears for heaven. Otherwise, Jesus will shed tears once again, and God will also shed tears again. Now, as we stand before God, we must pray, "Let us also become the vanguard of tears, connecting with God as Jesus did while taking responsibility for human history and fighting against Satan!"

309 Looking at the currents of thought in the world, we can see that nationalism has been abolished to allow Christianity to flourish, expanding the global landscape to welcome the protagonist of that sorrow. Now is the time for humanity to welcome Jesus globally. Therefore, today’s humanity must overcome the global hill of Golgotha. In such times, the question arises for you: "Will you weep for heaven, for the earth, or for yourself?" Depending on whom you weep for, the path you take will change. If you wish to unfold God's will for those living in this world of suffering, you must not forget the overall will and become one who weeps and laments centered on your own will. Such a person will naturally be expelled from the path toward the will. We, who follow the will, must not shed tears for our own circumstances, and if there are nations, states, or the world that wish to uphold the will, they too must not weep solely for themselves. We must shed tears only for all humanity. The value of a life that sheds blood, sweat, and tears must reconnect the severed providential will through you. If you cannot find the day of victorious tears that Satan cannot accuse, you cannot find the day of global victory that God desires. Just as Jesus came to this earth and walked the path of blood, sweat, and tears to fulfill the will, you too must walk the path of blood, sweat, and tears to meet the day of cosmic victory. The history of the universe must also walk the path of tears, the path of the cross of suffering, and no individual can succeed without going through the path of blood and sweat. In other words, we all must endure hardships and become victors for God by overcoming suffering and fighting against Satan. How earnestly have you fought for heaven? You may have shed tears and sweat for yourself or your family. However, Jesus did not only shed tears and sweat for His family; He took responsibility and shed tears and sweat for the nation and the world. Now, you too must go beyond yourself, your family, and your nation to shed tears and sweat for the world. This journey of fighting through tears and sweat becomes the first element of victory. Therefore, to achieve victory, you must become sons and daughters who walk the path of tears and sweat while battling hardships. Furthermore, Jesus prayed with tears and sweat in the Garden of Gethsemane, and you must have the same heart as Jesus. A united nation that advances toward one goal while shedding tears and sweat has never failed in history. What kind of beings are the glorious spirits who have entered the heavenly realm in the spirit world? They are those who have followed the path Jesus walked, tirelessly shedding tears and sweat while pioneering the path of battle on this earth. If we understand that we have the responsibility to establish the conditions for victory that fulfill this cosmic will of God, we must shed more tears and sweat than any historical figure who has come and gone on this earth. Do you love your family? If so, you must sweat for your family. If you love your nation, you must sweat for your nation, and if you love the world, you must sweat for the world. We must also build hidden altars that others do not tread upon, following the example of Jesus, who prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, and we must embody the second Jesus who can shed sweat and tears for all humanity. Have you ever risked your life and shed tears in prayer for God's will? Have you spent time praying while sweating? Even if we have walked the path of tears and the road of sweat, we must not forget that before us lies the final path of death, where we shed blood. After going through three years of public life, Jesus walked the path of death on the cross for all humanity. Even Jesus, who came as the only begotten Son of God, went through the path of shedding blood to have the day of spiritual victory; therefore, we, who have stepped forward to take on the cosmic mission in place of Jesus, must follow the path He walked.

310 The spirit of sacrifice of Jesus who walked the path of the cross. Do you have life left in you? Do you have hope? Do you have a will to move forward? If so, you must understand that these are not solely yours. If you have life, you must not think of it as your own. If Jesus had thought that His life was for Himself, He would not have achieved resurrection beyond the death of the cross. Because He knew His life belonged to God the Father, Jesus endured the suffering and trials of being nailed to the cross. Therefore, that path of the cross was never for Jesus alone. For you too, your life is not your own, and this world is not humanity's, nor is the universe, nor is all creation. All of these belong to God the Father. What thoughts and ideologies do you hold at the center? You must seek the truth and ideology that appeals to the Father. Whether you live or die, you must do so for the Father. If you live with this attitude for heaven, then even if you die, it is not truly death. However, if you live for yourself, even if you live, it cannot be a glorious life. We must each judge why we must walk this path, which we inevitably have to cross, the path of death. Jesus walked the path of tears and sweat, and in the end, He offered even His own body to heaven. For heaven, He did not acknowledge Himself but offered everything, praying, "Father, receive my spirit." The reason He became a sacrificial offering of blood is that He knew that when He fully devoted Himself, God could fully accept Him. If you are to overcome Satan and achieve victory, you must reflect on whether you are clinging to your own life when offering it to heaven. If we are to become the most sacred offerings that must fulfill the Father's wishes eternally, any element centered on me will make us offerings that Satan can accuse. Do you wish to be one whom God can call, "My son, my daughter!"? If you desire that, you must establish the truth of heaven, the life of heaven, and the love of heaven, and you must seek to establish all things and yourself as belonging to heaven. Jesus prayed, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me." However, in contrast, He also prayed, "Yet not as I will, but as you will." In this way, you too must conclude your own will into the Father's will and build the altar of heaven. Those who cannot do so cannot fulfill God's hopes and cannot achieve victory in the battle against Satan. Because humanity has fallen, we have walked the path of laboring with sweat for thousands of years, traversing the hill of tears and the path of death to become living sacrifices before God. Likewise, we today must walk the path of becoming offerings for our nation. If we do so, those who follow you will also walk that path, and even the enemy Satan can be subdued and turned into a friend. Humanity, which has labored for 6,000 years for God's will, must now be equipped with victorious glory to sing God's glory in place of Christ's cosmic responsibility. Until today, Satan, who has opposed God, will oppose you as well. However, the day when this opposition of Satan turns around and Satan offers himself as an offering before God alongside you will be the end time, the day of great judgment. When we establish the conditions under which Satan can submit to God, namely, the conditions that center on the providence of heaven, and command Satan, he will comply with that command. Therefore, you must become victors in the battle against Satan in the heavenly realm.

311 The way to establish an eternal father-son relationship with God. When we appear before heaven as victors, we can finally live as the eternal and unchanging true form centered on God, in a garden where God's eternal will is fulfilled, without any connection to Satan. Because Satan knows that this final battle is beginning, he will exert all his strength to invade. Therefore, to achieve victory in that battle, God must exert His intellect, and you, as God's sons and daughters, must also give your all. In this battle, Satan will not blindly submit to you; rather, you must understand that he will resist with all his might alongside those who are under Satan's dominion. Just as we shed tears for heaven, Satan sheds tears for his own will, and just as we sweat for heaven, Satan sweats for himself, and just as we fight with the resolve to face death, Satan also fights with the resolve to face death for himself. You must understand this. In this confrontation between the two forces, we cannot win if we live for ourselves. We must live thoroughly for the Father, nullifying our own will and striving to establish the Father's value by offering everything before Him. This is the way to victory in the battle against Satan and to establish an eternal father-son relationship with God. You have now found the way to overcome Satan and establish a relationship with God. Therefore, from now on, you must live a life of greater sacrifice for the Father.
