21) Those Who Will Remain Before God's Will
Matthew 15:7-18
What God has been laboring and providentially working for until now has been solely to fulfill His will. However, where did He place the focal point of that will? He placed it in the relationship where humans and God can share joy and sorrow together. When we humans fulfill the will that God desires and establish a relationship where we can eternally share joy and sorrow with Him, God becomes the true Father of humanity, and humanity becomes the true children of God. When this happens, God's will becomes humanity's will, and humans will harmonize with all creation, eternally praising God's wisdom, kindness, and grace while giving glory to Him. All of heaven, humanity, and creation hope for that day to come. The will is God's ideal of creation, and it is also the eternal ideal for fallen humanity. Therefore, when that will is fulfilled, God and humanity become one, and when God is joyful, humanity is joyful, and when humanity is joyful, God is joyful. In other words, by making God's will humanity's will, they can harmonize as one, allowing humanity to return eternal joy to God and also feel eternal happiness through that. To establish this will, God will seek one person who can completely communicate and become one with Him. And through that person, He will manifest His will. 

316   Therefore, if there is a person who can completely align with God's will and realize it, that person will possess God's wisdom and kind nature and can manifest it to all creation. If there is someone who resembles the eternal and absolute God and can manifest God's wisdom, love, and character in every place they stay, then God's will will be fulfilled through them, and God will look upon them with eternal joy. In this ideology, heaven has been carrying out the providence of restoration, and the history of restoration has flowed. If humanity cannot understand this ideology and circumstances of God, they cannot establish any relationship with God. Humanity, having fallen, possesses an ideology centered around themselves that is unrelated to God. Just as God's ideology comes from God, humanity's ideology comes from human wisdom. Therefore, if the ideology of humanity that has governed human history does not meet with God's ideology at any point, humanity cannot encounter the eternal ideal world. Religion aims to reconcile these two ideologies. If you do not realize this, you will not be able to escape the realm of human ethics. The moral and doctrines that have passed through human history must be attributed to the heavenly ideology. It is the responsibility of religion, especially Christianity, to connect these two ideologies. Therefore, if Christianity cannot align these ethical ideologies with the heavenly ones, it cannot achieve the eternal ideal of creation centered around Christianity. If you do not possess the unchanging ideal of creation that can enjoy eternity with God, you will become a traitor to heaven at some point. Thus, you must practice and realize this heavenly ideal of creation in your daily life so that the heavenly ideology can be actualized and embodied. God has been working for this will for 6,000 years. Therefore, if you cannot fulfill this will, God's providence will come to nothing, and His will will remain merely an ideology.

317   The one who came to fulfill this eternal and unchanging ideology is Jesus Christ. He came to this earth as the truth that represents God's wisdom, as the cosmic mercy that represents God's love, and as the tolerance that represents God's kindness, paving the way for God's will. Jesus came to establish the heavenly ideology on this earth. Thus, Jesus appeared with purity and nobility to embody God's ideology in human life. However, there was not a single person who recognized the personality of Jesus, who came to this earth with purity and nobility, representing God's nature. Moreover, Jesus came with a heart of harmony to manifest the heavenly character. This heart of harmony could resonate with good people as well as evil ones, but due to human disbelief, harmony did not occur on this earth. And although Jesus appeared with an unchanging commitment to God's will, the people of that time did not understand or follow His heart. Therefore, we, the later generations, must embody the heavenly purity, nobility, harmony, and commitment to God that Jesus possessed in order to fulfill the heavenly ideology that Jesus desired and strived for on this earth. If we do not live out this life, we cannot resolve the grievances that are bound to Jesus. If humanity does not escape from all human ethics and establish the heavenly ideology as a standard of living, they will not possess the ideology of God and Jesus. Furthermore, the ideal world of creation that God desires and Jesus hopes for will not be realized on this earth. 

318   So what must you do? You must become someone who can replace all human ideologies with heavenly ideologies and completely digest the human into the heavenly. Otherwise, you cannot live a life in the heavenly kingdom on earth. Jesus and the Holy Spirit have worked spiritually for 2,000 years to connect human will with heavenly will. If you believe in such a Jesus, you must inherit that will and fulfill the mission of aligning human will with heavenly will. To inherit this mission, you must first be able to overcome all conditions of evil in your life. To do this, you must possess the life ideology of Jesus. Believing in the cross was to spiritually sever ties with Satan, but now you must possess the life ideology of Jesus and, based on that, sever ties with Satan both spiritually and physically. The day of judgment is approaching. How will judgment be conducted? It will be based on how much heavenly ideology humanity has established on earth. To avoid this judgment, you must become someone who can take responsibility for the will that God desires and fulfill it before fearing God's judgment. If you cannot do this, Satan will take you before you even receive God's judgment. Is there anyone on this earth who possesses God's character? Is there anyone in this world who possesses Jesus' pure character? Make him your friend. Who is noble? Follow him. And who possesses God's character and can resonate? Follow and honor him. Then you will surely find the path of life. Moreover, on the condition that you follow and honor that person, you will avoid judgment. Have you ever possessed the purity, nobility, and harmony of Jesus? If you have not, fight against yourself. Satan is not far away; it is within you. Therefore, discover the differences between the heavenly character within you and the satanic character, and live a life of discernment. 

319   Next, you must appear in an unchanging form. The fact that Jesus did not change means that He remained unchanging concerning the heavenly ideology. Fallen humans under the dominion of Satan are cunning beings. The Satan of the Garden of Eden revealed his sins, but at the time of the final judgment, Satan will not reveal his sins. You must become someone who can stand before Jesus with an unchanging heart, completely letting go of any lingering attachments to your environment and life to unite with Jesus' unchanging heart. Know that everything, including yourself, is the opponent you must fight against. Before the unchanging Jesus, everything was an opponent, and all was an enemy. Moreover, even the spiritual realm attacked Jesus. The entire heaven and earth were opponents before Jesus, so how pitiful He must have been! We must understand that even in such circumstances, He was able to stand with an unchanging form. Now, you must stand before God with an unchanging form and be able to boast of your unchanging form against Satan. Such people must gather to create a foundation that manifests God's wisdom on earth, so that all creation may welcome them. When this happens, humanity will be able to sing of joy and glory, welcoming a day of hope, in contrast to the past when they faced Satan in unhappiness and suffering. They will be able to sing of God's glory. *

22) Finding the Nature of Good to Avoid the Consequences of Sin
All creation was originally created good, but due to the fall of Adam and Eve, it has been unable to manifest the value of goodness and has not escaped the consequences of sin while pursuing goodness. You are well aware that in the original garden created by God, only goodness should exist, and since this goodness has not yet manifested on this earth, God and all creation have been groaning until now. Therefore, fallen humanity must fulfill the ideology of goodness through any historical process of suffering. Humanity must achieve this purpose not only as individuals but also extend it to nations, the world, and all of creation. Thus, we must restore the time when we can reveal the will of goodness in heaven and earth. However, you are the ones who must fulfill this absolute will of goodness and achieve the universal purpose, and you are in such a destiny. We, who admire the original goodness, must first recognize the reality of God, who is the embodiment of goodness, and we must also understand God's good value and spread His words. Thus, through good words, you must find and manifest the good value of all creation that God has created. Otherwise, you must understand that the original purpose of goodness that God created cannot be fulfilled. Before the fall, humanity possessed God's absolute goodness, and God allowed humanity to relate to all creation that was created good. God created the created world through absolute and good words, and among them, humanity was created as a being of total value. Therefore, humanity must manifest as a central figure who can sing of God's goodness, which was the original purpose of creation. However, humanity lost this value due to the fall. How can fallen humanity return to the good God? First, they must resemble the original goodness through their conscience. Next, they must act according to God's words and manifest the value of God's goodness and words. When this happens, God will find the joy of the ideal of goodness that He had when creating all creation, and humans who have pursued the purpose of goodness will also become the reality of goodness that feels God's value of goodness. However, all of this has been completely frustrated due to humanity's fall. Now, you must realize that you are the descendants of fallen Adam and Eve and become the ancestors of goodness who have achieved the purpose of goodness. If you do not fulfill the purpose of goodness, the sins inherited from Adam and Eve will not only remain with you but will also extend to the entire created world and even to heaven through each individual. You must establish yourself correctly and feel the good value of all creation that God created with His words, praising all things as good. You must also be able to relatively manifest the absolute value of God's goodness, who is the source of goodness, through your conscience. If you cannot do this, you will not be able to achieve the ultimate purpose that God desires, nor will you find the goodness you seek.
322   Let us find the nature of goodness and escape the retribution of sin. This inherent goodness must manifest through the essence centered on God's eternal, unique, and unchanging nature. However, due to the fall of humanity, the goodness that should have been expressed relatively by humans, who are meant to reflect the eternal, unchanging, and unique value of God, has not been realized. Consequently, humans have lost the autonomy, dignity, and value necessary to establish goodness as a guiding principle in their lives. The ultimate goal that fallen humanity seeks is God's autonomy, dignity, and value. Without achieving this, we cannot establish a relationship with God's eternal, unchanging, and unique goodness. If our ancestral humans, Adam and Eve, had lived and died to establish these three principles, this hope would not have remained with us today. Had this been the case, humanity would have enjoyed the autonomy, dignity, and value of goodness while living joyfully in an eternal garden centered on God's infinite goodness. However, due to the mistakes of Adam and Eve, this has remained a hope that each individual must seek even to this day. In other words, if Adam and Eve had been able to possess the autonomy, dignity, and value of goodness relative to the absolute essence of goodness, humanity today would not be living in fear, sorrow, and despair. Adam and Eve were in a position of creation, representing God, and were responsible for the whole; thus, their sin did not only affect themselves but also had a fearful impact on the entire created world. We understand that Adam and Eve should have established God's absolute goodness relatively on this earth. However, they did not realize that their transgressions would affect not only themselves but also their future descendants, ultimately causing sorrow to God as well. If Adam and Eve had resolved to follow God's eternal, unchanging, and unique word, such historical, temporal, and future sins would not have existed. However, because they did not follow God's absolute word, the historical, temporal, and future sins manifested from the moment of their fall. When Adam and Eve were tempted by Satan, they had a heart willing to conform to God's word, yet their bodies were drawn to Satan's temptation. Because the power of the body was strong, they transgressed God's will. At that time, the stronger the power of their conscience aimed at absolute goodness, the greater the fear they felt. This fear foreshadowed that their act of falling would become the origin of sin throughout history and eternity. However, they were unaware of this. When Adam and Eve felt fear before their fall, they should have been stimulated by that fear to hold onto absolute goodness and establish an immutable center of righteousness to suppress the evil within them. Instead, they ended up colluding with the essence of evil. This sorrowful reality does not only affect them but has also extended to you, who have inherited the bloodline of the fall. Therefore, you must not forget that you cannot avoid fighting against the essence of evil through your conscience in your daily lives. Remember that one sin has historically confronted human conscience even into the future, and we must break free from the realm of the fall. Although humans are descendants of the fallen Adam and Eve, they possess a conscience that fights against fear, following the subject of absolute goodness; hence, there has never been a person in any era who has not fought against sin. By choosing the path of fear, Adam and Eve brought about sorrow and despair, ultimately leading them to a state of hopelessness. Standing in such a position of fear, the eternal God, the source of life and love who had been with them until then, departed from them, leading them to feel an indescribable sorrow. They came to feel the heart of wanting to find the nature of goodness and escape the retribution of sin. Thus, the garden of Eden, which was created as a garden of ideals, goodness, and pleasure, became a garden with which Adam and Eve had no connection, and they fell into a position of despair in the world of darkness. As humans who have gone through the history of sin, we must seek the purpose of life and rise to the standard of absolute goodness throughout our lives. You must understand that Jesus Christ is the one who pioneered this path. You must rely on the words established by God and the leaders appointed by God to strive toward absolute goodness. You should establish a conscience that your heart can rely on and the words of God that your conscience can rely on, and establish a reality that can represent God's will, connecting yourself to those words and that reality to restore the purpose of absolute goodness. Only then can you enter into God's eternal, unchanging, and unique realm of goodness and manifest the autonomy, dignity, and value of your true nature, fulfilling God's hope that He has had for 6,000 years. Humans are destined to restore absolute goodness, and thus, the ethics and morals established by humans do not aim for anything other than goodness. Furthermore, God has given words to humans to practice, so that they may find the absolute standard of historical goodness in the process of living and achieve the purpose of goodness. Therefore, you must represent the history of fighting with God's word for 6,000 years since Adam by practicing the words of historical goodness. This is the final task given to us. You must not stand in the same position as Adam and Eve, who left behind the resentment of the fall while dealing with the universal words of goodness in a personal manner in the garden of Eden, but instead, you must hold onto the eternal words of God's goodness and manifest them in an eternal and unchanging form. Otherwise, you cannot escape the historical sins that betrayed the word and violated the will. 325 Adam and Eve, due to their fall, came to possess a heart of fear, felt sorrow, and experienced despair, and this has historically continued, leading the end-time humanity to walk this path as well. In the world, there are those who aim for goodness and those who aim for evil. It goes without saying that those who aim for evil do not experience satisfaction and peace, and even those who aim for goodness do not always enjoy satisfaction and peace; they too encounter unknown fears at times and groan under them. Even those who aim for goodness cannot manifest eternal goodness and ideals by themselves. This is because humanity is in the process of restoration. In the end times, where global fear, sorrow, and despair manifest due to the fall, the most important thing we must do is to strive to emulate the character and life of Jesus Christ, who fought with all His might against infinite fear, sorrow, and despair, and established the realm of victory and resurrection. We must understand that He forgot Himself and fought until the moment of victory over infinite fear, sorrow, and despair on this earth. Every human has the nature to establish themselves and manifest their value to the whole. This nature, which seeks to express value through oneself, is good. Originally, humans were meant to express the value of this nature one hundred percent, but due to the fall, they lost that value. Jesus Christ, despite having the value to represent the dignity of the whole by asserting Himself, fought against sin with an unchanging conviction even when He was violated and disregarded in a pitiful position. He also gave up all hope for Himself to establish the hope of the whole. With the assurance that the hope He leaves for the whole will surely be fulfilled even a thousand or two thousand years later, He confronted all sorrow, despair, and fear with an immutable form to establish the essence of goodness. Jesus, without caring for Himself, endured for the purpose of goodness aimed at by heaven, bearing the sacrifices of the present for the hope of the future, forgetting the toil of reality, and possessing the conviction to overcome the fears of reality and transform them into future authority. You too must resemble the character of Jesus and emulate His heart, enduring and overcoming even if your individual self is disregarded and violated in reality, so that you can break free from the realm of the fall. Now, to forget all the affairs of the world and overcome all suffering, you must establish hope amidst despair, joy amidst sorrow, and authority amidst fear. This is the mission you must undertake. You must never accept the invasions of Satan that Jesus Christ faced. You must possess the joy, hope, and authority of heaven that can eliminate the invasions of Satan and be able to manifest the goodness of heaven. Thus, you must manifest the relative value of absolute goodness on this earth, qualifying yourself to express the autonomy that has been lost as the protagonists of all creation. On that day, even God will not be able to act freely with you. When our fallen nature returns to its original nature, we will be able to dwell with God and become qualified to represent Him. After that, when you appear before all things, all creation will silently bow their heads before your dignity, just as they have long awaited the day of victory and glory before God. You must also express the value of goodness. Even if you do not claim or prove that you are good, others should admire your value of goodness and follow you to establish an eternal relationship with you. You must become a reality that can represent eternal hope, eternal joy, eternal authority, and goodness so that God can finally rest. Only such a person can escape the historical providence that deserves the retribution of sin. Otherwise, you will realize that you will receive the retribution of sin and leave behind a grudge for eternity if you do not move with a new determination and resolution. 327 Do you have the words that can express your new autonomy, dignity, and value? Have you seen and felt the essence of goodness? If so, you must uphold your dignity. Do not lose the heavenly autonomy that God has protected. Do you believe that the words held by the Unification Church can introduce eternal goodness as the truth? Do you believe that you can meet God through these words? If so, from now on, do not lose your autonomy, dignity, and value wherever you go on behalf of heaven. Satan will always target your autonomy. He will aim for your dignity. And he will seek your value. Regardless of the environment you find yourself in, you must realize that when you move forward without losing this authority and dignity, the eternal God, who is the essence of goodness, will grant you the authority to judge the world of Satan. * 23) Let us cross over the peak of the fall and enter the original garden. Genesis 1:28, 3:6-24. From Genesis 1:28 and the last verses of chapter 3, we can see that God first blessed humanity and then, due to the fall of humanity, became a God of judgment. This passage records the events from just before the fall of Adam and Eve to their expulsion from the garden of Eden after receiving God's curse. Although this event occurred with Adam and Eve, because they were the ancestors of humanity and the rulers of all creation, the curse of judgment did not only fall upon them but also affected all beings in the created world. Due to the fall of humanity, God's joy turned into sorrow, human hope turned into despair, and heaven and earth became filled with sorrow and resentment. You must not forget that the heart of Adam and Eve, who fell into death, has clearly been passed down to us. When Adam received God's blessing in front of all creation, his heart was filled with joy, but when he lost everything after the fall and was expelled from the Creator God, his heart was in stark contrast to that joy. Thus, Adam and Eve could not stand before all creation and could not find a center in any direction, whether above or below, or to the left or right. We must remember that we, who are faced with the end times, are destined to escape from such a historically tragic connection. The sins committed by Adam have continued to us through the ages, transcending time and nations or ethnicities, taking on a lawful form. Therefore, your individual self must manifest the will of heaven with a universal value, and that value must be the same as the value of heaven. This value must be established in the universe despite any historical difficulties. Otherwise, it is natural that the ideals of humanity and the original garden created by God cannot be manifested through me. The sorrow of the garden of Eden is not limited to the sorrow of the garden itself; the sorrow and despair of God toward fallen Adam and Eve have continued to the countless beings of today, and you must realize this. Therefore, the most important issue is myself. You may think that you are a being limited to a particular family or tribe, but you are not limited to just that. I am in a position similar to a scale, weighing the ideals of hope. The hope that God has for me is cosmic and historical. When that hope of God is fulfilled, all humanity will want to relate to me. Considering this amazing fact, I must establish myself to fulfill their hopes and also manifest the beauty of my true nature before God alongside them. However, the significant issue is where to find such value. What must we do to find this? You must carefully examine the position of Adam and Eve just before their fall and just after their fall. And you must understand that God's hope is to personally call Adam and Eve, "My sons and daughters!"
330   Let us cross the peak of the fall and enter the original garden. Then, what is the fall? The fall is what has separated the inseparable relationship between God and man. Adam and Eve, created by God, were meant to call God "Father" from the very beginning, but the fact that they ended up calling Satan "Father" became the source of historical sorrow. Thus, Adam and Eve's betrayal of God, through their disbelief, became the seed of cosmic resentment (恨). So, what will happen at the end of days? At the end of days, the relationship between God and man will be disrupted. Because of the lineage of disbelief that betrayed God, the descendants of humanity will also rise against their parents at the end of days. When such a time comes, you must find the true parents on this earth, whom you cannot betray even if you wanted to. The current environment you are in is not established by a bond of faith, which is why phenomena of disbelief are occurring. The relationship between God and man is like this, the relationship between husband and wife is like this, and even the relationships among relatives have become trends of disbelief, fundamentally destroying the will that humanity strives for. When such rejection phenomena appear here and there, you must realize that it is the end of days. Even if we witness such phenomena in the reality we live in, we must never stand in such a position. Adam and Eve fell by not keeping God's word and listening to Satan's words; thus, while God's word exists, there also came the unexpected words of Satan. Today, on this earth, there are two streams of words: one belongs to the truth, and the other belongs to falsehood, directly affecting your lives at any time. So, what should we do in such a situation? We must keep the words that come from the God we believe in, the true Father we desire, and establish those words as the standard of our lives, the standard of our ideals, and the standard of our struggles. If we fail to do so, we will not receive the blessing to govern all things on the earth. Today, there are many people who have lost their center. There are words centered on individual ideologies based on certain doctrines or systems, but the groups that take God's word as their eternal standard and fight for it with their lives are gradually disappearing. The phenomenon of those who speak centered on themselves, like Satan, is increasing. In the Garden of Eden, the being that tempted Adam and Eve is referred to as the serpent, which symbolizes one who speaks two words with one tongue. Therefore, those who bear the words that represent the heavenly principle must stand firm in their position and protect those words. You must not stand in a position that is neither this nor that, neither left nor right. A position that is neither this nor that often causes more confusion than a position that creates chaos on either side. Adam and Eve lost their bodies, lost their faith, lost the word, and simultaneously lost their substance. However, we have regained faith and the word, and what remains is only to restore the substance, and the time to restore this substance is what we call the "day of hope." Therefore, to reach the restored standard of substance, there is a peak we must cross, and the question is whether you have become the substance in which God can dwell and operate. God commanded Adam from a relative position and treated him based on the conditions of faith from that relative position, but in the future, He will seek to find the substance. Thus, it is essential to find our one substance through the unity of my heart and body, rather than from a relative position. To find this substance, we must go through the laws of creation.

332   Let us cross the peak of the fall and enter the original garden. Originally, humans were meant to have their hearts united with God, their hearts and bodies united, and everything that is relative to their bodies must establish a relationship. This is the standard of true reciprocity. Since humans are born as such, they must complete their lives through the standard of true reciprocity; therefore, we must seek the ideals that our hearts aspire to, find the point of unity where our bodies follow the commands of our hearts, and leave behind a purpose that both body and heart aspire to on this earth. Those of you in the process of restoration must now unite your previously contradictory hearts and bodies. Thus, if you are in the position of Adam and Eve before the fall, where you were one with God's word, then my heart can become one with my body, and my body can become one with my heart. When you stand in this position, you can pioneer a living environment that is one with all things. So, what mission do you have at the end of days? You have the responsibility to prepare and practice the historical, heavenly value that can replace the cosmic value of restoration. Depending on how you fulfill this responsibility, it will be determined whether you are granted relative authority on this earth, and according to the extent of that granted authority, it will be determined whether a heavenly personality is formed or not. You must understand this. That is why the providence of restoration starts from the tabernacle, passes through the temple, and reaches the substance. Jesus Christ came as such a person of character, and through him, God has carried out the providential history, and today we are walking the path of faith following Christ. Thus, when humanity resembles Christ, the history of sin will be overturned. We are now moving toward the final battleground of judgment. Think of yourself as one who is responsible for the providence of restoration and stand before the universe. If there are a thousand things, do you have the qualifications to be the owner of a thousand things? If there are ten thousand things, do you have the qualifications to be the owner of ten thousand things? 

333 What is the hope of all things? It is nothing other than to welcome the day of glory that moves toward God through humanity. To become a substantial object in which God can dwell, you must feel the responsibility that you must do this work, regardless of where you go or what environment you stay in. Are you living with such a sense of responsibility? “This is my work, and that is my work! There is nothing that is unrelated to me! Father, if I cannot accomplish this work while I am alive, let me do it even after I die!” You must live with the heart that takes responsibility for anything. You must understand that all things want to relate to you and live with you and enjoy life. Furthermore, you have the responsibility to fight with hostility against Satan, who has caused sorrow until now, as he accuses humanity before God. You must be able to say, “Father! Beloved Father, I will fight in your place. I will repay your enemies. I will find what you have lost. Please use us according to your will to find your ideals.” If you do not become a being who can say this, you cannot fulfill God's purpose of restoring the substantial temple. Therefore, you must always be a person who is worthy of the heavenly principle in the living environment you are in to establish the kingdom of heaven. You must bring about a revolution in yourself through a life of separation that distinguishes good from evil, embody the victorious appearance of a heavenly soldier as an eternal and unchanging projection, and be able to take pride in being the sons and daughters of God the Father. Only then can you realize that you can cross the peak of judgment at the end of days and enter the ideal garden of restored Eden to be completed as the embodiment of truth. 

24) Jesus' Design for God  
Matthew 7:1-27 <Prayer> Children who have fought while looking at the hope of the Father according to the will granted for a week kneel and prostrate themselves before the altar of the Father at this time. Merciful Father, loving Father, compassionate Father, please take charge and oversee us. Our hearts are in an indescribably anxious position. We know that without the grace of harmony and the comfort of heaven in our hearts, there is no one as pitiful as we are; therefore, please consider us and grant us the grace of compassion. We know that it is also you, Father, who works to be a friend to the weak, so please strengthen the hearts of the weak and comfort the hearts of the lonely. Allow us to deeply engrave the amazing will of the heavenly principle in our hearts and to be able to offer thanks and worship as we are immersed in the gifts of heaven, and let this time be one where we can manifest the glory you desire and offer songs of joy. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Father, even if we are in a place of hardship, if we stand in place of this sleeping nation, we know that it must become a glory of your joy, and if our sorrow, despair, and sighs are centered not on ourselves but for all things and the universe, then we know that there is nothing more glorious than that. 

335 We know that only a heart that can worry for heaven and worry for the earth can fully work in us at this time, and we earnestly hope and wish for this time to be one where we cannot help but feel the mission entrusted to us from heaven. Now, please allow us to realize that we are standing before the heavenly will, and let us have the conscious heart that what we do is done in place of heaven, and allow us to fight against Satan in place of our nation and fulfill the responsibilities you have entrusted to us, and lead us to be sons and daughters who can receive and bear the blessings you have granted on behalf of our nation. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Thus, please allow us to awaken this sleeping nation and lead us to be sons and daughters who can appeal before you to save all of humanity that is being swallowed by darkness. Help us not to stand in a position where we only take responsibility for our individual lives, but let us be able to stand as responsible beings who can offer our lives before you and stand as representatives for our nation and humanity, as you desire. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Now, please allow us to dedicate all our body and heart's loyalty before you during this one hour, and may that loyalty deeply touch your heart so that you can comfort and bless us during this time. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. In every place where we are scattered in the region, raising the beacon of battle before you in loneliness, Father, please be with us, oversee us, and protect us. Lead us to be able to testify that we are the living sons and daughters of the Father and to be able to boast even in adversity, beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. I know that there are sons and daughters who are in lonely circumstances at this time, so please oversee their environments and all their circumstances, comfort them, and reveal yourself to them with a uniform grace. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. We entrust everything to you, and we earnestly ask that only the will you have granted and the glory you have granted may fully manifest and work in our bodies and minds. 

336   For God’s Design for Jesus, I earnestly ask that you fully manifest and work in us. <Message> At this time, I would like to share with you a brief message titled "The Deep Affection of Jesus for God." The Original Path of Humanity Today, countless humans live their lives without clearly knowing the fundamental purpose of life. In other words, they do not accurately understand the fundamental questions of life: why humans are born on this earth, how they should live, and where they go after death. However, it is simple. Humans exist for the sake of others. In other words, they are born for others, live for others, and die for others; this is the original path of humanity. However, our human ancestors, Adam and Eve, were supposed to walk this original path of humanity, that is, they were supposed to live for each other, but they could not take that path. This is the root of the fall. Therefore, until now, humans have been striving to indemnify the root of that fall. However, because they have not escaped the lineage of the fall, even though they tried to live for others, ultimately, it was only a life centered on themselves. In other words, they were born for themselves, lived for themselves, and died for themselves. Nevertheless, God has established the cosmic value of life through the historical process, even if humans do not know it, to realize the ideal of creation. You must reflect on this once again. Thus, you must find the value that can replace the heavenly relationships, the human relationships, and the cosmic relationships by upholding the human integrity regarding the heavenly principle. Furthermore, you must restore your position that can eternally remain unchanged regarding God's will and become one who can sing the value of the one who lives eternally for the sake of others, and you yourself must establish a connection with the whole, so that the practical manifestation of that connection can fully reveal the beauty of God's creation. This is God's highest goal in guiding humanity to seek the value of their own lives. Therefore, you must establish that cosmic integrity of humanity and find a day when you can boast before God, before all humanity, and before all creation. You are placed on a cosmic path of fate that you must restore that day, even if it means dying. You must keep this in mind. 

337 Establishing this unchanging standard of integrity, whether before heaven, humanity, or all created beings, you must be a person who can solely manifest that value and glory. There has never been a true person of character who cannot change, cannot violate, and cannot turn back. Throughout history, there have been many prophets and sages sent by heaven, but there has never been a true person of character like this. Thus, humanity has been searching for this one character throughout long history. Today, humans must meet the one who has sworn and resolved to stand before the heavenly principle and human principle with an unchanging appearance, inheriting the missions and faith of all the prophets and sages who have come before. Otherwise, they will not be able to fulfill the responsibilities that God desires, and human history will not be able to approach the one destination that the heavenly principle desires. In this way, the one character who can replace heaven and all created beings with the eternal standard of integrity must appear. If such a character does not appear before humanity, the will of the heavenly principle cannot be fulfilled, and this evil world cannot be restored. You must realize that this is the principle of the heavenly principle. Therefore, that central being must surely appear on this earth. Otherwise, the one who said he would appear at the end of history cannot manifest on this earth, and the ideal world centered on God cannot be realized. That central being must manifest the value and glory of all creation within his sphere of life.
338   Jesus must become the core agent of my essential power for God. God, who has been providentially working to save humanity, has sent such central figures to this earth throughout the ages of providential history. If human history had not been passed down through these interconnected historical figures, we would not be able to inherit God's providential will today. The ultimate purpose of history is to find the ideal of the return through a single worldview. Today, people living on this earth universally acknowledge this fact. 

The point of the restoration providence and true religion. So, what is the point of such providential history? It is to establish a standard that can eternally coexist with God, equipped with a personality that can be established forever before the heavenly and human principles, representing the heavenly, human, and cosmic principles with an unchanging attitude of loyalty and filial piety. Since the purpose of human history is directed toward that one point, we can understand how human history is driven by certain ideologies, certain movements, and certain constructive activities. And that one standard is a historical standard, a standard of human nature, and a standard that humanity has historically longed for. Furthermore, humans have also hoped for the central figure who has completed that one standard to appear before them. In other words, they have wished for that central figure to appear in their own time, establishing a relationship with them, so that they too can become beings who have completed the standard of the heavenly principles and can boast before all creation. 

When that one being appears before you, you should be able to regard Him as the central being and emulate His integrity. The question will then be whether you have become such a person. God has sent individuals of loyalty and integrity who could represent the era and take responsibility for it, passing on the heavenly principles that the figures of that time should uphold, but the people of that time did not recognize this. 

On the other hand, human history is moving toward the goal of restoration as many movements are unified into one ideology. What is the reason for this unification of many movements and the reason why the providence of the heavenly principles has been unified from the beginning through the process to the destination? It is because if the goal of providence changes from age to age, it cannot achieve the purpose of the unification of providence. Thus, you must understand that God's providence is consistently advancing toward one standard centered on the eternal axis. 

This is not a movement that appears through any ideology, nor is it a law that appears through ideology, nor is it a morality that appears through ideology. It is the course of God's providence that has fought alone against all historical elements centered on the law of the heavenly principles that transcends human principles. Therefore, we must become the personalities of the heavenly principles who can establish unchanging integrity on behalf of the heavenly will. Thus, you must be able to find the value of unification through the unchanging path of God's providence from the starting point to the destination, representing the value of the whole. Furthermore, the value of that found unification must be established as the condition for the overall restoration. If not, God's will to establish a personality representing the ideology of the heavenly principles will not be fulfilled. 

Looking at the historical process, we can see that religions have formed around nations and regions that are appropriate for them. Among them, there must be a religion with a long historical background that asserts an unchanging personality and can connect the heavenly love and heavenly values. That religion must set an absolute standard for this purpose, regardless of changes in time and environment, and must persist until the end. Furthermore, that religion must present the purpose for which humans were born, the purpose for which they should live, and must have a historical background that can contribute in some aspects of history and culture. 

To find such a religion, you must consider whether that religion has fought infinitely on earth to practice its faith-based ideology and whether it is a religion that has a consistent historical background to manifest God's consistent ideology and love before humanity, even as times and movements change. If such a religion exists, then the fundamental purpose that moves around that religion is to represent the heavenly principles, to represent human principles, and to represent the ideologies of the entire earth. It is also a religion that can establish a relationship with a practical being equipped with unchanging integrity. That religion is Christianity. 

Christianity has developed to this day based on the ideology centered on Jesus, and there has been a life aimed at realizing that ideology, as well as a fervent hope to achieve that ideology. Therefore, the ideology that is being proclaimed in Christianity today must align with the ideology that Jesus initiated, and the practical lives of Christians must match the practical life that Jesus lived, and the desires of Christians must be the same as Jesus' desires. 

Thus, all Christians must represent Jesus' unchanging integrity and be able to inherit the heavenly inheritance He has granted. If you cannot become such saints, then you cannot present the ideology of Christianity, which aims to fulfill the will of Jesus Christ, as an unchanging ideology, as a single movement, or as a practical object before the heavenly principles, which should unify humanity. 

Jesus' life of integrity and loyalty. Now, when we examine the character of Jesus over His 30 years of life, we see that He was not just an individual confined to His time. His character was not only that of His own person but also the character of the heavenly values that represented 4,000 years of history. You must realize this. The ideology that Jesus advocated was both the hope that countless prophets and sages had historically looked forward to and the ideology of the Creator aimed at fulfilling the purpose of providence. It was a life in which Jesus walked the path of blood and tears to fulfill such a mission. 

Therefore, you must emulate His integrity and character through Jesus' ideology and life with an unchanging heart. Just as Jesus fought without caring about infinite struggles to establish the integrity of the heavenly principles on behalf of 4,000 years of history, you too must appear before heaven as a personality equipped with unchanging integrity, inheriting the mission that Jesus left behind, on behalf of the 6,000 years of history added to the 2,000 years. If you cannot become such individuals, you will not be able to establish an eternal relationship with the ideology that represents the heavenly principles, the ideology that Jesus Christ hoped for, and the ideology we are seeking today. You must keep this in mind. 

So how did Jesus live? Jesus made the will of God the purpose of His life and vowed before the heavenly principles to take responsibility for the whole until that will was fulfilled, living a life of integrity without considering His own comfort. 

Then how could God establish Jesus as the Savior of all mankind? Throughout the 4,000 years of history, only Jesus dedicated His entire life to God's will and, for the first time since creation, maintained loyalty and integrity for God's will. Thus, Jesus could be established as the eternal Messiah, and the providential history that had been passed down centered on Moses entered a new stage through Jesus' ideology. 

As we stand before the final judgment, what can bring an end to the infinite fear of Golgotha that we must cross? It will not be achieved with the ideologies present on this earth until now. Therefore, we need a central being that can clear the blocked path before us. Historically, God also knew that it was impossible with the ideologies of the time, so He promised to send central figures of providence through numerous religions that aim for providence. This is what is meant by the Second Coming. You must understand this. 

Now, we must not stand on relative value standards regarding God or creation. We must become those who have a center that represents the absolute personality of God, the absolute unchanging ideology of God, and the ideology of heavenly life, standing in a position where the beginning and end can eternally relate according to God's will, and we must be able to manifest our value before all creation. Furthermore, you must seek the truth that will guide you to become such humans. 

If you are those who have embarked on the quest for such truth, you must inherit the hopes of Jesus, the ideology that Jesus desired, and the standards of Jesus' life, and you must be able to add new ideologies to them. Additionally, you must find such a stage for your activities. Thus, you must find an absolute position that can govern all aspects with ideological and practical standards, becoming the true person that heaven desires to find at the end, representing the entire purpose of the heavenly principles. If you cannot do this, you must at least be someone who can possess a heart capable of repentance. 

Today, we are individuals, but we must not stop at being individuals. The Christianity we believe in must not remain a religion only for nations and states; it must become a religion for the world and humanity. It must also be able to represent humanity's historical hopes and be capable of fulfilling both human and heavenly ideologies. 

You must clearly feel that such history, historical hopes, human ideologies, and heavenly ideologies are connected to the environment in which you live, and you must be able to appear before Jesus, who came 2,000 years ago as the embodiment of hope, without shame, saying, "Lord, is this not your desire? I will fulfill it." And we must recall Jesus, who prayed, "Heaven, receive this," after fulfilling His responsibilities for the heavenly will with unchanging integrity on behalf of the principles of the heavenly principles. 

The heart attitude of Jesus who overcame a lonely environment. So, what kind of heart attitude did Jesus, who came with the historical mission to fulfill God's will, have as He overcame difficult environments? Jesus felt a sense of responsibility to restore human principles, to establish a relationship with the heavenly principles, and to fulfill humanity's historical hopes, harboring a solemn heart that no one could feel. 

What kind of difficult circumstances did Jesus face? Jesus was in a difficult position where He had to fight against the invisible billions of satans invading not only Himself but also the people of His time. Moreover, He was in a difficult position where He had to pioneer the path blocked by the people of that time and the historical habits and trends of the era. 

Who fought against Satan on behalf of Jesus, who was in such a difficult and lonely position? Who had the courage to pioneer that difficult path on His behalf? Today, you must become those who can fight to save the world on behalf of Jesus, who was in such a position, fulfilling the responsibilities of humanity on this earth. If such people do not emerge, the ideals that Jesus hoped for cannot be realized on this earth. 

And the people of that time did not recognize Jesus, who came to save fallen humanity as a being representing the historical personality. Thus, Jesus walked a path of extreme loneliness and solitude. However, He did not have personal hopes. His only hope was to save fallen humanity. Yet, even to this day, people do not recognize Jesus' lonely circumstances and the fact that He, despite His loneliness, dedicated His entire hope to saving humanity. Furthermore, even the disciples who followed Jesus did not understand His circumstances. You must recognize that Jesus was the great king of the sorrowful lonely ones. 

Moreover, Jesus did not pray only for Himself. Everything Jesus said, saw, heard, felt, and did was not for His own sake. They were intended to represent history, humanity, and the heavenly principles, manifesting the eternal and unchanging existential value of God. 

Thus, even while living a sorrowful life with tears shed in silence, you must understand that Jesus was a being with a great purpose. You must repent for not being able to fathom the unfortunate circumstances in which Jesus had to fight against Satan without losing the ideology and belief of the Creator. You must also lament for this. Jesus did not come to this earth to establish an ideology for Himself; He established an ideology for the heavenly principles. His ideology was the unchanging ideology that represented God's inner heart and the fundamental ideology of the numerous movements and thoughts that appeared throughout history. 

So how did Jesus live with such an ideology? What kind of heart did He have to overcome His environment and establish a relationship with heaven? Jesus Himself was the original human who could sing of God's glory centered on God's goodness, a being who could enjoy joy just as Adam and Eve did before the fall, but He was born on this fallen earth and had to suppress that difficult environment on behalf of God. 

Humans have no choice but to live a life of sorrow because they have fallen. Furthermore, because humans have fallen, they must suffer and dwell in the realm of death. Jesus, who came to this earth filled with the resentment of sorrow, pain, and death, was the protagonist who stood on that resentment, establishing the center of the heavenly principles in His heart and fighting to hold onto it. 

Jesus walked the path of sorrow to feel God's sorrow as His own. His lament was not for His own sake but because He had a mission to atone for the sorrows of the historical nation through His own being. Thus, He lamented on behalf of history, on behalf of providence, and on behalf of the nation. 

Jesus' love, loyalty, and patience toward God. No matter how much He was in a place of bleeding, sorrow, and pain, or in a position gripped by fear, His center did not change. If Jesus, who had to take on the overall mission of pioneering an unchanging path on earth by inheriting the heavenly ideology, had changed His center in such an environment, the victorious history of the heavenly principles could not have begun.
345 Jesus overcame all difficulties, the position of lost hope, and the accusations of Satan, paving the victorious path of heavenly principles. To carve out this path, Jesus emphasized a love that had never existed in history. He asserted that no matter what difficult circumstances one might face, one must have patience to overcome those circumstances, and that sinners should be faithful to God's will just as they are loyal to evil. This is the foundation of the nine fruits of the Holy Spirit spoken of in Christianity. When one lives a life of love, joy and peace emerge; through patience, mercy and goodness arise; and a life of faithfulness brings forth gentleness and humility. Jesus emphasized heavenly love, heavenly patience, and heavenly faithfulness to eliminate all elements of evil in fallen humanity. These are practical ideals that can achieve the ideology of heaven, but do you have such love of Christ in your hearts today? Do you also have patience and loyalty? Jesus was the embodiment of love who manifested God's heart, and He was the protagonist of patience who cared for the suffering of all people even on the sorrowful path of Golgotha. He was the representative of loyalty who was more faithful to heaven than anyone in history. 

Then, where did Jesus' love, patience, and loyalty originate? They did not originate from Jesus Himself. Rather, Jesus played the role of mediator connecting God's love to humanity. Jesus, who came to save ignorant humans, was the embodiment of God's love and the essence of divine value. How could Jesus manifest God's love, which had never existed in history? He was able to overcome all those difficulties for God's will and could even give up His own life. Thus, God's love could come upon such a Jesus, and for the first time in history, He could personally represent God's love. When Jesus came to this earth to seek God's love, He did not prioritize logical aspects. Jesus did not speak of definitions or logic of love, but represented the practical aspects of love in history. 

346 Jesus did not speak of what He felt or did not feel, nor what He could not act upon for God's purpose. He understood that one could only establish an eternal relationship with God through practical actions. Then, where did Jesus' practical love come from? It did not come from Jesus Himself. Because He could sense God's inner heart, Jesus was able to establish such inner mental standards. Humans did not understand this well. 

What is God's love? Today, humans on this earth may betray and change a million times, but God cannot do that. God's love is eternal and unchanging. Because humans did not understand the heart of God's love, they have betrayed and distrusted one another. Where did God's patience come from? God has engaged in the history of conflict to fulfill love. He has infinitely endured evil to establish the ideal of a life of goodness. In other words, He has endured for 6,000 years to set an unchanging standard of heavenly law to establish just one human being. God, in order to fulfill this true purpose, sought a person who could represent Himself and the value of the whole, and before humans could be loyal to God, He was first loyal to humanity and has infinitely endured. 

Therefore, you must understand the circumstances in which God, who operates centered on heavenly principles, has been infinitely loyal to humanity to fulfill His will, and you must comprehend God's heart, which has infinitely sacrificed to establish this will, as well as God's heart, which has infinitely transcended Himself to establish future ideals, and God's heart of love, which seeks to give infinitely. 

You must also understand that you cannot stand before God with any of your own claims or ideas. Who was the one worthy of receiving God's love, which He has endured for 4,000 years to give infinite love? That person was only Jesus. Knowing this, even in times of loneliness, Jesus was able to feel that love and give thanks before God. And who was the one who could represent the value of God's patience and show the results of that patience, knowing that God had been grieving for 4,000 years and had been enduring and fighting? It was only Jesus. Thus, bearing the hope of God, who wished to lead humanity through Himself, Jesus had to walk the path of heavenly principles alone, filled with sorrow. You must understand this. 

Saints of the Last Days to Follow Jesus 
Therefore, just as Jesus felt all of God's loyal heart, you too must feel God's loyal heart. Thus, you should not remain in the position of the prodigal son but should be able to represent the overall value of God's heavenly principles established from the beginning through the ideology of creation, and you must realize that the value of the cosmos and historical value can be compared to your own value. You must inherit the love, patience, and loyalty of Jesus, who felt God's love, God's patience, and God's loyalty, and who realized that He was the hope found after 4,000 years of God's hard work and endurance. You must understand the heart of Jesus, who sought such a person. 

And you must recognize that Jesus came to this earth as the representative of heavenly love and the historical representative of heavenly loyalty, meaning that all heavenly battles have been transferred to this earth. Therefore, you must be able to inherit the unfinished mission that Jesus left behind when He came to this earth and could not fulfill all His will. If such a person does not appear, Jesus cannot come again to this earth, nor can He connect with this world. The sorrow of God, who looked upon Jesus in a position where no one believed in Him, was beyond words. Also, Jesus Himself felt unspeakable sorrow, thinking of God's heart, which had worked hard for 4,000 years to find just one person, while He had to cross the path of death. 

348 Knowing that God's sorrow was compounded, Jesus prayed, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39) 

Then how could Jesus, who died on the cross, resurrect? Jesus was able to laugh at the enemies and Satan who mocked His death while maintaining the dignity of being the Son of God, and because He pioneered the cosmic path of the Lord by transcending death, He was able to resurrect. Furthermore, because He inherited patience, love, and loyalty that do not exist in the world of Satan, He accomplished what is unimaginable in the world of Satan, that is, blessing those who killed Him, and thus, Jesus was able to resurrect. By believing in this resurrected Lord, Christians can be reborn. 

Today, you must emulate the heart of Jesus, who, despite knowing the principles of heavenly principles established by God, went forth with the determination that even if He were to die a million times or fail a million times, He would not change. You must also become a resurrected child who inherits the loyalty and patience that Jesus established for us and practices His legacy left on this earth. 

You must establish an unchanging heart relationship with God, whether in joy or sorrow, cultivate God's love together, and become someone who can fight against Satan in place of Jesus. Such a person is indeed the brother of Jesus and the person that God has longed to find for 4,000 years. Furthermore, you, who are in the Last Days, must emulate Jesus' love, patience, and loyalty, and as His representative, not only complete His ideals in a flat manner but also in a three-dimensional manner, and you must be able to win against all historical battles with Satan and subdue Satan. Remember that this is the mission of the saints in the Last Days. *
